   ADMIN_QUERY_DOCUMENTS_FOLDER_ID: '19WkI0rDotx93UCOpfMEzHvET6wzqRI9i',

//  Additional constants for date blocking functionality
 const SHEET_ID = '1M0AdgnK2B71XOMw_I6L7eCV6mY9hv9trfno5PheTFOg';
 const BLOCKED_DATES_SHEET = 'Blocked Dates';
 const AVAILABLE_DATES_SHEET = 'Available Dates';

/**
 * Returns the canonical public web app URL for use in emails and external links.
 * Always uses CONFIG.WEB_APP_URL as the single source of truth.
 * Never uses ScriptApp.getService().getUrl() which returns account-scoped /u/N/ URLs
 * that break for recipients signed into different Google accounts.
 */
function getPublicWebAppUrl() {
  if (!CONFIG.WEB_APP_URL) {
    throw new Error(
      'CONFIG.WEB_APP_URL is not set. ' +
      'Open the script, set WEB_APP_URL to your canonical /macros/s/.../exec URL, and save.'
    );
  }
  // Strip any /u/N/ account prefix and query/hash, return clean base URL.
  return CONFIG.WEB_APP_URL
    .trim()
    .replace(/\/macros\/u\/\d+\/s\//, '/macros/s/')
    .replace(/[?#].*$/, '');
}

/**
 * Run this function inside Google Apps Script editor to verify the URL is correct.
 * Open Apps Script → select verifyWebAppUrl → click Run → check Execution log.
 */
function verifyWebAppUrl() {
  const url = getPublicWebAppUrl();
  Logger.log('=== Web App URL Verification ===');
  Logger.log('Base URL : ' + url);
  Logger.log('Consent  : ' + url + '?appointmentId=TEST-001&giveConsent=true');
  Logger.log('Payment  : ' + url + '?appointmentId=TEST-001&uploadPayment=true');
  Logger.log('Feedback : ' + url + '?appointmentId=TEST-001&submitFeedback=true');
  Logger.log('Proceed  : ' + url + '?appointmentId=TEST-001&response=proceed');
  Logger.log('================================');
  Logger.log('If the Base URL above contains /u/1/ or /u/0/, update CONFIG.WEB_APP_URL.');
}

/**
 * Helper function to get session-specific brochure URL
 */
function getSessionSpecificBrochure(sessionType, serviceCategory) {
  console.log('Getting brochure for sessionType:', sessionType, 'serviceCategory:', serviceCategory);
  
  // For advisory services, use advisory brochure
  if (serviceCategory === 'Advisory' || serviceCategory === 'advisory') {
    return CONFIG.DOCUMENTS.BROCHURES.ADVISORY;
  }
  
  // For consultancy services, use session-specific brochures
  if (serviceCategory === 'Consultancy' || serviceCategory === 'consultancy') {
    switch (sessionType) {
      case 'Generalized':
      case 'generalized':
        return CONFIG.DOCUMENTS.BROCHURES.GENERALIZED;
      
      case 'Specialized (Virtual)':
      case 'specialized':
        return CONFIG.DOCUMENTS.BROCHURES.SPECIALIZED;
      
      case 'Super-Specialized (In-Person)':
      case 'super-specialized':
        return CONFIG.DOCUMENTS.BROCHURES.SUPER_SPECIALIZED;
      
      case 'Long-term Projects':
      case 'long-term-engagement':
        return CONFIG.DOCUMENTS.BROCHURES.LONG_TERM_ENGAGEMENT;
      
      default:
        console.log('Unknown session type, using default brochure');
        return CONFIG.DOCUMENTS.BROCHURES.DEFAULT;
    }
  }
  
  // Fallback to default brochure
  console.log('Unknown service category, using default brochure');
  return CONFIG.DOCUMENTS.BROCHURES.DEFAULT;
}

/**
 * Handle form submissions and admin actions
 */
function doPost(e) {
  try {
    // CRITICAL LOGGING - Log EVERYTHING to diagnose submission issues
    console.log('=== doPost CALLED ===');
    console.log('Timestamp:', new Date().toISOString());
    console.log('e.parameter:', JSON.stringify(e.parameter));
    console.log('e.postData:', e.postData ? JSON.stringify(e.postData) : 'No postData');
    console.log('e.contentLength:', e.contentLength);
    console.log('e.queryString:', e.queryString);
    
    // Handle client query submissions FIRST (before other validations)
    if (e.parameter && e.parameter.action === 'submitClientQuery') {
      console.log('Processing client query submission');
      return handleClientQuery(e.parameter);
    }
    
    // Handle confirmed proceed action (from the confirmation page)
    if (e.parameter && e.parameter.action === 'confirmProceed') {
      console.log('Processing confirmed proceed for appointmentId:', e.parameter.appointmentId);
      try {
        const apptId = e.parameter.appointmentId;
        
        // Check if already responded
        const existingResponse = getClientResponseStatus(apptId);
        if (existingResponse && !existingResponse.includes('Awaiting Response')) {
          return createCORSResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'You have already responded to this appointment.' });
        }
        
        // Get appointment and update status
        const appointment = getAppointmentData(apptId);
        if (!appointment) {
          return createCORSResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Appointment not found.' });
        }
        
        updateClientStatus(apptId, 'Proceed', null);
        
        return createCORSResponse({ status: 'success', message: 'Your response has been recorded. You chose to proceed.' });
      } catch (err) {
        console.error('Error in confirmProceed:', err);
        return createCORSResponse({ status: 'error', message: err.toString() });
      }
    }
    
    // Handle payment proof upload submissions
    if (e.parameter && e.parameter.action === 'uploadPaymentProof') {
      console.log('Processing payment proof upload');
      return handlePaymentProofUpload(e.parameter);
    }
    
    // Handle consent submissions
    if (e.parameter && e.parameter.action === 'giveConsent') {
      console.log('Processing consent submission');
      return handleConsentSubmission(e.parameter);
    }
    
    // Handle feedback submissions
    if (e.parameter && e.parameter.action === 'submitFeedback') {
      console.log('Processing feedback submission');
      return handleFeedbackSubmission(e.parameter);
    }
    
    // Reschedule functionality removed - now handled via booking form redirect
    
    // Handle admin query resolution with document upload
    if (e.parameter && e.parameter.action === 'resolveQueryWithDocument') {
      console.log('Processing admin query resolution with document');
      return handleAdminQueryResolution(e.parameter);
    }
    
    // Handle test refund document upload
    if (e.parameter && e.parameter.action === 'testRefundUpload') {
      console.log('Processing test refund document upload');
      return createCORSResponse(testRefundDocumentUploadAndDelete());
    }
    
    // Handle refund initiation by admin
    if (e.parameter && e.parameter.action === 'initiateRefund') {
      console.log('Processing refund initiation by admin');
      console.log('🔍 Raw parameters received:', e.parameter);
      
      // Parse actionData if it's a JSON string
      let refundParams = { ...e.parameter };
      if (e.parameter.actionData) {
        try {
          console.log('📦 Parsing actionData JSON...');
          const actionData = JSON.parse(e.parameter.actionData);
          console.log('✅ Parsed actionData:', actionData);
          
          // Merge actionData into refundParams
          refundParams = {
            appointmentId: e.parameter.appointmentId,
            refundNotes: actionData.notes,
            refundProofDocument: actionData.refundProofDocument,
            refundProofName: actionData.refundProofName,
            refundProofType: actionData.refundProofType
          };
          console.log('✅ Merged refund parameters:', {
            appointmentId: refundParams.appointmentId,
            hasNotes: !!refundParams.refundNotes,
            hasDocument: !!refundParams.refundProofDocument,
            hasName: !!refundParams.refundProofName,
            hasType: !!refundParams.refundProofType,
            documentLength: refundParams.refundProofDocument ? refundParams.refundProofDocument.length : 0
          });
        } catch (parseError) {
          console.error('❌ Error parsing actionData:', parseError);
        }
      }
      
      return handleRefundInitiation(refundParams);
    }
    
    // Handle refund acknowledgment by client
    if (e.parameter && e.parameter.action === 'acknowledgeRefund') {
      console.log('Processing refund acknowledgment by client');
      return handleRefundAcknowledgment(e.parameter);
    }
    
    // FIRST PRIORITY: Check if this is an admin action or fetch request
    if (e.parameter && e.parameter.action) {
      console.log('Processing admin/fetch request:', e.parameter.action);
      
      // Handle fetching appointments (READ operation - no changes to sheet)
      if (e.parameter.action === 'getAppointments') {
        console.log('Fetching appointments - READ ONLY operation');
        const result = getAppointmentsData(); // Get raw data
        
        // Check if JSONP callback is requested
        if (e.parameter.callback && e.parameter.format === 'jsonp') {
          const jsonpResponse = e.parameter.callback + '(' + JSON.stringify(result) + ')';
          return ContentService.createTextOutput(jsonpResponse)
            .setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JAVASCRIPT);
        }
        
        return ContentService.createTextOutput(JSON.stringify(result))
          .setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON);
      }
      
      // Handle login history requests
      if (e.parameter.action === 'getLoginHistory') {
        console.log('Fetching login history');
        return getLoginHistory();
      }
      
      // Handle logging admin login to spreadsheet
      if (e.parameter.action === 'logAdminLogin') {
        console.log('Logging admin login to spreadsheet');
        const adminUser = e.parameter.adminUser || 'Unknown';
        const ipAddress = e.parameter.ipAddress || 'Unknown';
        const browserInfo = e.parameter.browserInfo || 'Unknown';
        const loginStatus = e.parameter.loginStatus || 'Success';
        
        logAdminLogin(adminUser, ipAddress, browserInfo, loginStatus);
        
        return createCORSResponse({
          status: 'success',
          message: 'Login logged successfully'
        });
      }
      
      // SECURE LOGIN: Validate credentials server-side without exposing passwords
      if (e.parameter.action === 'validateLogin') {
        console.log('Validating admin login credentials');
        const email = e.parameter.email;
        const password = e.parameter.password;
        return validateAdminLogin(email, password);
      }
      
      // Handle user management requests
      if (e.parameter.action === 'getUsersAndRoles') {
        console.log('Fetching users and roles');
        return getUsersAndRoles();
      }
      
      if (e.parameter.action === 'addUser') {
        console.log('Adding new user');
        const userData = {
          name: e.parameter.name,
          email: e.parameter.email,
          password: e.parameter.password,
          role: e.parameter.role
        };
        return addUser(userData);
      }
      
      if (e.parameter.action === 'deleteUser') {
        console.log('Deleting user');
        const userId = e.parameter.userId;
        return deleteUser(userId);
      }
      
      if (e.parameter.action === 'updateUserLastLogin') {
        console.log('Updating user last login');
        const email = e.parameter.email;
        updateUserLastLogin(email);
        return createCORSResponse({
          status: 'success',
          message: 'Last login updated'
        });
      }
      
      if (e.parameter.action === 'changeUserPassword') {
        console.log('Changing user password');
        const userId = e.parameter.userId;
        const newPassword = e.parameter.newPassword;
        const changedByEmail = e.parameter.changedByEmail;
        return changeUserPassword(userId, newPassword, changedByEmail);
      }
      
      // Handle date blocking actions
      if (e.parameter.action === 'blockDates') {
        console.log('Processing block dates request with parameters:', e.parameter);
        return handleBlockDates(e.parameter);
      }
      
      if (e.parameter.action === 'unblockDate') {
        console.log('Processing unblock date request with parameters:', e.parameter);
        return handleUnblockDate(e.parameter);
      }
      
      if (e.parameter.action === 'unblockSpecificDates') {
        console.log('Processing unblock specific dates request with parameters:', e.parameter);
        return handleUnblockSpecificDates(e.parameter);
      }
      
      if (e.parameter.action === 'manualUnblockDate') {
        console.log('Processing manual unblock single date request with parameters:', e.parameter);
        return handleManualUnblockDate(e.parameter);
      }
      
      if (e.parameter.action === 'getBlockedDates') {
        console.log('Fetching blocked dates');
        return getBlockedDates();
      }
      
      // Handle available dates actions
      if (e.parameter.action === 'getAvailableDates') {
        console.log('Fetching available dates');
        return getAvailableDates();
      }
      
      if (e.parameter.action === 'makeMultipleDatesAvailable') {
        console.log('Processing make multiple dates available request with parameters:', e.parameter);
        return handleMakeMultipleDatesAvailable(e.parameter);
      }
      
      if (e.parameter.action === 'makeDateAvailable') {
        console.log('Processing make date available request with parameters:', e.parameter);
        return handleMakeDateAvailable(e.parameter);
      }
      
      if (e.parameter.action === 'removeAvailableDate') {
        console.log('Processing remove available date request with parameters:', e.parameter);
        return handleRemoveAvailableDate(e.parameter);
      }
      
      // Handle client responses (Proceed/Query)
      if (e.parameter.action === 'clientResponse') {
        console.log('Processing client response');
        return handleClientResponse(e.parameter);
      }
      
      // Handle other admin actions (approve, reject, etc.)
      console.log('Processing admin action:', e.parameter.action);
      return handleAdminAction(e.parameter);
    }
    
    // SECOND PRIORITY: Check if this is a JSON request (admin actions)
    if (e.postData && e.postData.contents) {
      try {
        const data = JSON.parse(e.postData.contents);
        if (data.action) {
          console.log('Processing JSON admin action:', data.action);
          return handleAdminAction(data);
        }
      } catch (parseError) {
        console.log('Not JSON data, checking for form submission');
      }
    }
    
    // PRIORITY: Check if this is a RESCHEDULE submission FIRST (before other validations)
    const isRescheduleSubmission = e.parameter && 
                                    e.parameter['reschedule-mode'] === 'true' && 
                                    e.parameter['original-session-id'];
    
    if (isRescheduleSubmission) {
      console.log('=== RESCHEDULE SUBMISSION DETECTED ===');
      console.log('Reschedule mode:', e.parameter['reschedule-mode']);
      console.log('Original Session ID:', e.parameter['original-session-id']);
      console.log('Bypassing standard form validation for reschedule');
      return handleFormSubmission(e.parameter);
    }
    
    // THIRD PRIORITY: Check if this is a valid NEW form submission
    const requiredFormFields = ['name', 'email', 'country-code', 'phone', 'organization'];
    const hasAllFormFields = requiredFormFields.every(field => 
      e.parameter && e.parameter[field] && e.parameter[field].trim() !== ''
    );
    
    console.log('Form validation check:');
    console.log('- Has all required fields:', hasAllFormFields);
    console.log('- Required fields status:');
    requiredFormFields.forEach(field => {
      console.log(`  ${field}: ${e.parameter[field] ? 'PRESENT' : 'MISSING'}`);
    });
    
    // More flexible date/time field check - look for ANY date/time related field
    const hasDateTimeField = e.parameter['selected-slot'] || 
                             e.parameter['selected-date'] || 
                             e.parameter['selected-time'] ||
                             e.parameter['advisory-datetime'] ||
                             e.parameter['advisory-selected-datetime'] ||
                             e.parameter['advisory-selected-date'] ||
                             e.parameter['advisory-selected-time'] ||
                             e.parameter['selected-time-slot--in-case-of-consultancyist'];
    
    console.log('- Has date/time field:', hasDateTimeField);
    
    const isNotAdminRequest = !e.parameter.action && !e.parameter.fetchOnly && !e.parameter.adminRequest;
    console.log('- Is not admin request:', isNotAdminRequest);
    
    if (hasAllFormFields && isNotAdminRequest) {
      console.log('Processing NEW form submission (date/time validation relaxed)');
      return handleFormSubmission(e.parameter);
    }
    
    // Return error for invalid requests
    console.log('Form validation FAILED - returning error');
    return createCORSResponse({ 
      status: 'error', 
      message: `Invalid request. Missing required fields or invalid format. Required: ${requiredFormFields.join(', ')}` 
    });
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error in doPost:', error);
    return createCORSResponse({ 
      status: 'error', 
      message: error.toString() 
    });
  }
}

/**
 * Generate a unique session ID in format GIS-YYYY-XXX
 * GIS = Global Intelligence Session
 */
function generateSessionId() {
  try {
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = spreadsheet.getActiveSheet();
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    
    // Get current year
    const currentYear = new Date().getFullYear();
    
    // Find Session ID column index
    const headers = data[0];
    const sessionIdColumnIndex = headers.indexOf('Session ID');
    
    if (sessionIdColumnIndex === -1) {
      console.log('Session ID column not found, using fallback');
      // Fallback to timestamp-based ID
      const timestamp = Date.now().toString().slice(-6);
      return `GIS-${currentYear}-${timestamp.slice(0, 3)}`;
    }
    
    // Count existing sessions for this year
    let maxSessionNumber = 0;
    const sessionIdPattern = new RegExp(`GIS-${currentYear}-(\\d{3})`);
    
    for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) { // Skip header row
      const sessionId = data[i][sessionIdColumnIndex];
      if (sessionId && typeof sessionId === 'string') {
        const match = sessionId.match(sessionIdPattern);
        if (match) {
          const sessionNumber = parseInt(match[1]);
          maxSessionNumber = Math.max(maxSessionNumber, sessionNumber);
        }
      }
    }
    
    // Generate next session number
    const nextSessionNumber = maxSessionNumber + 1;
    const sessionId = `GIS-${currentYear}-${String(nextSessionNumber).padStart(3, '0')}`;
    
    console.log('Generated Session ID:', sessionId);
    return sessionId;
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error generating session ID:', error);
    // Fallback to timestamp-based ID
    const timestamp = Date.now().toString().slice(-6);
    return `GIS-${new Date().getFullYear()}-${timestamp.slice(0, 3)}`;
  }
}

/**
 * Handle GET requests for fetching appointments and client responses
 */
function doGet(e) {
  try {
    // Set script timezone to IST at the start
    try {
      PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty('timeZone', 'Asia/Kolkata');
    } catch (tzError) {
      console.log('Timezone setting error (non-critical): ' + tzError.toString());
    }
    
    console.log('doGet called with parameters:', e.parameter);
    
    // SIMPLE TEST ENDPOINT - Test if deployment is working
    if (e.parameter.test === 'ping') {
      return ContentService.createTextOutput(JSON.stringify({
        status: 'success',
        message: 'Google Apps Script is working!',
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
        ownerEmail: CONFIG.OWNER_EMAIL,
        spreadsheetId: '1M0AdgnK2B71XOMw_I6L7eCV6mY9hv9trfno5PheTFOg'
      })).setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON);
    }
    
    const action = e.parameter.action;
    const appointmentId = e.parameter.appointmentId;
    const response = e.parameter.response;
    
    // Handle blocked dates request
    if (action === 'getBlockedDates') {
      // Handle test requests
      if (e.parameter.test === 'true') {
        return createCORSResponse({
          success: true,
          message: 'Blocked dates endpoint is working',
          test: true
        });
      }
      return getBlockedDates();
    }
    
    // Handle available dates request
    if (action === 'getAvailableDates') {
      // Handle test requests
      if (e.parameter.test === 'true') {
        return createCORSResponse({
          success: true,
          message: 'Available dates endpoint is working',
          test: true
        });
      }
      return getAvailableDates();
    }
    
    // Handle login validation via GET (for CORS compatibility)
    if (action === 'validateLogin') {
      console.log('Validating admin login credentials via GET');
      const email = e.parameter.email;
      const password = e.parameter.password;
      return validateAdminLogin(email, password);
    }
    
    // Handle payment proof upload form
    if (appointmentId && e.parameter.uploadPayment === 'true') {
      return showPaymentUploadForm(appointmentId);
    }
    
    // Handle consent form
    if (appointmentId && e.parameter.giveConsent === 'true') {
      return showConsentForm(appointmentId);
    }
    
    // Handle feedback form
    if (appointmentId && e.parameter.submitFeedback === 'true') {
      return showFeedbackForm(appointmentId);
    }
    
    // Handle refund acknowledgment form
    if (appointmentId && e.parameter.acknowledgeRefund === 'true') {
      return showRefundAcknowledgmentForm(appointmentId);
    }
    
    // Handle direct client response URLs without requiring 'action' parameter
    if (appointmentId && response) {
      if (response === 'uploadPayment') {
        return showPaymentUploadForm(appointmentId);
      }
      if (response === 'giveConsent') {
        return showConsentForm(appointmentId);
      }
      if (response === 'submitFeedback') {
        return showFeedbackForm(appointmentId);
      }
      // For 'proceed': show a confirmation page instead of updating immediately.
      // This prevents Gmail link-prefetch and /u/N/ redirects from silently
      // updating the client status before the user actually sees the page.
      if (response === 'proceed') {
        return showProceedConfirmation(appointmentId);
      }
      if (response === 'query') {
        return showQueryForm(appointmentId);
      }
      return handleClientResponse({
        appointmentId: appointmentId,
        response: response
      });
    }
    
    // Reschedule functionality removed - now handled via booking form redirect
    
    if (action === 'getAppointments') {
      return getAppointments();
    }
    
    // Debug function to check Session ID column status
    if (action === 'debugSessionId') {
      return debugSessionIdColumn();
    }
    
    // Handle client responses (Proceed/Query)
    if (action === 'clientResponse') {
      return handleClientResponse(e.parameter);
    }
    
    // Default response - return a simple HTML page
    const defaultHtml = `
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
  <title>Appointment Management System</title>
  <style>
    body { 
      font-family: Arial, sans-serif; 
      text-align: center; 
      padding: 50px; 
      background: linear-gradient(135deg, #667eea 0%, #764ba2 100%);
      color: white;
      min-height: 100vh;
      margin: 0;
      display: flex;
      align-items: center;
      justify-content: center;
    }
    .container {
      background: rgba(255,255,255,0.1);
      padding: 40px;
      border-radius: 15px;
      backdrop-filter: blur(10px);
    }
  </style>
</head>
<body>
  <div class="container">
    <h1>✅ Appointment Management System</h1>
    <p>System is working properly!</p>
    <p>This is the base URL for client responses.</p>
  </div>
</body>
</html>`;
    
    return HtmlService.createHtmlOutput(defaultHtml)
      .setTitle('Appointment Management System')
      .setXFrameOptionsMode(HtmlService.XFrameOptionsMode.ALLOWALL);
      
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error in doGet:', error);
    
    const errorHtml = `
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
  <title>System Error</title>
  <style>
    body { 
      font-family: Arial, sans-serif; 
      text-align: center; 
      padding: 50px; 
      background: #f8f9fa;
    }
    .error { color: #dc3545; }
  </style>
</head>
<body>
  <h1 class="error">System Error</h1>
  <p>Error: ${error.toString()}</p>
</body>
</html>`;
    
    return HtmlService.createHtmlOutput(errorHtml)
      .setTitle('System Error')
      .setXFrameOptionsMode(HtmlService.XFrameOptionsMode.ALLOWALL);
  }
}

/**
 * Handle OPTIONS requests for CORS preflight
 */
function doOptions(e) {
  return createCORSResponse('', true);
}

/**
 * Show a confirmation page for "Proceed" instead of updating status immediately.
 * 
 * This prevents two problems:
 * 1. Gmail's /u/N/ URL rewriting — the page renders fine even through /u/1/ URLs
 *    because HtmlService output works regardless of the account prefix.
 * 2. Silent status updates — the status only changes when the user clicks "Confirm"
 *    which sends a POST request, not on the initial GET (which Gmail may prefetch).
 */
function showProceedConfirmation(appointmentId) {
  // Check if client has already responded
  const existingResponse = getClientResponseStatus(appointmentId);
  if (existingResponse && !existingResponse.includes('Awaiting Response')) {
    return showAlreadyRespondedPage(appointmentId, existingResponse);
  }
  
  const appointment = getAppointmentData(appointmentId);
  if (!appointment) {
    return HtmlService.createHtmlOutput('<html><body><h2>Appointment not found</h2></body></html>')
      .setTitle('Error')
      .setXFrameOptionsMode(HtmlService.XFrameOptionsMode.ALLOWALL);
  }
  
  const scriptUrl = getPublicWebAppUrl();
  
  const html = `
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
  <title>Confirm Proceed - Anurag Sharma Consultation</title>
  <meta charset="utf-8">
  <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1">
  <style>
    body { 
      font-family: 'Segoe UI', Tahoma, Geneva, Verdana, sans-serif; 
      background: linear-gradient(135deg, #667eea 0%, #764ba2 100%);
      min-height: 100vh;
      margin: 0;
      padding: 20px;
      display: flex;
      align-items: center;
      justify-content: center;
    }
    .container {
      background: white;
      padding: 40px;
      border-radius: 15px;
      box-shadow: 0 10px 30px rgba(0,0,0,0.2);
      max-width: 500px;
      width: 90%;
      text-align: center;
    }
    .icon { font-size: 48px; margin-bottom: 20px; }
    .title { color: #333; font-size: 24px; font-weight: 600; margin-bottom: 15px; }
    .message { font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.6; color: #555; margin-bottom: 30px; }
    .highlight { color: #0d6efd; font-weight: 600; }
    .btn {
      display: inline-block;
      padding: 14px 40px;
      font-size: 18px;
      font-weight: 600;
      color: white;
      background: #28a745;
      border: none;
      border-radius: 8px;
      cursor: pointer;
      text-decoration: none;
    }
    .btn:hover { background: #218838; }
    .btn:disabled { background: #ccc; cursor: not-allowed; }
    .spinner { display: none; margin: 20px auto; }
    .success-msg { display: none; color: #28a745; font-size: 18px; margin-top: 20px; }
    .error-msg { display: none; color: #dc3545; font-size: 16px; margin-top: 20px; }
    .footer { font-size: 14px; color: #666; border-top: 1px solid #eee; padding-top: 20px; margin-top: 30px; }
  </style>
</head>
<body>
  <div class="container">
    <div class="icon">🚀</div>
    <div class="title">Confirm Your Response</div>
    <div class="message">
      <p>Dear <span class="highlight">${appointment.name || 'Client'}</span>,</p>
      <p>Please confirm that you would like to <strong>proceed</strong> with your session as planned.</p>
    </div>
    <button class="btn" id="confirmBtn" onclick="confirmProceed()">✅ Confirm Proceed</button>
    <div class="spinner" id="spinner">⏳ Processing...</div>
    <div class="success-msg" id="successMsg">✅ Your response has been recorded successfully!</div>
    <div class="error-msg" id="errorMsg"></div>
    <div class="footer">
      Anurag Sharma - Consultation Services
    </div>
  </div>
  <script>
    function confirmProceed() {
      var btn = document.getElementById('confirmBtn');
      var spinner = document.getElementById('spinner');
      var successMsg = document.getElementById('successMsg');
      var errorMsg = document.getElementById('errorMsg');
      
      btn.disabled = true;
      btn.style.display = 'none';
      spinner.style.display = 'block';
      
      var formData = new FormData();
      formData.append('appointmentId', '${appointmentId}');
      formData.append('action', 'confirmProceed');
      
      fetch('${scriptUrl}', {
        method: 'POST',
        body: formData
      })
      .then(function(resp) { return resp.json(); })
      .then(function(data) {
        spinner.style.display = 'none';
        if (data.status === 'success' || data.success) {
          successMsg.style.display = 'block';
        } else {
          errorMsg.textContent = data.message || 'Something went wrong. Please try again.';
          errorMsg.style.display = 'block';
          btn.style.display = 'inline-block';
          btn.disabled = false;
        }
      })
      .catch(function(err) {
        spinner.style.display = 'none';
        errorMsg.textContent = 'Network error. Please try again.';
        errorMsg.style.display = 'block';
        btn.style.display = 'inline-block';
        btn.disabled = false;
      });
    }
  </script>
</body>
</html>`;
  
  return HtmlService.createHtmlOutput(html)
    .setTitle('Confirm Proceed - Anurag Sharma Consultation')
    .setXFrameOptionsMode(HtmlService.XFrameOptionsMode.ALLOWALL);
}

/**
 * Handle client responses (Proceed/Query)
 */
function handleClientResponse(params) {
  try {
    const { appointmentId, response } = params;
    
    if (!appointmentId || !response) {
      return createCORSResponse({
        status: 'error',
        message: 'Missing appointment ID or response type'
      });
    }
    
    // Check if client has already responded
    const existingResponse = getClientResponseStatus(appointmentId);
    if (existingResponse) {
      return showAlreadyRespondedPage(appointmentId, existingResponse);
    }
    
    if (response === 'proceed') {
      return showProceedConfirmation(appointmentId);
    } else if (response === 'query') {
      return showQueryForm(appointmentId);
    } else {
      return createCORSResponse({
        status: 'error',
        message: 'Invalid response type'
      });
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error handling client response:', error);
    return createCORSResponse({
      status: 'error',
      message: error.toString()
    });
  }
}

/**
 * Handle client choosing to proceed
 */
function handleClientProceed(appointmentId) {
  try {
    // Check if client has already responded - extra protection
    const existingResponse = getClientResponseStatus(appointmentId);
    if (existingResponse && !existingResponse.includes('Awaiting Response')) {
      return showAlreadyRespondedPage(appointmentId, existingResponse);
    }
    
    // Get appointment data to determine appropriate next status
    const appointment = getAppointmentData(appointmentId);
    if (!appointment) {
      throw new Error('Appointment not found');
    }
    
    const mainStatus = appointment.status || 'Pending';
    const currentClientStatus = appointment.clientStatus || appointment['Client Status'] || '';
    
    // Determine the appropriate new client status based on main appointment status
    let newClientStatus;
    if (mainStatus === 'Approved') {
      newClientStatus = 'Proceed';
    } else if (mainStatus === 'Session Scheduled') {
      newClientStatus = 'Proceed';
    } else if (mainStatus === 'Query Resolved') {
      // If query was resolved, continue with the flow based on what stage we're at
      if (currentClientStatus.includes('Query Resolved')) {
        newClientStatus = 'Proceed';
      } else {
        newClientStatus = 'Proceed';
      }
    } else {
      newClientStatus = 'Proceed';
    }
    
    // Update client status in spreadsheet
    updateClientStatus(appointmentId, newClientStatus, null);
    
    // Create HTML using HtmlService for better rendering
    const htmlTemplate = HtmlService.createTemplate(`
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
  <title>Response Recorded - Anurag Sharma Consultation</title>
  <meta charset="utf-8">
  <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1">
  <style>
    body { 
      font-family: 'Segoe UI', Tahoma, Geneva, Verdana, sans-serif; 
      background: linear-gradient(135deg, #667eea 0%, #764ba2 100%);
      min-height: 100vh;
      margin: 0;
      padding: 20px;
      display: flex;
      align-items: center;
      justify-content: center;
    }
    .container {
      background: white;
      padding: 40px;
      border-radius: 15px;
      box-shadow: 0 10px 30px rgba(0,0,0,0.2);
      max-width: 500px;
      width: 90%;
      text-align: center;
    }
    .success { 
      color: #28a745; 
      font-size: 48px; 
      margin-bottom: 20px; 
    }
    .title {
      color: #333;
      font-size: 24px;
      font-weight: 600;
      margin-bottom: 20px;
    }
    .message { 
      font-size: 16px; 
      line-height: 1.6; 
      color: #555; 
      margin-bottom: 30px;
    }
    .highlight {
      color: #0d6efd;
      font-weight: 600;
    }
    .footer {
      font-size: 14px;
      color: #666;
      border-top: 1px solid #eee;
      padding-top: 20px;
      margin-top: 30px;
    }
  </style>
</head>
<body>
  <div class="container">
    <div class="success">✅</div>
    <div class="title">Thank You!</div>
    <div class="message">
      <p>Your response has been recorded successfully.</p>
      <p>You have chosen to <span class="highlight">proceed</span> with the session as planned.</p>
      <p>We will contact you soon with further details including payment information and session confirmation.</p>
    </div>
    <div class="footer">
      <p>Anurag Sharma - Strategic Consultation Services</p>
    </div>
  </div>
</body>
</html>`);
    
    return htmlTemplate.evaluate()
      .setTitle('Response Recorded')
      .setXFrameOptionsMode(HtmlService.XFrameOptionsMode.ALLOWALL);
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error handling proceed response:', error);
    return createCORSResponse({
      status: 'error',
      message: error.toString()
    });
  }
}

/**

 */
function showQueryForm(appointmentId) {
  try {
    // Check if client has already responded - extra protection
    const existingResponse = getClientResponseStatus(appointmentId);

      Please describe your questions or concerns regarding the session. You can also upload a document if needed. We will review your query and respond within 24 hours.
    </div>
    
    <form id="queryForm">
      <input type="hidden" name="action" value="submitClientQuery">
      <input type="hidden" name="appointmentId" value="<?= appointmentId ?>">
      
      <div class="form-group">
        <label for="query">Your Query:</label>
        <textarea name="query" id="query" rows="6" maxlength="600" required 
                  placeholder="Please describe your questions or concerns about the session..."></textarea>
        <div class="char-count" id="charCount">0 / 100 words</div>
      </div>
      
      <div class="form-group">
        <label for="queryDocument">
          <i class="fas fa-paperclip"></i> Attach Document (Optional)
        </label>
        <input type="file" name="queryDocument" id="queryDocument" class="form-control" 
               accept=".pdf,.doc,.docx,.txt,.jpg,.jpeg,.png,.gif">
        <div class="file-info">
          <small>Supported formats: PDF, DOC, DOCX, TXT, JPG, PNG, GIF (Max 10MB)</small>
        </div>
      </div>
      
      <button type="submit" class="btn" id="submitBtn">
        <span id="submitText">Submit Query</span>
        <span id="submitLoader" style="display: none;">
          <i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> Processing...
        </span>
      </button>
    </form>
  </div>
    
  <script>
    const form = document.getElementById('queryForm');
    const submitBtn = document.getElementById('submitBtn');
    
    form.addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      
      const submitText = document.getElementById('submitText');
      const submitLoader = document.getElementById('submitLoader');
      const queryText = document.getElementById('query').value;
      const fileInput = document.getElementById('queryDocument');
      const file = fileInput.files.length > 0 ? fileInput.files[0] : null;

      // Disable button to prevent double submission
      submitBtn.disabled = true;
      submitText.style.display = 'none';
      submitLoader.style.display = 'inline-block';

      const handleSubmission = (fileData = '', fileName = '', fileType = '') => {
        // Prepare parameters for google.script.run
        const params = {
          action: 'submitClientQuery',
          appointmentId: '<?= appointmentId ?>',
          query: queryText
        };
        
        if (file && fileData) {
          params.queryDocument = fileData;
          params.queryDocumentName = fileName;
          params.queryDocumentType = fileType;
        }

        // Use google.script.run instead of fetch to avoid CORS issues
        google.script.run
          .withSuccessHandler(function(response) {
            if (response && response.status === 'success') {
              // Show success message by replacing the form
              document.getElementById('formContainer').innerHTML = \`
                <div style="text-align: center;">
                  <div style="font-size: 48px; color: #28a745;">✅</div>
                  <h2 style="color: #333;">Query Submitted!</h2>
                  <p style="font-size: 16px; color: #555;">Your query has been submitted successfully. We will review it and respond within 24 hours.</p>
                </div>
              \`;
            } else {
              // Show error message
              alert('Error: ' + (response ? response.message : 'Unknown error occurred'));
              resetSubmitButton();
            }
          })
          .withFailureHandler(function(error) {
            console.error('Submission Error:', error);
            alert('There was a technical error submitting your query. Please try again.');
            resetSubmitButton();
          })
          .handleClientQuery(params);
      };

      if (file) {
        // Validate file size (10MB max)
        if (file.size > 10 * 1024 * 1024) {
          alert('File size exceeds 10MB limit. Please choose a smaller file.');
          resetSubmitButton();
          return;
        }
        
        // Read file as base64 (EXACTLY like payment proof upload)
        const reader = new FileReader();
        reader.onload = function(e) {
          const base64Data = e.target.result.split(',')[1]; // Get base64 part only
          handleSubmission(base64Data, file.name, file.type);
        };
        reader.readAsDataURL(file);
      } else {
        // If no file, submit directly
        handleSubmission();
      }
    });

    function resetSubmitButton() {
      const submitText = document.getElementById('submitText');
      const submitLoader = document.getElementById('submitLoader');
      submitBtn.disabled = false;
      submitText.style.display = 'inline-block';
      submitLoader.style.display = 'none';
    }

    // Word count functionality (no changes needed here)
    const textarea = document.getElementById('query');
    const charCount = document.getElementById('charCount');
    textarea.addEventListener('input', function() {
        const words = this.value.trim().split(/\\s+/).filter(word => word.length > 0);
        const wordCount = this.value.trim() === '' ? 0 : words.length;
        charCount.textContent = wordCount + ' / 100 words';
    });
  </script>
</body>
</html>`);
    
    htmlTemplate.scriptUrl = scriptUrl;
    htmlTemplate.appointmentId = appointmentId;
    
    return htmlTemplate.evaluate()
      .setTitle('Submit Your Query')
      .setXFrameOptionsMode(HtmlService.XFrameOptionsMode.ALLOWALL);
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error showing query form:', error);
    return createCORSResponse({
      status: 'error',
      message: error.toString()
    });
  }
}

/**
 * Handle submitted client query - CRITICAL: Must run with proper permissions
 */
/**
 * Handle submitted client query - CRITICAL: Must run with proper permissions
 */
function handleClientQuery(params) {
  try {
    console.log('handleClientQuery called with:', params);

    const { appointmentId, query, isAdminAction } = params;

    if (!appointmentId || !query) {
      console.error('Missing appointment ID or query text');
      // Return a simple error object
      return { status: 'error', message: 'Missing appointment ID or query text' };
    }

    // Check if client has already responded (skip this for admin actions)
    if (!isAdminAction) {
      const existingResponse = getClientResponseStatus(appointmentId);
      if (existingResponse) {
        // This won't show the nice page, but will prevent duplicate submissions
        return { status: 'error', message: 'You have already responded to this request.' };
      }
    }

    const appointment = getAppointmentData(appointmentId);
    if (!appointment) {
      console.error('Appointment not found for query submission');
      return { status: 'error', message: 'Appointment not found' };
    }

    // Smart query submission checks (skip some for admin actions)
    if (!isAdminAction && isQueryOnCooldown(appointment)) {
      const msg = `Please wait at least ${CONFIG.QUERY_COOLDOWN_MINUTES} minutes between query submissions.`;
      console.error(msg);
      return { status: 'error', message: msg };
    }

    if (!isAdminAction && isDuplicateQuery(appointment, query)) {
      const msg = 'This query appears to be very similar to a recent submission.';
      console.error(msg);
      return { status: 'error', message: msg };
    }

    const currentClientStatus = appointment.clientStatus || appointment['Client Status'] || '';
    // Allow new queries if:
    // 1. There's no current query status OR
    // 2. The previous query has been resolved (contains "Resolved") OR  
    // 3. This is an admin action
    // Note: We allow new queries even after "Query Resolved" to enable unlimited queries
    if (!isAdminAction && 
        currentClientStatus === 'Query' && 
        !currentClientStatus.includes('Resolved')) {
        const msg = 'You have a query currently being processed. Please wait for our response.';
        console.error(msg);
        return { status: 'error', message: msg };
    }

    const wordCount = query.trim().split(/\s+/).filter(word => word.length > 0).length;
    if (wordCount > 100) {
      const msg = 'Query exceeds 100 words limit';
      console.error(msg, wordCount);
      return { status: 'error', message: msg };
    }

    let fileLink = '';
    if (params.queryDocument && params.queryDocumentName && params.queryDocumentType) {
      try {
        console.log('Processing query document upload:', params.queryDocumentName);
        const fileBlob = Utilities.newBlob(
          Utilities.base64Decode(params.queryDocument),
          params.queryDocumentType,
          params.queryDocumentName
        );
        const clientNameForFile = appointment.name || appointment['Full Name *'] || 'UnknownClient';
        const uploadedFile = uploadUserQueryDocument(appointmentId, fileBlob, clientNameForFile);
        fileLink = uploadedFile.url;
        console.log('User query document uploaded:', uploadedFile);
      } catch (fileError) {
        console.error('Error uploading user query document:', fileError);
      }
    }

    updateClientStatus(appointmentId, 'Query', query);
    
    // Also update the main appointment status to indicate a new query was received
    updateMainAppointmentStatus(appointmentId, 'New Query Received');
    
    addQueryToHistory(appointmentId, query, fileLink);

    if (fileLink) {
      updateUserQueryDocuments(appointmentId, fileLink);
    }

    sendQueryNotificationToAdmin(appointmentId, query, fileLink);

    // *** THE FIX: Return a simple JavaScript object ***
    return { status: 'success', message: 'Query submitted successfully.' };

  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error handling client query:', error);
    // *** THE FIX: Return a simple JavaScript error object ***
    return { status: 'error', message: error.toString() };
  }
}

<body>
  <div class="container" id="errorContainer">
    <div class="icon" id="errorIcon">❌</div>
    <div class="title" id="errorTitle">Query Submission Issue</div>
    <div class="message">
      <p id="errorMessage">${message}</p>
    </div>
    <a href="javascript:history.back()" class="retry-btn">← Go Back</a>
    <div class="footer">
      <p>For urgent matters, contact us at <strong>theanuragsharma.web@gmail.com</strong></p>
    </div>
  </div>
  
  <script>
    function getErrorClass(message) {
      if (message.includes('minutes between')) return 'cooldown';
      if (message.includes('similar to a recent')) return 'duplicate';
      if (message.includes('currently being processed')) return 'processing';
      return 'error';
    }
    
    function getErrorIcon(message) {
      if (message.includes('minutes between')) return '⏰';
      if (message.includes('similar to a recent')) return '📋';
      if (message.includes('currently being processed')) return '⚙️';
      return '❌';
    }
    
    function getErrorTitle(message) {
      if (message.includes('minutes between')) return 'Query Cooldown Active';
      if (message.includes('similar to a recent')) return 'Similar Query Detected';
      if (message.includes('currently being processed')) return 'Query In Progress';
      return 'Query Submission Issue';
    }
    
    // Apply the appropriate class and content after page loads
    const container = document.getElementById('errorContainer');
    const message = document.getElementById('errorMessage').textContent;
    container.className = 'container ' + getErrorClass(message);
    document.getElementById('errorIcon').textContent = getErrorIcon(message);
    document.getElementById('errorTitle').textContent = getErrorTitle(message);
  </script>
</body>
</html>`;

  return HtmlService.createHtmlOutput(errorHtml)
    .setTitle('Query Submission Notice')
    .setXFrameOptionsMode(HtmlService.XFrameOptionsMode.ALLOWALL);
}

/**
 * Update client status in spreadsheet
 */
function updateClientStatus(appointmentId, status, query) {
  try {
    console.log('updateClientStatus called:', { appointmentId, status, query: !!query });
    
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = spreadsheet.getActiveSheet();
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    
    if (data.length <= 1) {
      console.error('No appointment data found in spreadsheet');
      throw new Error('No appointment data found in spreadsheet');
    }
    
    const headers = data[0];
    // Find row index by Session ID instead of assuming appointmentId is a row number
    const rowIndex = findRowIndexBySessionId(appointmentId);
    
    console.log('Processing row index:', rowIndex, 'Total rows:', data.length);
    
    if (rowIndex === -1) {
      console.error('Appointment not found for Session ID:', appointmentId);
      throw new Error(`Appointment not found for Session ID: ${appointmentId}`);
    }
    
    if (rowIndex >= 2 && rowIndex <= data.length) {
      // Find the Client Status, Client Query, and Reschedule History column indices
      let clientStatusColIndex = headers.indexOf('Client Status');
      let clientQueryColIndex = headers.indexOf('Client Query');
      let rescheduleHistoryColIndex = headers.indexOf('Reschedule History');
      
      // Add Client Status column if it doesn't exist
      if (clientStatusColIndex === -1) {
        console.log('Client Status column not found, adding it...');
        headers.push('Client Status');
        clientStatusColIndex = headers.length - 1;
        sheet.getRange(1, clientStatusColIndex + 1).setValue('Client Status');
        console.log('Client Status column added at index:', clientStatusColIndex);
      }
      
      // Add Client Query column if it doesn't exist
      if (clientQueryColIndex === -1) {
        console.log('Client Query column not found, adding it...');
        headers.push('Client Query');
        clientQueryColIndex = headers.length - 1;
        sheet.getRange(1, clientQueryColIndex + 1).setValue('Client Query');
        console.log('Client Query column added at index:', clientQueryColIndex);
      }
      
      // Reschedule History column removed - reschedule now via booking form
      
      // Update the client status
      console.log('Updating client status at row:', rowIndex, 'column:', clientStatusColIndex + 1, 'with value:', status);
      sheet.getRange(rowIndex, clientStatusColIndex + 1).setValue(status);
      
      // Update the client query if provided
      if (query && clientQueryColIndex !== -1) {
        console.log('Updating client query at row:', rowIndex, 'column:', clientQueryColIndex + 1);
        sheet.getRange(rowIndex, clientQueryColIndex + 1).setValue(query);
        console.log('Client query updated successfully');
      }
      
      // Force save to ensure the update is persisted
      SpreadsheetApp.flush();
      
      console.log('Client status and query update completed successfully');
      
      // Verify the updates by reading the values back
      const updatedStatus = sheet.getRange(rowIndex, clientStatusColIndex + 1).getValue();
      const updatedQuery = query ? sheet.getRange(rowIndex, clientQueryColIndex + 1).getValue() : 'N/A';
      console.log('Verification - Status written:', updatedStatus, 'Query written:', updatedQuery);
      
    } else {
      const errorMsg = `Invalid row index: ${rowIndex}, Data length: ${data.length}`;
      console.error(errorMsg);
      throw new Error(errorMsg);
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error updating client status:', error);
    throw error;
  }
}

/**
 * Update main appointment status in spreadsheet
 */
function updateMainAppointmentStatus(appointmentId, status) {
  try {
    console.log('updateMainAppointmentStatus called:', { appointmentId, status });
    
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = spreadsheet.getActiveSheet();
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    
    if (data.length <= 1) {
      console.error('No appointment data found in spreadsheet');
      throw new Error('No appointment data found in spreadsheet');
    }
    
    const headers = data[0];
    const rowIndex = findRowIndexBySessionId(appointmentId);
    
    console.log('Processing row index:', rowIndex, 'Total rows:', data.length);
    
    if (rowIndex === -1) {
      console.error('Appointment not found for Session ID:', appointmentId);
      throw new Error(`Appointment not found for Session ID: ${appointmentId}`);
    }
    
    if (rowIndex >= 2 && rowIndex <= data.length) {
      // Find the main Status column
      let statusColIndex = headers.indexOf('Status');
      
      // Add Status column if it doesn't exist (though it should exist)
      if (statusColIndex === -1) {
        console.log('Status column not found, adding it...');
        headers.push('Status');
        statusColIndex = headers.length - 1;
        sheet.getRange(1, statusColIndex + 1).setValue('Status');
        console.log('Status column added at index:', statusColIndex);
      }
      
      // Update the main appointment status
      console.log('Updating main status at row:', rowIndex, 'column:', statusColIndex + 1, 'with value:', status);
      sheet.getRange(rowIndex, statusColIndex + 1).setValue(status);
      
      // Force save to ensure the update is persisted
      SpreadsheetApp.flush();
      
      console.log('Main appointment status update completed successfully');
      
      // Verify the update by reading the value back
      const updatedStatus = sheet.getRange(rowIndex, statusColIndex + 1).getValue();
      console.log('Verification - Main status written:', updatedStatus);
      
    } else {
      const errorMsg = `Invalid row index: ${rowIndex}, Data length: ${data.length}`;
      console.error(errorMsg);
      throw new Error(errorMsg);
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error updating main appointment status:', error);
    throw error;
  }
}

/**
 * Update payment proof hyperlink in spreadsheet
 */
function updatePaymentProofLink(appointmentId, fileId, fileName) {
  try {
    console.log('updatePaymentProofLink called:', { appointmentId, fileId, fileName });
    
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = spreadsheet.getActiveSheet();
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    
    if (data.length <= 1) {
      console.error('No appointment data found in spreadsheet');
      return;
    }
    
    const headers = data[0];
    const rowIndex = findRowIndexBySessionId(appointmentId);
    
    console.log('Headers:', headers);
    console.log('Looking for appointment ID:', appointmentId);
    console.log('Found row index:', rowIndex);
    
    if (rowIndex >= 2 && rowIndex <= data.length) {
      // Find the Payment Proof Link column index
      let paymentProofColIndex = -1;
      
      headers.forEach((header, index) => {
        if (header === 'Payment Proof Link') {
          paymentProofColIndex = index;
        }
      });
      
      console.log('Payment Proof Link column index:', paymentProofColIndex);
      
      // Add Payment Proof Link column if it doesn't exist
      if (paymentProofColIndex === -1) {
        headers.push('Payment Proof Link');
        paymentProofColIndex = headers.length - 1;
        sheet.getRange(1, paymentProofColIndex + 1).setValue('Payment Proof Link');
        console.log('Added Payment Proof Link column at index:', paymentProofColIndex);
      }
      
      // Create hyperlink formula for Google Drive file
      const fileUrl = `https://drive.google.com/file/d/${fileId}/view`;
      const hyperlinkFormula = `=HYPERLINK("${fileUrl}", "${fileName}")`;
      
      // Update the payment proof link
      sheet.getRange(rowIndex, paymentProofColIndex + 1).setValue(hyperlinkFormula);
      console.log('Updated payment proof link:', hyperlinkFormula);
      
      console.log('Payment proof link update completed successfully');
    } else {
      console.error('Invalid row index:', rowIndex, 'Data length:', data.length);
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error updating payment proof link:', error);
    throw error;
  }
}

/**
 * Upload user query document to Google Drive
 */
function uploadUserQueryDocument(appointmentId, fileBlob, clientName) {
  try {
    console.log('Uploading user query document for appointment:', appointmentId);
    
    // Get the folder
    const folder = DriveApp.getFolderById(CONFIG.USER_QUERY_DOCUMENTS_FOLDER_ID);
    
    // Create filename with appointment ID and client name
    const timestamp = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 19).replace(/:/g, '-');
    const originalName = fileBlob.getName() || 'document';
    const extension = originalName.split('.').pop() || 'txt';
    const fileName = `${appointmentId}_${clientName}_Query_${timestamp}.${extension}`;

    // Upload file
    const file = folder.createFile(fileBlob.setName(fileName));
    
    // Get the file and make it publicly accessible
    const driveFile = DriveApp.getFileById(file.getId());
    
    // Set sharing to anyone with link can view
    try {
      driveFile.setSharing(DriveApp.Access.ANYONE_WITH_LINK, DriveApp.Permission.VIEW);
    } catch (e) {
      console.log('Could not set sharing, file may inherit folder permissions:', e);
    }
    
    // Use the sharing URL format that works
    const fileUrl = `https://drive.google.com/file/d/${file.getId()}/view?usp=sharing`;    console.log('User query document uploaded successfully:', fileName);
    
    return {
      id: file.getId(),
      name: fileName,
      url: fileUrl,
      size: fileBlob.getBytes().length
    };
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error uploading user query document:', error);
    throw error;
  }
}

/**
 * Upload admin query response document to Google Drive
 */
function uploadAdminQueryDocument(appointmentId, fileBlob, adminName = 'Admin') {
  try {
    console.log('Uploading admin query document for appointment:', appointmentId);
    
    // Get the folder
    const folder = DriveApp.getFolderById(CONFIG.ADMIN_QUERY_DOCUMENTS_FOLDER_ID);
    
    // Create filename with appointment ID and admin identifier
    const timestamp = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 19).replace(/:/g, '-');
    const originalName = fileBlob.getName() || 'document';
    const extension = originalName.split('.').pop() || 'txt';
    const fileName = `${appointmentId}_${adminName}_Response_${timestamp}.${extension}`;

    // Upload file
    const file = folder.createFile(fileBlob.setName(fileName));
    
    // Get the file and make it publicly accessible
    const driveFile = DriveApp.getFileById(file.getId());
    
    // Set sharing to anyone with link can view
    try {
      driveFile.setSharing(DriveApp.Access.ANYONE_WITH_LINK, DriveApp.Permission.VIEW);
    } catch (e) {
      console.log('Could not set sharing, file may inherit folder permissions:', e);
    }
    
    // Use the sharing URL format that works
    const fileUrl = `https://drive.google.com/file/d/${file.getId()}/view?usp=sharing`;    console.log('Admin query document uploaded successfully:', fileName);
    
    return {
      id: file.getId(),
      name: fileName,
      url: fileUrl,
      size: fileBlob.getBytes().length
    };
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error uploading admin query document:', error);
    throw error;
  }
}

/**
 * Update user query documents column in spreadsheet
 */
function updateUserQueryDocuments(appointmentId, fileLink) {
  try {
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = spreadsheet.getActiveSheet();
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const headers = data[0];
    
    const rowIndex = findRowIndexBySessionId(appointmentId);
    
    if (rowIndex >= 2 && rowIndex <= data.length) {
      let userDocumentsIndex = headers.indexOf('User Query Documents');
      
      // Add column if it doesn't exist
      if (userDocumentsIndex === -1) {
        headers.push('User Query Documents');
        userDocumentsIndex = headers.length - 1;
        sheet.getRange(1, userDocumentsIndex + 1).setValue('User Query Documents');
      }
      
      // Get existing documents
      const existingDocs = sheet.getRange(rowIndex, userDocumentsIndex + 1).getValue() || '';
      
      // Append new document link
      const updatedDocs = existingDocs ? 
        `${existingDocs}\n${fileLink}` : fileLink;
      
      sheet.getRange(rowIndex, userDocumentsIndex + 1).setValue(updatedDocs);
      console.log('User query documents updated successfully');
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error updating user query documents:', error);
    throw error;
  }
}

/**
 * Send query notification to admin
 */
function sendQueryNotificationToAdmin(appointmentId, query, fileLink = '') {
  try {
    console.log('sendQueryNotificationToAdmin called:', { appointmentId, query: !!query, hasFile: !!fileLink });
    
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = spreadsheet.getActiveSheet();
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    
    if (data.length <= 1) {
      console.error('No appointment data found for notification');
      return;
    }
    
    const headers = data[0];
    const rowIndex = findRowIndexBySessionId(appointmentId);
    
    if (rowIndex >= 2 && rowIndex <= data.length) {
      const row = data[rowIndex - 1];
      const appointment = {};
      
      headers.forEach((header, index) => {
        const fieldKey = getFieldKey(header);
        appointment[fieldKey] = row[index] || '';
      });
      
      const clientName = appointment.name || appointment['name'] || appointment['Full Name *'] || 'Unknown Client';
      const subject = `Client Query Received - ${clientName}`;
      const body = `
<h2>Client Query Received</h2>
<p><strong>Client:</strong> ${clientName}</p>
<p><strong>Email:</strong> ${appointment.email || appointment['email'] || appointment['Email Address *'] || 'Unknown'}</p>
<p><strong>Organization:</strong> ${appointment.organization || appointment['organization'] || appointment['Organization *'] || 'Unknown'}</p>
<p><strong>Session ID:</strong> ${appointment.sessionId || appointment['Session ID'] || 'Not specified'}</p>

<h3>Client Query:</h3>
<div style="background: #f8f9fa; padding: 15px; border-radius: 8px; margin: 15px 0; border-left: 4px solid #007bff;">
  <p style="margin: 0; font-style: italic;">"${query}"</p>
</div>

${fileLink ? `
<h3>📎 Attached Document:</h3>
<div style="background: #e3f2fd; padding: 15px; border-radius: 8px; margin: 15px 0; border-left: 4px solid #2196f3;">
  <p><a href="${fileLink}" target="_blank" style="color: #1976d2; text-decoration: none;">📄 View Uploaded Document</a></p>
</div>
` : ''}

<p>Please review and respond to the client's query through the admin dashboard.</p>

<p><a href="http://theanuragsharma.com/admin-login.html" style="background: #007bff; color: white; padding: 10px 20px; text-decoration: none; border-radius: 5px;">Manage Appointments</a></p>
      `;
      
      MailApp.sendEmail({
        to: CONFIG.OWNER_EMAIL,
        subject: subject,
        htmlBody: body
      });
      
      console.log('Query notification sent to admin successfully');
    } else {
      console.error('Invalid appointment ID for notification:', appointmentId);
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error sending query notification:', error);
    throw error;
  }
}

/**
 * DEPRECATED: Check reschedule cooldown
 * This function is no longer used. Rescheduling is now handled via the booking form redirect.
 * Kept for reference only - can be removed in future cleanup.
 */
function isRescheduleOnCooldown(appointment) {
  try {
    const rescheduleHistory = appointment.rescheduleHistory || appointment['Reschedule History'] || '';
    
    if (!rescheduleHistory || rescheduleHistory.trim() === '') {
      return false; // No previous reschedules, no cooldown
    }
    
    // Get the most recent reschedule timestamp
    const rescheduleEntries = rescheduleHistory.split('\n').filter(entry => 
      entry.trim() !== '' && entry.includes('rescheduled')
    );
    
    if (rescheduleEntries.length === 0) {
      return false; // No reschedules found
    }
    
    // Parse the most recent reschedule timestamp
    const mostRecentEntry = rescheduleEntries[rescheduleEntries.length - 1];
    const timestampMatch = mostRecentEntry.match(/^([^:]+):/);
    
    if (!timestampMatch) {
      return false; // Could not parse timestamp
    }
    
    try {
      const lastRescheduleTime = new Date(timestampMatch[1]);
      const now = new Date();
      const minutesSinceLastReschedule = (now - lastRescheduleTime) / (1000 * 60);
      
      console.log('Last reschedule was', minutesSinceLastReschedule, 'minutes ago');
      return minutesSinceLastReschedule < CONFIG.RESCHEDULE_COOLDOWN_MINUTES;
    } catch (parseError) {
      console.log('Could not parse reschedule timestamp, allowing reschedule');
      return false;
    }
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error checking reschedule cooldown:', error);
    return false; // Allow reschedule if we can't check
  }
}

/**
 * Check if client has submitted a query too recently (cooldown period)
 */
function isQueryOnCooldown(appointment) {
  try {
    const queryHistory = appointment.queryHistory || appointment['Query History'] || '';
    
    if (!queryHistory || queryHistory.trim() === '') {
      return false; // No previous queries, no cooldown
    }
    
    // Get the most recent query timestamp
    const queryEntries = queryHistory.split('\n').filter(entry => 
      entry.trim() !== '' && entry.includes('Client submitted query')
    );
    
    if (queryEntries.length === 0) {
      return false; // No client queries found
    }
    
    // Parse the most recent query timestamp
    const mostRecentEntry = queryEntries[queryEntries.length - 1];
    const timestampMatch = mostRecentEntry.match(/^(\d{2}\/\d{2}\/\d{4}, \d{1,2}:\d{2}:\d{2} [AP]M):/);
    
    if (!timestampMatch) {
      return false; // Could not parse timestamp
    }
    
    const lastQueryTime = new Date(timestampMatch[1]);
    const now = new Date();
    const minutesSinceLastQuery = (now - lastQueryTime) / (1000 * 60);
    
    console.log('Last query was', minutesSinceLastQuery, 'minutes ago');
    return minutesSinceLastQuery < CONFIG.QUERY_COOLDOWN_MINUTES;
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error checking query cooldown:', error);
    return false; // Allow query if we can't check
  }
}

/**
 * Check if query is a duplicate of recent queries
 */
function isDuplicateQuery(appointment, newQuery) {
  try {
    const queryHistory = appointment.queryHistory || appointment['Query History'] || '';
    
    if (!queryHistory || queryHistory.trim() === '') {
      return false; // No previous queries
    }
    
    // Get recent query texts (last 3 queries)
    const queryEntries = queryHistory.split('\n').filter(entry => 
      entry.trim() !== '' && entry.includes('Client submitted query')
    );
    
    const recentQueries = queryEntries.slice(-3); // Last 3 queries
    
    // Check if new query is similar to any recent query
    const normalizedNewQuery = newQuery.toLowerCase().trim();
    
    for (const entry of recentQueries) {
      // Extract query text from history entry
      const queryMatch = entry.match(/Client submitted query: (.+?)(?:\s\[Document:|$)/);
      if (queryMatch) {
        const existingQuery = queryMatch[1].toLowerCase().trim();
        
        // Check for exact match or very similar queries
        if (existingQuery === normalizedNewQuery || 
            calculateSimilarity(existingQuery, normalizedNewQuery) > 0.8) {
          return true;
        }
      }
    }
    
    return false;
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error checking duplicate query:', error);
    return false; // Allow query if we can't check
  }
}

/**
 * Calculate similarity between two strings (simple algorithm)
 */
function calculateSimilarity(str1, str2) {
  const len1 = str1.length;
  const len2 = str2.length;
  
  if (len1 === 0 || len2 === 0) return 0;
  
  const maxLen = Math.max(len1, len2);
  const minLen = Math.min(len1, len2);
  
  // Simple character overlap calculation
  let matches = 0;
  for (let i = 0; i < minLen; i++) {
    if (str1[i] === str2[i]) matches++;
  }
  
  return matches / maxLen;
}

/**
 * Get client response status to prevent duplicate submissions
 */
function getClientResponseStatus(appointmentId) {
  try {
    console.log('Checking existing response for appointment ID:', appointmentId);
    
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = spreadsheet.getActiveSheet();
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    
    if (data.length <= 1) {
      console.log('No data found in spreadsheet');
      return null;
    }
    
    const headers = data[0];
    // Find row index by Session ID instead of assuming appointmentId is a row number
    const rowIndex = findRowIndexBySessionId(appointmentId);
    
    if (rowIndex === -1) {
      console.log('Appointment not found for Session ID:', appointmentId);
      return null;
    }
    
    if (rowIndex >= 2 && rowIndex <= data.length) {
      const row = data[rowIndex - 1];
      
      // Find Client Status column
      const clientStatusIndex = headers.indexOf('Client Status');
      
      if (clientStatusIndex !== -1) {
        const clientStatus = row[clientStatusIndex];
        console.log('Found client status:', clientStatus);
        
        // Allow responses for statuses that include "Awaiting Response" or "New Time Slot Chosen"
        const allowedResponseStatuses = ['Awaiting Response', 'New Time Slot Chosen', 'Pending'];
        const canRespond = allowedResponseStatuses.some(status => 
          clientStatus && clientStatus.toString().includes(status)
        ) || !clientStatus || clientStatus === '';
        
        if (canRespond) {
          console.log('Client can respond, current status:', clientStatus);
          return null;
        }
        
        // Block responses only for final statuses
        const finalStatuses = ['Proceed', 'Payment Proof Uploaded', 'Consent Given', 'Feedback Received'];
        const isBlocked = finalStatuses.some(status => 
          clientStatus && clientStatus.toString() === status
        );
        
        if (isBlocked) {
          console.log('Client has already completed response with:', clientStatus);
          return clientStatus;
        }
        
        // For "Query" status, check if it's resolved or still pending
        if (clientStatus === 'Query') {
          console.log('Client has Query status - checking if resolved');
          // Allow response only if query has been resolved
          const queryHistory = appointment.queryHistory || appointment['Query History'] || '';
          const hasResolution = queryHistory.includes('Admin resolved query');
          
          if (!hasResolution) {
            console.log('Query is still pending resolution - blocking response');
            return clientStatus; // Block response
          } else {
            console.log('Query has been resolved - allowing response');
            return null; // Allow response
          }
        }
        
        console.log('Client can still respond, current status:', clientStatus);
      }
    }
    
    console.log('No existing response found - client can respond');
    return null;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error checking client response status:', error);
    return null; // Allow proceeding if there's an error checking
  }
}

/**
 * Show page when client has already responded
 */
function showAlreadyRespondedPage(appointmentId, existingResponse) {
  try {
    const htmlTemplate = HtmlService.createTemplate(`
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
  <title>Already Responded - Anurag Sharma Consultation</title>
  <meta charset="utf-8">
  <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1">
  <style>
    body { 
      font-family: 'Segoe UI', Tahoma, Geneva, Verdana, sans-serif; 
      background: linear-gradient(135deg, #ffc107 0%, #ff8800 100%);
      min-height: 100vh;
      margin: 0;
      display: flex;
      align-items: center;
      justify-content: center;
    }
    .container {
      background: white;
      padding: 40px;
      border-radius: 15px;
      box-shadow: 0 10px 30px rgba(0,0,0,0.2);
      max-width: 500px;
      width: 90%;
      text-align: center;
    }
    .warning { 
      color: #ff8800; 
      font-size: 48px; 
      margin-bottom: 20px; 
    }
    .title {
      color: #333;
      font-size: 24px;
      font-weight: 600;
      margin-bottom: 20px;
    }
    .message { 
      font-size: 16px; 
      line-height: 1.6; 
      color: #555; 
      margin-bottom: 30px;
    }
    .highlight {
      color: #ff8800;
      font-weight: 600;
    }
    .status-badge {
      background: #e3f2fd;
      color: #1976d2;
      padding: 8px 16px;
      border-radius: 20px;
      font-weight: 600;
      display: inline-block;
      margin: 10px 0;
    }
    .footer {
      font-size: 14px;
      color: #666;
      border-top: 1px solid #eee;
      padding-top: 20px;
      margin-top: 30px;
    }
  </style>
</head>
<body>
  <div class="container">
    <div class="warning">⚠️</div>
    <div class="title">Response Already Recorded</div>
    <div class="message">
      <p>You have already responded to this appointment request.</p>
      <p>Your current response status is:</p>
      <div class="status-badge"><?= existingResponse ?></div>
      <p>If you need to make changes or have additional questions, please contact us directly at <span class="highlight">theanuragsharma.web@gmail.com</span></p>
    </div>
    <div class="footer">
      <p>Anurag Sharma - Strategic Consultation Services</p>
    </div>
  </div>
</body>
</html>`);
    
    htmlTemplate.existingResponse = existingResponse;
    
    return htmlTemplate.evaluate()
      .setTitle('Already Responded')
      .setXFrameOptionsMode(HtmlService.XFrameOptionsMode.ALLOWALL);
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error showing already responded page:', error);
    return createCORSResponse({
      status: 'error',
      message: error.toString()
    });
  }
}


/**
 * Get appointment data by ID
 */
function getAppointmentData(appointmentId) {
  try {
    console.log('getAppointmentData called with ID:', appointmentId);
    
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = spreadsheet.getActiveSheet();
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const formulas = sheet.getDataRange().getFormulas(); // Get formulas for HYPERLINK handling
    const displayValues = sheet.getDataRange().getDisplayValues(); // Get display values
    
    if (data.length <= 1) {
      console.error('No appointment data found in spreadsheet');
      return null;
    }
    
    const headers = data[0];
    // Find row index by Session ID instead of assuming appointmentId is a row number
    const rowIndex = findRowIndexBySessionId(appointmentId);
    
    console.log('Headers:', headers);
    console.log('Looking for row index:', rowIndex);
    
    // Find Payment Proof Link column index
    const paymentProofColIndex = headers.indexOf('Payment Proof Link');
    console.log('Payment Proof Link column index:', paymentProofColIndex);
    
    if (rowIndex === -1) {
      console.error('Appointment not found for Session ID:', appointmentId);
      return null;
    }
    
    if (rowIndex >= 2 && rowIndex <= data.length) {
      const row = data[rowIndex - 1];
      const formulaRow = formulas[rowIndex - 1] || [];
      const displayRow = displayValues[rowIndex - 1] || [];
      const appointment = {};
      
      headers.forEach((header, index) => {
        const fieldKey = getFieldKey(header);
        let value = row[index] || '';
        
        // Special handling for Payment Proof Link column
        if (header === 'Payment Proof Link' && index === paymentProofColIndex) {
          const formula = formulaRow[index] || '';
          const displayValue = displayRow[index] || '';
          
          console.log(`Payment Proof Link for row ${rowIndex}:`, {
            rawValue: value,
            formula: formula,
            displayValue: displayValue
          });
          
          // If there's a HYPERLINK formula, use it
          if (formula && formula.includes('=HYPERLINK')) {
            value = formula;
            console.log(`Using HYPERLINK formula:`, value);
          } 
          // If no formula but there's a raw value, use it
          else if (value && value.trim() !== '') {
            console.log(`Using raw value:`, value);
          }
          // If there's a display value, use it
          else if (displayValue && displayValue.trim() !== '') {
            console.log(`Using display value:`, displayValue);
            value = displayValue;
          }
        }
        
        appointment[fieldKey] = value;
      });
      
      appointment.rowIndex = rowIndex;
      appointment.id = rowIndex - 1;
      
      console.log('Found appointment data:', appointment);
      return appointment;
    } else {
      console.error('Invalid appointment ID:', appointmentId);
      return null;
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error getting appointment data:', error);
    return null;
  }
}

/**
 * Get or create spreadsheet
 * 
 * IMPORTANT: This function now uses the SPREADSHEET_ID from the config.js file
 * to ensure it always accesses the correct spreadsheet, regardless of which
 * Google account is running the script.
 * 
 * To set up:
 * 1. Create a spreadsheet in the desired Google account (theanuragsharma.web@gmail.com)
 * 2. Share it with the account that will run this script (with Editor permissions)
 * 3. Copy the spreadsheet ID from the URL
 * 4. Add it to the CONFIG object below as SPREADSHEET_ID
 */
function getOrCreateSpreadsheet() {
  try {
    // CRITICAL FIX: Use the specific spreadsheet ID instead of searching by name
    // This ensures the script always uses the correct spreadsheet regardless of
    // which Google account is currently logged in
    const SPREADSHEET_ID = '1M0AdgnK2B71XOMw_I6L7eCV6mY9hv9trfno5PheTFOg';
    
    try {
      // Try to open the spreadsheet by ID
      const spreadsheet = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
      console.log('Successfully opened spreadsheet by ID:', SPREADSHEET_ID);
      return spreadsheet;
    } catch (error) {
      // If opening by ID fails, the spreadsheet might not exist or user doesn't have access
      console.error('Cannot access spreadsheet with ID:', SPREADSHEET_ID);
      console.error('Error details:', error.toString());
      
      // Provide helpful error message
      throw new Error(
        'Cannot access the specified spreadsheet. ' +
        'Please ensure: ' +
        '1) The spreadsheet ID is correct, ' +
        '2) The spreadsheet exists, ' +
        '3) This script\'s Google account has been granted Editor access to the spreadsheet. ' +
        'Original error: ' + error.toString()
      );
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error getting spreadsheet:', error);
    throw error;
  }
}
