/**
 * Find row index by Session ID
 * Since appointmentId is now a Session ID (e.g., "GIS-2025-001"), we need to find the row where this ID exists
 */
/**
 * Debug function to check Session ID column status
 * Can be called from admin dashboard to verify Session ID setup
 */
function debugSessionIdColumn() {
  try {
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = spreadsheet.getActiveSheet();
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    
    if (data.length <= 1) {
      return createCORSResponse({
        status: 'error',
        message: 'No data found in spreadsheet'
      });
    }
    
    const headers = data[0];
    const sessionIdColumnIndex = headers.indexOf('Session ID');
    
    const debugInfo = {
      status: 'success',
      sessionIdColumnExists: sessionIdColumnIndex !== -1,
      sessionIdColumnIndex: sessionIdColumnIndex,
      totalRows: data.length,
      headers: headers,
      sampleSessionIds: []
    };
    
    // Get sample Session IDs from first few rows
    if (sessionIdColumnIndex !== -1) {
      for (let i = 1; i < Math.min(6, data.length); i++) {
        debugInfo.sampleSessionIds.push({
          row: i + 1,
          sessionId: data[i][sessionIdColumnIndex] || 'EMPTY',
          rowData: data[i].slice(0, 5) // First 5 columns for context
        });
      }
    }
    
    return createCORSResponse(debugInfo);
  } catch (error) {
    return createCORSResponse({
      status: 'error',
      message: error.toString()
    });
  }
}

/**
 * Helper function to get proper appointment ID (Session ID) from appointment object
 * This ensures consistent Session ID handling across all functions
 * 
 * UPDATED FUNCTIONS TO USE THIS HELPER:
 * - handleApproveAction
 * - handleMarkSessionDoneAction  
 * - handleQueryResolvedAction
 * - sendNewApprovalEmail
 * - sendQueryResolutionEmail
 * - sendRescheduleEmail
 * - sendPaymentEmail
 * - sendConsentEmail
 * - sendSessionCompletionEmail
 * - sendPaymentProofNotificationEmail
 * 
 * UPDATED PAYMENT PROOF HANDLING:
 * - handlePaymentProofUpload function now uses getAppointmentId() for proper file naming
 * - updatePaymentProofLink function now uses findRowIndexBySessionId() for proper lookup
 * - File names now follow format: GIS-YYYY-XXX_ClientName_OriginalFileName.ext
 * 
 * UPDATED FRONTEND:
 * - performAction function in admin-dashboard.js now constructs proper Session IDs
 */
function getAppointmentId(appointment) {
  // First try to get the actual Session ID
  let appointmentId = appointment.sessionId || appointment['Session ID'];
  
  // If no Session ID, construct it from rowIndex
  if (!appointmentId && appointment.rowIndex) {
    const currentYear = new Date().getFullYear();
    const sequenceNumber = appointment.rowIndex - 1; // rowIndex is 1-based, sequence is 0-based
    appointmentId = `GIS-${currentYear}-${String(sequenceNumber).padStart(3, '0')}`;
    console.log('Constructed Session ID from rowIndex:', appointmentId);
  }
  
  // Final fallback to rowIndex if Session ID construction fails
  appointmentId = appointmentId || appointment.rowIndex || appointment.id;
  
  return appointmentId;
}

function findRowIndexBySessionId(sessionId) {
  try {
    console.log('findRowIndexBySessionId called with:', sessionId);
    
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = spreadsheet.getActiveSheet();
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    
    if (data.length <= 1) {
      console.log('No data found in spreadsheet');
      return -1;
    }
    
    const headers = data[0];
    const sessionIdColumnIndex = headers.indexOf('Session ID');
    
    // First, try to find by actual Session ID if the column exists
    if (sessionIdColumnIndex !== -1) {
      // Search for the session ID in the Session ID column
      for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) { // Start from row 1 (data rows)
        const rowSessionId = data[i][sessionIdColumnIndex];
        if (rowSessionId && rowSessionId.toString().trim() === sessionId.toString().trim()) {
          console.log('Found session ID at row index:', i + 1); // +1 because sheet rows are 1-indexed
          return i + 1; // Return 1-based row index
        }
      }
    }
    
    // Fallback: If sessionId is numeric, treat it as a row index (legacy support)
    const numericId = parseInt(sessionId);
    if (!isNaN(numericId) && numericId > 0 && numericId <= data.length - 1) {
      console.log('Using numeric ID as row index (legacy fallback):', numericId + 1);
      return numericId + 1; // Convert 0-based to 1-based row index
    }
    
    // Additional fallback: Check if the sessionId looks like "GIS-YYYY-XXX" format
    // and try to extract the sequence number to use as row index
    const sessionIdMatch = sessionId.toString().match(/^GIS-\d{4}-(\d{3})$/);
    if (sessionIdMatch) {
      const sequenceNum = parseInt(sessionIdMatch[1]);
      const estimatedRowIndex = sequenceNum + 2; // +1 for 0-based to 1-based, +1 for header row
      if (estimatedRowIndex > 1 && estimatedRowIndex <= data.length) {
        console.log('Using Session ID sequence number as row index:', estimatedRowIndex);
        return estimatedRowIndex;
      }
    }
    
    console.log('Session ID not found in spreadsheet and no valid fallback available');
    return -1;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error finding row by session ID:', error);
    return -1;
  }
}

/**
 * Handle form submissions
 */
function handleFormSubmission(formData) {
  try {
    console.log('=== FORM SUBMISSION DEBUG ===');
    console.log('Processing form submission');
    console.log('reschedule-mode value:', formData['reschedule-mode']);
    console.log('original-session-id value:', formData['original-session-id']);
    console.log('Full formData keys:', Object.keys(formData).join(', '));
    console.log('============================');
    
    // Check if this is a reschedule submission
    const isReschedule = formData['reschedule-mode'] === 'true';
    const originalSessionId = formData['original-session-id'];
    
    console.log('Is reschedule?', isReschedule);
    console.log('Has originalSessionId?', !!originalSessionId);
    
    if (isReschedule && originalSessionId) {
      console.log('ROUTING TO RESCHEDULE HANDLER');
      return handleRescheduleSubmission(formData, originalSessionId);
    }
    
    console.log('PROCESSING AS NEW SUBMISSION');
    
    const requiredFields = ['name', 'email', 'country-code', 'phone', 'organization'];
    const missingFields = requiredFields.filter(field => 
      !formData[field] || formData[field].trim() === ''
    );
    
    if (missingFields.length > 0) {
      console.log('Missing required form fields:', missingFields);
      return createCORSResponse({ 
        status: 'error', 
        message: `Missing required fields: ${missingFields.join(', ')}` 
      });
    }
    
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = spreadsheet.getActiveSheet();
    
    const headers = [
      'Time Stamp *', 'Session ID', 'Full Name *', 'Email Address *', 'Country Code *', 'Phone Number *',
      'Organization *', 'Designation *', 'Region *', 'Other Region *', 'Category *',
      'Type of Session *', 'Domain(s) *', 'Other Domain *', 'Region(s) *', 'Other Region(s) *', 'What do you want to talk about? *',
      'What specific area of space policy interests you most?', 'Are you looking for general guidance or specific insights? *',
      'If Specific insights, Details', 'Is there any policy directive you are concerned with? *',
      'If Yes, Policy Directive Details', 'Is there any specific Geopolitical development/ situation you are concerned with? *',
      'If Yes, Geopolitical Development/Situation Details', 'Is there any particular "Use Case" related to your work profile/project you are concerned with? *',
      'If Yes, Use Case Details', 'Is there any other specific information you would like to discuss before the consultancy session to make the session more personalized? *',
      'If Yes, Additional Information Details', 'Is there any specific Entity you are already dealing with? *',
      'If Yes, Entity Details', 'What level of detail are you expecting from this consultation? *',
      'What are your primary strategic objectives for this engagement? *', 'Which specific outcomes are you hoping to achieve over the 2-6 month period? *',
      'What is your preferred engagement model (weekly/bi-weekly consultations)? *', 'Do you need deliverables like reports, frameworks, or policy recommendations? *',
      'What complex challenges or strategic decisions are you currently facing? *', 'Which regional dynamics are most relevant to your current situation? *',
      'Are you looking for comprehensive analysis or strategic planning assistance? *', 'Do you need customized frameworks or policy recommendations? *',
      'Selected Date', 'Selected Time', 'Selected Slot', 'Selected Timezone', 'Additional Notes', 'Data Consent', 'Terms Consent',
      'Status', 'Admin Notes', 'Last Updated', 'Client Status', 'Client Query', 'Payment Proof Link', 'Reschedule History', 'Query History', 'User Query Documents', 'Admin Query Documents'
    ];    
    setupHeaders(sheet, headers);
    const rowData = prepareRowData(formData, headers);
    
    // Use getRange().setValues() instead of appendRow() to prevent formula interpretation
    const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
    const newRowIndex = lastRow + 1;
    const range = sheet.getRange(newRowIndex, 1, 1, rowData.length);
    
    // Set the values as text to prevent formula interpretation
    range.setValues([rowData]);
    
    // Format the country code column specifically as text if it exists
    const countryCodeColumnIndex = headers.indexOf('Country Code *') + 1;
    if (countryCodeColumnIndex > 0) {
      const countryCodeRange = sheet.getRange(newRowIndex, countryCodeColumnIndex, 1, 1);
      countryCodeRange.setNumberFormat('@'); // @ format means text
    }
    
    // Booked sessions recording removed due to timezone complications
    
    sendOwnerNotification(formData);
    
    console.log('Form submission processed successfully');
    
    return createCORSResponse({ 
      status: 'success', 
      message: 'Form submitted successfully! You will receive a confirmation email shortly.' 
    });
      
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error processing form submission:', error);
    return createCORSResponse({ 
      status: 'error', 
      message: 'Error submitting form: ' + error.toString() 
    });
  }
}

/**
 * Handle reschedule form submission - updates existing row with new date/time
 */
function handleRescheduleSubmission(formData, originalSessionId) {
  try {
    console.log('=== RESCHEDULE SUBMISSION DEBUG ===');
    console.log('Original Session ID:', originalSessionId);
    console.log('Full formData object:', JSON.stringify(formData));
    console.log('selected-date:', formData['selected-date']);
    console.log('selected-time:', formData['selected-time']);
    console.log('selected-slot:', formData['selected-slot']);
    console.log('advisory-selected-date:', formData['advisory-selected-date']);
    console.log('advisory-selected-time:', formData['advisory-selected-time']);
    console.log('===================================');
    
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = spreadsheet.getActiveSheet();
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const headers = data[0];
    
    // Find column indices
    const sessionIdColIndex = headers.indexOf('Session ID');
    const selectedDateColIndex = headers.indexOf('Selected Date');
    const selectedTimeColIndex = headers.indexOf('Selected Time');
    const selectedSlotColIndex = headers.indexOf('Selected Slot');
    const selectedTimezoneColIndex = headers.indexOf('Selected Timezone');
    const statusColIndex = headers.indexOf('Status');
    const clientStatusColIndex = headers.indexOf('Client Status');
    const lastUpdatedColIndex = headers.indexOf('Last Updated');
    const rescheduleHistoryColIndex = headers.indexOf('Reschedule History');
    
    if (sessionIdColIndex === -1) {
      console.error('Session ID column not found');
      return createCORSResponse({ 
        status: 'error', 
        message: 'Session ID column not found in spreadsheet' 
      });
    }
    
    // Find the row with the original session ID
    let targetRowIndex = -1;
    let oldDate = '';
    let oldTime = '';
    let oldSlot = '';
    let clientEmail = '';
    let clientName = '';
    
    for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (data[i][sessionIdColIndex] === originalSessionId) {
        targetRowIndex = i + 1; // +1 because sheet rows are 1-indexed
        oldDate = data[i][selectedDateColIndex] || '';
        oldTime = data[i][selectedTimeColIndex] || '';
        oldSlot = data[i][selectedSlotColIndex] || '';
        
        // Get client info for notifications
        const emailColIndex = headers.indexOf('Email Address *');
        const nameColIndex = headers.indexOf('Full Name *');
        if (emailColIndex !== -1) clientEmail = data[i][emailColIndex];
        if (nameColIndex !== -1) clientName = data[i][nameColIndex];
        break;
      }
    }
    
    if (targetRowIndex === -1) {
      console.error('Session not found:', originalSessionId);
      return createCORSResponse({ 
        status: 'error', 
        message: 'Original session not found: ' + originalSessionId 
      });
    }
    
    console.log('Found session at row:', targetRowIndex);
    console.log('Old date/time:', oldDate, oldTime);
    
    // Prepare new values
    const newDate = formData['selected-date'] || formData['advisory-selected-date'] || '';
    const newTime = formData['selected-time'] || formData['advisory-selected-time'] || '';
    const newSlot = formData['selected-slot'] || '';
    const newTimezone = formData['timezone-selector'] || '';
    const timestamp = new Date().toISOString();
    
    // Update the row
    if (selectedDateColIndex !== -1 && newDate) {
      sheet.getRange(targetRowIndex, selectedDateColIndex + 1).setValue(newDate);
    }
    if (selectedTimeColIndex !== -1 && newTime) {
      sheet.getRange(targetRowIndex, selectedTimeColIndex + 1).setValue(newTime);
    }
    if (selectedSlotColIndex !== -1 && newSlot) {
      sheet.getRange(targetRowIndex, selectedSlotColIndex + 1).setValue(newSlot);
    }
    if (selectedTimezoneColIndex !== -1 && newTimezone) {
      sheet.getRange(targetRowIndex, selectedTimezoneColIndex + 1).setValue(newTimezone);
    }
    
    // Update Status to "Rescheduled" to indicate the session has been rescheduled
    if (statusColIndex !== -1) {
      sheet.getRange(targetRowIndex, statusColIndex + 1).setValue('Rescheduled');
    }
    
    // Update Client Status to "Rescheduled" (matching previous implementation)
    if (clientStatusColIndex !== -1) {
      sheet.getRange(targetRowIndex, clientStatusColIndex + 1).setValue('Rescheduled');
    }
    
    // Update Last Updated timestamp
    if (lastUpdatedColIndex !== -1) {
      sheet.getRange(targetRowIndex, lastUpdatedColIndex + 1).setValue(timestamp);
    }
    
    // Add to Reschedule History
    if (rescheduleHistoryColIndex !== -1) {
      const existingHistory = sheet.getRange(targetRowIndex, rescheduleHistoryColIndex + 1).getValue() || '';
      // Format timestamp for history
      const historyTimestamp = new Date().toLocaleString('en-IN', { 
        day: '2-digit', month: 'short', year: 'numeric', 
        hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit', hour12: true 
      });
      // Format old and new dates/times for history
      const formatForHistory = (dateStr, timeStr) => {
        let result = '';
        if (dateStr) {
          try {
            const d = new Date(dateStr);
            if (!isNaN(d.getTime())) {
              result = d.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { weekday: 'short', month: 'short', day: 'numeric', year: 'numeric' });
            } else {
              result = String(dateStr);
            }
          } catch (e) { result = String(dateStr); }
        }
        if (timeStr) {
          const timeString = String(timeStr);
          if (timeString.includes(':')) {
            const parts = timeString.split(':');
            if (parts.length >= 2) {
              let hours = parseInt(parts[0]);
              const minutes = parts[1];
              const ampm = hours >= 12 ? 'PM' : 'AM';
              hours = hours % 12 || 12;
              result += ` ${hours}:${minutes} ${ampm}`;
            } else {
              result += ` ${timeString}`;
            }
          } else {
            result += ` ${timeString}`;
          }
        }
        return result || 'Not specified';
      };
      const oldFormatted = formatForHistory(oldDate, oldTime);
      const newFormatted = formatForHistory(newDate, newTime);
      const historyEntry = `${historyTimestamp}: Client rescheduled from ${oldFormatted} to ${newFormatted}`;
      const newHistory = existingHistory ? existingHistory + '\n' + historyEntry : historyEntry;
      sheet.getRange(targetRowIndex, rescheduleHistoryColIndex + 1).setValue(newHistory);
    }
    
    console.log('Session updated successfully');
    
    // Send notification emails
    sendRescheduleNotifications(originalSessionId, clientName, clientEmail, oldDate, oldTime, oldSlot, newDate, newTime, newSlot);
    
    return createCORSResponse({ 
      status: 'success', 
      message: 'Session rescheduled successfully! You and the admin will receive confirmation emails.' 
    });
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error processing reschedule submission:', error);
    return createCORSResponse({ 
      status: 'error', 
      message: 'Error rescheduling session: ' + error.toString() 
    });
  }
}

/**
 * Send notification emails for reschedule
 */
function sendRescheduleNotifications(sessionId, clientName, clientEmail, oldDate, oldTime, oldSlot, newDate, newTime, newSlot) {
  try {
    const adminEmail = CONFIG.OWNER_EMAIL;

    const extractTimezoneFromSlot = (slotValue) => {
      if (!slotValue) return '';
      const match = String(slotValue).trim().match(/\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}\s+\d{2}:\d{2}(?::\d{2})?\s+(.+)$/);
      return match ? match[1].trim() : '';
    };

    const oldTimezone = extractTimezoneFromSlot(oldSlot);
    const newTimezone = extractTimezoneFromSlot(newSlot);
    
    // Format dates for display
    const formatDateDisplay = (dateStr) => {
      if (!dateStr) return 'Not specified';
      try {
        // If it's already a formatted date string like "2026-01-30", parse it
        const date = new Date(dateStr);
        if (isNaN(date.getTime())) return dateStr;
        return date.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { weekday: 'short', year: 'numeric', month: 'short', day: 'numeric' });
      } catch (e) {
        return dateStr;
      }
    };
    
    const formatTimeDisplay = (timeStr, timezoneLabel = '') => {
      if (!timeStr) return 'Not specified';
      try {
        // Convert to string if it's not already
        const timeString = String(timeStr);
        // Handle time strings like "18:00:00" or "16:00:00"
        if (timeString.includes(':')) {
          const parts = timeString.split(':');
          if (parts.length >= 2) {
            let hours = parseInt(parts[0]);
            const minutes = parts[1];
            const ampm = hours >= 12 ? 'PM' : 'AM';
            hours = hours % 12 || 12;
            return `${hours}:${minutes} ${ampm}${timezoneLabel ? ' ' + timezoneLabel : ''}`;
          }
        }
        return timeString;
      } catch (e) {
        return String(timeStr);
      }
    };
    
    const oldDateFormatted = formatDateDisplay(oldDate);
    const oldTimeFormatted = formatTimeDisplay(oldTime, oldTimezone);
    const newDateFormatted = formatDateDisplay(newDate);
    const newTimeFormatted = formatTimeDisplay(newTime, newTimezone);
    
    // Email to Admin
    const adminSubject = `Session Rescheduled: ${sessionId}`;
    const adminBody = `
A session has been rescheduled by the client.

Session ID: ${sessionId}
Client Name: ${clientName}
Client Email: ${clientEmail}

Previous Schedule:
Date: ${oldDateFormatted}
Time: ${oldTimeFormatted}

New Schedule:
Date: ${newDateFormatted}
Time: ${newTimeFormatted}

Please review and update your calendar accordingly.

This is an automated notification from the GIS Booking System.
    `.trim();
    
    MailApp.sendEmail({
      to: adminEmail,
      subject: adminSubject,
      body: adminBody
    });
    console.log('Admin notification email sent for reschedule');
    
    // Email to Client
    if (clientEmail) {
      const clientSubject = `Your Session Has Been Rescheduled - ${sessionId}`;
      const clientBody = `
Dear ${clientName},

Your session has been successfully rescheduled.

Session ID: ${sessionId}

Previous Schedule:
Date: ${oldDateFormatted}
Time: ${oldTimeFormatted}

New Schedule:
Date: ${newDateFormatted}
Time: ${newTimeFormatted}

If you have any questions, please contact us.

Best regards,
${CONFIG.FROM_NAME}
📧 ${CONFIG.OWNER_EMAIL}
      `.trim();
      
      MailApp.sendEmail({
        to: clientEmail,
        subject: clientSubject,
        body: clientBody
      });
      console.log('Client notification email sent for reschedule');
    }
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error sending reschedule notification emails:', error);
  }
}

/**
 * Setup spreadsheet headers
 */
function setupHeaders(sheet, headers) {
  try {
    const existingData = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    
    // Check if headers need to be added
    // New spreadsheet: existingData.length === 0 or first row is empty
    const needsHeaders = existingData.length === 0 || 
                        (existingData.length === 1 && existingData[0].every(cell => cell === '')) ||
                        existingData[0].length === 0 ||
                        !existingData[0].includes('Time Stamp *');
    
    if (needsHeaders) {
      // Clear existing content and add headers for completely new spreadsheet
      sheet.clear();
      sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length).setValues([headers]);
      
      const headerRange = sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length);
      headerRange.setFontWeight('bold');
      headerRange.setBackground('#4285f4');
      headerRange.setFontColor('white');
      sheet.setFrozenRows(1);
      
      console.log('New headers setup completed with', headers.length, 'columns');
    } else {
      // SIMPLE: Just check if Session ID column is missing and add it
      const existingHeaders = existingData[0];
      
      if (!existingHeaders.includes('Session ID')) {
        console.log('Adding Session ID column to existing spreadsheet...');
        
        // Insert Session ID column at position 2 (after Time Stamp)
        sheet.insertColumnAfter(1);
        
        // Set the Session ID header
        const sessionIdCell = sheet.getRange(1, 2);
        sessionIdCell.setValue('Session ID');
        sessionIdCell.setFontWeight('bold');
        sessionIdCell.setBackground('#4285f4');
        sessionIdCell.setFontColor('white');
        
        // Add Session IDs to existing rows
        const dataRows = existingData.length - 1;
        if (dataRows > 0) {
          const currentYear = new Date().getFullYear();
          for (let i = 2; i <= dataRows + 1; i++) {
            const sessionId = `GIS-${currentYear}-${String(i - 1).padStart(3, '0')}`;
            sheet.getRange(i, 2).setValue(sessionId);
          }
          console.log(`Added Session IDs to ${dataRows} existing rows`);
        }
      }

      // Add Selected Timezone column if it is missing
      if (!existingHeaders.includes('Selected Timezone')) {
        console.log('Adding Selected Timezone column to existing spreadsheet...');

        const currentHeaders = sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
        const selectedSlotHeaderIndex = currentHeaders.indexOf('Selected Slot');

        if (selectedSlotHeaderIndex !== -1) {
          sheet.insertColumnAfter(selectedSlotHeaderIndex + 1);
          const timezoneCell = sheet.getRange(1, selectedSlotHeaderIndex + 2);
          timezoneCell.setValue('Selected Timezone');
          timezoneCell.setFontWeight('bold');
          timezoneCell.setBackground('#4285f4');
          timezoneCell.setFontColor('white');
        } else {
          const newCol = sheet.getLastColumn() + 1;
          const timezoneCell = sheet.getRange(1, newCol);
          timezoneCell.setValue('Selected Timezone');
          timezoneCell.setFontWeight('bold');
          timezoneCell.setBackground('#4285f4');
          timezoneCell.setFontColor('white');
        }
      }
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error setting up headers:', error);
    throw error;
  }
}

/**
 * Generate Session ID for existing rows (with sequence number)
 */
function generateSessionIdForRow(sequenceNumber) {
  const currentYear = new Date().getFullYear();
  const sessionId = `GIS-${currentYear}-${String(sequenceNumber).padStart(3, '0')}`;
  console.log('Generated Session ID for existing row:', sessionId);
  return sessionId;
}

/**
 * Manually add Session ID column to existing spreadsheet
 * Call this function once to update existing spreadsheets
 */
function addSessionIdColumnToExistingSpreadsheet() {
  try {
    console.log('Starting manual Session ID column addition...');
    
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = spreadsheet.getActiveSheet();
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    
    if (data.length === 0) {
      console.log('No data in spreadsheet');
      return { status: 'success', message: 'No data in spreadsheet' };
    }
    
    const existingHeaders = data[0];
    console.log('Existing headers:', existingHeaders);
    
    // Check if Session ID column already exists
    if (existingHeaders.includes('Session ID')) {
      console.log('Session ID column already exists');
      return { status: 'success', message: 'Session ID column already exists' };
    }
    
    // Insert Session ID column at position 2 (after Time Stamp)
    sheet.insertColumnAfter(1); // Insert after column A (Time Stamp)
    
    // Set the Session ID header
    const sessionIdCell = sheet.getRange(1, 2);
    sessionIdCell.setValue('Session ID');
    sessionIdCell.setFontWeight('bold');
    sessionIdCell.setBackground('#4285f4');
    sessionIdCell.setFontColor('white');
    
    // Generate Session IDs for existing rows
    const dataRows = data.length - 1; // Exclude header row
    if (dataRows > 0) {
      console.log('Generating Session IDs for', dataRows, 'existing rows');
      
      for (let i = 2; i <= dataRows + 1; i++) { // Start from row 2 (after header)
        const sessionId = generateSessionIdForRow(i - 1); // i-1 because we want sequence based on row position
        sheet.getRange(i, 2).setValue(sessionId);
      }
    }
    
    console.log('Session ID column added successfully to existing spreadsheet');
    return { 
      status: 'success', 
      message: `Session ID column added successfully. Generated ${dataRows} Session IDs.` 
    };
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error adding Session ID column:', error);
    return { status: 'error', message: error.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Prepare row data for insertion
 */
function prepareRowData(formData, headers) {
  const rowData = [];
  
  console.log('Form data received:', JSON.stringify(formData, null, 2));
  console.log('Headers:', headers);
  
  // Display text mappings for specific fields
  const displayTextMappings = {
    'guidance-type': {
      'general': 'General',
      'specific': 'Specific'
    },
    'policy-directive': {
      'yes': 'Yes',
      'no': 'No'
    },
    'geopolitical-situation': {
      'yes': 'Yes',
      'no': 'No'
    },
    'use-case': {
      'yes': 'Yes',
      'no': 'No'
    },
    'additional-info': {
      'yes': 'Yes',
      'no': 'No'
    },
    'specific-entity': {
      'yes': 'Yes',
      'no': 'No'
    }
  };
  
  headers.forEach(header => {
    const fieldKey = getFieldKey(header);
    console.log(`Header: "${header}" -> Field Key: "${fieldKey}"`);
    
    let value = '';
    
    if (header === 'Time Stamp *') {
      value = new Date().toString();
    } else if (header === 'Session ID') {
      value = generateSessionId();
    } else if (header === 'Status') {
      value = 'Pending';
    } else if (header === 'Client Status') {
      value = 'Pending';
    } else if (header === 'Last Updated') {
      value = new Date().toString();
    } else if (header === 'Selected Date') {
      // Handle both regular and advisory date fields
      value = formData['selected-date'] || formData['advisory-selected-date'] || '';
    } else if (header === 'Selected Time') {
      // Handle both regular and advisory time fields
      value = formData['selected-time'] || formData['advisory-selected-time'] || '';
    } else if (header === 'Selected Slot') {
      // Handle both regular and advisory slot fields
      value = formData['selected-slot'] || formData['advisory-datetime'] || '';
    } else if (header === 'Selected Timezone') {
      value = formData['timezone-selector'] || '';
    } else {
      // CRITICAL FIX: Try to get value using multiple possible field name variations
      // 1. Try the exact fieldKey first (from getFieldKey mapping)
      value = formData[fieldKey] || '';
      
      // 2. Special handling for "Other Domain" and "Other Region" fields
      // These have alternative field names that need to be checked
      if (!value && header === 'Other Domain *') {
        value = formData['custom-domain-input'] || formData['others-domain-input'] || '';
      }
      if (!value && header === 'Other Region(s) *') {
        value = formData['custom-region-domain-input'] || formData['others-region-input'] || '';
      }
      
      // 3. Special handling for "What do you want to talk about?" field
      // This field appears in different contexts and might have different IDs
      // For consultancy (generalized, super-specialized, long-term): uses 'dynamic-topic'
      // For advisory: uses 'topic'
      if (!value && header === 'What do you want to talk about? *') {
        value = formData['dynamic-topic'] || formData['topic'] || '';
        console.log('Topic field lookup - dynamic-topic:', formData['dynamic-topic'], 'topic:', formData['topic'], 'final value:', value);
      }
      
      // 4. If not found, try using the header name directly (removing asterisks)
      if (!value && header) {
        const headerWithoutAsterisk = header.replace(/\s*\*\s*/g, '').trim();
        value = formData[headerWithoutAsterisk] || '';
      }
      
      // 5. Try common form field name patterns based on the header text
      if (!value && header) {
        // Create kebab-case version of header for matching
        const kebabCase = header
          .replace(/\s*\*\s*/g, '') // Remove asterisks
          .toLowerCase()
          .replace(/[()]/g, '') // Remove parentheses
          .replace(/\s+/g, '-') // Replace spaces with dashes
          .replace(/[^a-z0-9-]/g, '') // Remove special chars except dashes
          .replace(/-+/g, '-'); // Normalize multiple dashes
        
        value = formData[kebabCase] || '';
        
        // Log for debugging
        if (value) {
          console.log(`Found value using kebab-case: "${kebabCase}" = "${value}"`);
        }
      }
      
      // Apply display text mapping if exists
      if (displayTextMappings[fieldKey] && displayTextMappings[fieldKey][value]) {
        value = displayTextMappings[fieldKey][value];
      }
      
      // Special handling for country code to prevent formula parse error
      if (fieldKey === 'country-code' && value && value.startsWith('+')) {
        // Prepend with apostrophe to force text interpretation in Google Sheets
        value = "'" + value;
      }
    }
    
    console.log(`Final value for "${header}": "${value}"`);
    rowData.push(value);
  });
  
  console.log('Prepared row data:', rowData);
  return rowData;
}

/**
 * Send owner notification
 */
function sendOwnerNotification(formData) {
  try {
    const requiredFields = ['name', 'email', 'country-code', 'phone', 'organization'];
    const hasAllFields = requiredFields.every(field => 
      formData[field] && formData[field].trim() !== ''
    );
    
    if (!hasAllFields) {
      console.log('SKIPPING owner notification - not a valid form submission');
      return;
    }
    
    const subject = `New Appointment Request - ${formData.name}`;
    const body = `
<h2>New Appointment Request</h2>
<p><strong>Client:</strong> ${formData.name}</p>
<p><strong>Email:</strong> ${formData.email}</p>
<p><strong>Country Code:</strong> ${formData['country-code']}</p>
<p><strong>Phone:</strong> ${formData.phone}</p>
<p><strong>Organization:</strong> ${formData.organization}</p>
<p><strong>Session Type:</strong> ${formData['session-type'] || 'Not specified'}</p>

<p><a href="http://theanuragsharma.com/admin-login.html" style="background: #007bff; color: white; padding: 10px 20px; text-decoration: none; border-radius: 5px;">Manage Appointments</a></p>
    `;
    
    MailApp.sendEmail({
      to: CONFIG.OWNER_EMAIL,
      subject: subject,
      htmlBody: body
    });
    
    console.log('Owner notification sent successfully');
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error sending owner notification:', error);
  }
}

/**
 * Handle admin actions
 */
function handleAdminAction(data) {
  try {
    if (typeof data === 'object' && data.action === 'getAppointments') {
      return getAppointments();
    }
    
    // Handle special utility actions that don't require appointment data
    if (data.action === 'addSessionIdColumn') {
      console.log('Processing addSessionIdColumn action');
      const result = addSessionIdColumnToExistingSpreadsheet();
      return createCORSResponse(result);
    }
    
    // Handle user management actions
    if (data.action === 'getUsersAndRoles') {
      console.log('Processing getUsersAndRoles action');
      return getUsersAndRoles();
    }
    
    if (data.action === 'addUser') {
      console.log('Processing addUser action');
      const userData = {
        name: data.name,
        email: data.email,
        password: data.password,
        role: data.role
      };
      return addUser(userData);
    }
    
    if (data.action === 'deleteUser') {
      console.log('Processing deleteUser action');
      return deleteUser(data.userId);
    }
    
    if (data.action === 'updateUserLastLogin') {
      console.log('Processing updateUserLastLogin action');
      updateUserLastLogin(data.email);
      return createCORSResponse({
        status: 'success',
        message: 'Last login updated'
      });
    }
    
    if (data.action === 'changeUserPassword') {
      console.log('Processing changeUserPassword action');
      return changeUserPassword(data.userId, data.newPassword, data.changedByEmail);
    }
    
    let action, appointmentId, appointment, actionData;
    
    if (data.action && data.appointmentId) {
      action = data.action;
      appointmentId = data.appointmentId;
      
      console.log('Received admin action request:', {
        action: action,
        appointmentId: appointmentId,
        appointmentIdType: typeof appointmentId,
        isNumeric: !isNaN(appointmentId),
        isSessionIdFormat: /^GIS-\d{4}-\d{3}$/.test(appointmentId)
      });
      
      try {
        appointment = JSON.parse(data.appointment);
        actionData = JSON.parse(data.actionData);
        
        console.log('🔍 Parsed actionData for action:', action);
        console.log('ActionData contents:', actionData);
        console.log('ActionData keys:', Object.keys(actionData));
        
        if (action === 'initiateRefund') {
          console.log('🔍 Refund-specific actionData analysis:', {
            hasNotes: 'notes' in actionData,
            hasRefundProofDocument: 'refundProofDocument' in actionData,
            hasRefundProofName: 'refundProofName' in actionData,
            hasRefundProofType: 'refundProofType' in actionData,
            notes: actionData.notes,
            refundProofName: actionData.refundProofName,
            refundProofType: actionData.refundProofType,
            documentLength: actionData.refundProofDocument ? actionData.refundProofDocument.length : 0,
            allActionDataKeys: Object.keys(actionData)
          });
          
          // Log raw actionData for debugging
          console.log('🔍 Raw actionData for refund:', JSON.stringify(actionData).substring(0, 500) + '...');
        }
      } catch (parseError) {
        console.error('Error parsing admin action data:', parseError);
        return createCORSResponse({ 
          status: 'error', 
          message: 'Invalid admin action data format' 
        });
      }
    } else {
      action = data.action;
      appointmentId = data.appointmentId;
      appointment = data.appointment;
      actionData = data.data;
    }
    
    console.log(`Processing admin action: ${action} for appointment ID: ${appointmentId}`);
    
    if (!action || !appointmentId || !appointment) {
      return createCORSResponse({ 
        status: 'error', 
        message: 'Missing required fields for admin action' 
      });
    }
    
    try {
      switch (action) {
        case 'approve':
          handleApproveAction(appointment, actionData);
          break;
        case 'reject':
          handleRejectAction(appointment, actionData);
          break;
        case 'reschedule':
          handleRescheduleAction(appointment, actionData);
          break;
        case 'rescheduleWithCalendar':
          handleRescheduleWithCalendarAction(appointment, actionData);
          break;
        case 'cancel':
          handleCancelAction(appointment, actionData);
          break;
        case 'payment':
          handlePaymentAction(appointment, actionData);
          break;
        case 'paymentAcknowledgement':
          handlePaymentAcknowledgementAction(appointment, actionData);
          break;
        case 'sendConsent':
          handleSendConsentAction(appointment, actionData);
          break;
        case 'sendSessionReminder':
          handleSendSessionReminderAction(appointment, actionData);
          break;
        case 'sendFeedbackReminder':
          handleSendFeedbackReminderAction(appointment, actionData);
          break;
        case 'markSessionDone':
          handleMarkSessionDoneAction(appointment, actionData);
          // Note: Both main status and client status are updated within handleMarkSessionDoneAction
          break;
        case 'requestRebooking':
          handleRequestRebookingAction(appointment, actionData);
          break;
        case 'queryResolved':
          handleQueryResolvedAction(appointment, actionData);
          break;
        case 'submitClientQuery':
          // Handle client query submission from admin dashboard
          return handleClientQuery({ 
            appointmentId: appointmentId, 
            query: actionData.query || actionData.message, 
            isAdminAction: true 
          });
        case 'initiateRefund':
          // Handle refund initiation from admin dashboard
          return handleRefundInitiation({ 
            appointmentId: appointmentId, 
            refundNotes: actionData.notes || '', 
            refundProofDocument: actionData.refundProofDocument,
            refundProofName: actionData.refundProofName,
            refundProofType: actionData.refundProofType
          });
        default:
          throw new Error('Unknown action: ' + action);
      }
      
      // Update appointment status (skip for actions that handle their own status or have none)
      if (action !== 'markSessionDone' && action !== 'sendFeedbackReminder') {
        updateAppointmentStatus(appointmentId, action, actionData);
      }
      
      return createCORSResponse({ 
        status: 'success', 
        message: `Appointment ${action}d successfully` 
      });
      
    } catch (actionError) {
      console.error(`Error performing ${action} action:`, actionError);
      return createCORSResponse({ 
        status: 'error', 
        message: `Failed to ${action} appointment: ${actionError.message}` 
      });
    }
      
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error handling admin action:', error);
    return createCORSResponse({ 
      status: 'error', 
      message: error.toString() 
    });
  }
}

/**
 * Get all appointments data (returns raw object, not ContentService response)
 * This is used for JSONP callbacks and internal processing
 */
function getAppointmentsData() {
  try {
    // NOTE: Login tracking is now handled by the frontend login page
    // logAdminLogin has been removed from here to avoid duplicate entries
    
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = spreadsheet.getActiveSheet();
    
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const formulas = sheet.getDataRange().getFormulas();
    const displayValues = sheet.getDataRange().getDisplayValues();
    
    if (data.length <= 1) {
      return { status: 'success', appointments: [] };
    }
    
    const headers = data[0];
    const appointments = [];
    
    const paymentProofColIndex = headers.indexOf('Payment Proof Link');
    
    for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
      const row = data[i];
      const formulaRow = formulas[i] || [];
      const displayRow = displayValues[i] || [];
      const appointment = {};
      
      headers.forEach((header, index) => {
        const fieldKey = getFieldKey(header);
        let value = row[index] || '';
        
        if (header === 'Payment Proof Link' && index === paymentProofColIndex) {
          const formula = formulaRow[index] || '';
          const displayValue = displayRow[index] || '';
          if (formula && formula.includes('=HYPERLINK')) {
            value = formula;
          } else if (displayValue && displayValue.trim() !== '') {
            value = displayValue;
          }
        } else if (header === 'Selected Date' || header === 'Selected Time' || header === 'Selected Slot') {
          if (value instanceof Date) {
            if (header === 'Selected Date') {
              value = value.getFullYear() + '-' + 
                     String(value.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0') + '-' + 
                     String(value.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
            } else if (header === 'Selected Time') {
              value = String(value.getHours()).padStart(2, '0') + ':' + 
                     String(value.getMinutes()).padStart(2, '0') + ':' + 
                     String(value.getSeconds()).padStart(2, '0');
            } else if (header === 'Selected Slot') {
              const dateStr = value.getFullYear() + '-' + 
                             String(value.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0') + '-' + 
                             String(value.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
              const timeStr = String(value.getHours()).padStart(2, '0') + ':' + 
                             String(value.getMinutes()).padStart(2, '0') + ':' + 
                             String(value.getSeconds()).padStart(2, '0');
              value = dateStr + ' ' + timeStr;
            }
          }
        } else if (header === 'Time Stamp *') {
          if (value instanceof Date) {
            value = value.toString();
          }
        }
        
        appointment[fieldKey] = value;
      });
      
      appointment.rowIndex = i + 1;
      appointment.id = i;
      appointments.push(appointment);
    }
    
    return { status: 'success', appointments: appointments };
      
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error getting appointments data:', error);
    return { status: 'error', message: error.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Get all appointments
 */
function getAppointments() {
  try {
    // NOTE: Login tracking is now handled by the frontend login page
    // logAdminLogin has been removed from here to avoid duplicate entries
    
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = spreadsheet.getActiveSheet();
    
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const formulas = sheet.getDataRange().getFormulas(); // Get formulas for HYPERLINK handling
    const displayValues = sheet.getDataRange().getDisplayValues(); // Get display values
    
    console.log('Data length:', data.length);
    console.log('Formulas length:', formulas.length);
    console.log('Display values length:', displayValues.length);
    
    if (data.length <= 1) {
      return createCORSResponse({ 
        status: 'success', 
        appointments: [] 
      });
    }
    
    const headers = data[0];
    const appointments = [];
    
    console.log('Headers found:', headers);
    
    // Find Payment Proof Link column index
    const paymentProofColIndex = headers.indexOf('Payment Proof Link');
    console.log('Payment Proof Link column index:', paymentProofColIndex);
    
    for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
      const row = data[i];
      const formulaRow = formulas[i] || [];
      const displayRow = displayValues[i] || [];
      const appointment = {};
      
      headers.forEach((header, index) => {
        const fieldKey = getFieldKey(header);
        let value = row[index] || '';
        
        // Special handling for Payment Proof Link column
        if (header === 'Payment Proof Link' && index === paymentProofColIndex) {
          const formula = formulaRow[index] || '';
          const displayValue = displayRow[index] || '';
          
          console.log(`Row ${i + 1} Payment Proof Link:`, {
            rawValue: value,
            formula: formula,
            displayValue: displayValue
          });
          
          // If there's a HYPERLINK formula, use it
          if (formula && formula.includes('=HYPERLINK')) {
            value = formula;
            console.log(`Using HYPERLINK formula for row ${i + 1}:`, value);
          } 
          // If no formula but there's a display value, use the raw value
          else if (value && value.trim() !== '') {
            console.log(`Using raw value for row ${i + 1}:`, value);
          }
          // If there's a display value but no raw value, the cell might contain a link
          else if (displayValue && displayValue.trim() !== '') {
            console.log(`Using display value for row ${i + 1}:`, displayValue);
            value = displayValue;
          }
        }
        // Special handling for date/time fields to prevent serial date conversion
        else if (header === 'Selected Date' || header === 'Selected Time' || header === 'Selected Slot') {
          if (value instanceof Date) {
            // Convert Date object back to proper format
            if (header === 'Selected Date') {
              value = value.getFullYear() + '-' + 
                     String(value.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0') + '-' + 
                     String(value.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
            } else if (header === 'Selected Time') {
              value = String(value.getHours()).padStart(2, '0') + ':' + 
                     String(value.getMinutes()).padStart(2, '0') + ':' + 
                     String(value.getSeconds()).padStart(2, '0');
            } else if (header === 'Selected Slot') {
              // For Selected Slot, format as "YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS"
              const dateStr = value.getFullYear() + '-' + 
                             String(value.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0') + '-' + 
                             String(value.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
              const timeStr = String(value.getHours()).padStart(2, '0') + ':' + 
                             String(value.getMinutes()).padStart(2, '0') + ':' + 
                             String(value.getSeconds()).padStart(2, '0');
              value = dateStr + ' ' + timeStr;
            }
          }
        } else if (header === 'Time Stamp *') {
          // Handle timestamp field
          if (value instanceof Date) {
            value = value.toString();
          }
        }
        
        appointment[fieldKey] = value;
      });
      
      appointment.rowIndex = i + 1;
      appointment.id = i;
      appointments.push(appointment);
    }
    
    console.log(`Retrieved ${appointments.length} appointments`);
    
    return createCORSResponse({ 
      status: 'success', 
      appointments: appointments 
    });
      
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error getting appointments:', error);
    return createCORSResponse({ 
      status: 'error', 
      message: error.toString() 
    });
  }
}

/**
 * Create CORS-enabled response
 */
function createCORSResponse(data, isText = false) {
  let output;
  
  if (isText) {
    output = ContentService
      .createTextOutput(typeof data === 'string' ? data : JSON.stringify(data))
      .setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.TEXT);
  } else {
    output = ContentService
      .createTextOutput(JSON.stringify(data))
      .setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON);
  }
  
  // Add CORS headers to allow cross-origin requests
  // This is essential for requests from local development servers and deployed websites
  return output;
}

/**
 * Login History Management Functions
 */
function getLoginHistory() {
  try {
    console.log('getLoginHistory called');
    
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    let loginSheet = spreadsheet.getSheetByName('Login History');
    
    // If sheet doesn't exist, create it
    if (!loginSheet) {
      console.log('Creating Login History sheet...');
      loginSheet = spreadsheet.insertSheet('Login History');
      
      // Add headers
      const headers = ['Timestamp', 'Admin User', 'IP Address', 'Browser Info', 'Login Status'];
      loginSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length).setValues([headers]);
      
      // Format headers
      const headerRange = loginSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length);
      headerRange.setFontWeight('bold');
      headerRange.setBackground('#f0f0f0');
      
      console.log('Login History sheet created with headers');
    }
    
    // Get all data from the sheet
    const data = loginSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    
    if (data.length <= 1) {
      return createCORSResponse({
        status: 'success',
        data: [],
        message: 'No login history found'
      });
    }
    
    // Return data (excluding headers)
    const loginData = data.slice(1);
    
    return createCORSResponse({
      status: 'success',
      data: loginData,
      message: 'Login history retrieved successfully'
    });
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error fetching login history:', error);
    return createCORSResponse({
      status: 'error',
      message: error.toString()
    });
  }
}

function logAdminLogin(adminUser = 'Admin', ipAddress = '', browserInfo = '', loginStatus = 'Success') {
  try {
    console.log('Logging admin login:', { adminUser, ipAddress, browserInfo, loginStatus });
    
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    let loginSheet = spreadsheet.getSheetByName('Login History');
    
    // If sheet doesn't exist, create it
    if (!loginSheet) {
      console.log('Creating Login History sheet...');
      loginSheet = spreadsheet.insertSheet('Login History');
      
      // Add headers
      const headers = ['Timestamp', 'Admin User', 'IP Address', 'Browser Info', 'Login Status'];
      loginSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length).setValues([headers]);
      
      // Format headers
      const headerRange = loginSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length);
      headerRange.setFontWeight('bold');
      headerRange.setBackground('#f0f0f0');
      
      console.log('Login History sheet created with headers');
    }
    
    // Add new login entry with IST timezone
    const now = new Date();
    // Force IST timezone (Asia/Kolkata) - UTC+5:30
    const timestamp = Utilities.formatDate(now, "Asia/Kolkata", "yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss");
    console.log('Logging with IST timestamp:', timestamp);
    const newRow = [timestamp, adminUser, ipAddress, browserInfo, loginStatus];
    
    loginSheet.appendRow(newRow);
    
    // Auto-resize columns for better visibility
    try {
      loginSheet.autoResizeColumns(1, 5);
    } catch (resizeError) {
      console.log('Could not auto-resize columns:', resizeError);
    }
    
    console.log('Login entry added successfully');
    return { success: true, message: 'Login logged' };
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error logging admin login:', error);
    return { success: false, message: error.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * User Management Functions
 */
function getUsersAndRoles() {
  try {
    console.log('getUsersAndRoles called');
    
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    let usersSheet = spreadsheet.getSheetByName('Manage Users & Roles');
    
    // If sheet doesn't exist, create it with default users
    if (!usersSheet) {
      console.log('Creating Manage Users & Roles sheet...');
      usersSheet = spreadsheet.insertSheet('Manage Users & Roles');
      
      // Add headers
      const headers = ['User ID', 'Username', 'Email', 'Encrypted Password', 'Role', 'Created At', 'Last Login', 'Password Changed By', 'Password Changed At'];
      usersSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length).setValues([headers]);
      
      // Format headers
      const headerRange = usersSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length);
      headerRange.setFontWeight('bold');
      headerRange.setBackground('#4285f4');
      headerRange.setFontColor('#ffffff');
      
      // Add default users with encrypted passwords
      const defaultUsers = [
        ['USER001', 'Primary Admin', 'ishash2310@gmail.com', Utilities.base64Encode('111'), 'Super Admin', new Date().toISOString(), '', '', '']
      ];
      
      defaultUsers.forEach(user => {
        usersSheet.appendRow(user);
      });
      
      console.log('Manage Users & Roles sheet created with default users');
    }
    
    // Get all data from the sheet
    const data = usersSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    
    if (data.length <= 1) {
      return createCORSResponse({
        status: 'success',
        data: [],
        message: 'No users found'
      });
    }
    
    // Skip header row and return user data (WITHOUT passwords for security)
    const userData = data.slice(1).map(row => {
      const user = {
        id: String(row[0] || '').trim(),
        name: String(row[1] || '').trim(),
        email: String(row[2] || '').trim(),
        // SECURITY: Password field is intentionally excluded from response
        role: String(row[4] || '').trim(),
        createdAt: row[5] || '',
        lastLogin: row[6] || '',
        passwordChangedBy: row[7] || '',
        passwordChangedAt: row[8] || ''
      };
      return user;
    });
    
    return createCORSResponse({
      status: 'success',
      data: userData,
      message: 'Users retrieved successfully'
    });
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error fetching users:', error);
    return createCORSResponse({
      status: 'error',
      message: error.toString()
    });
  }
}

/**
 * SECURE LOGIN VALIDATION
 * Validates admin credentials server-side without exposing passwords to the client
 */
function validateAdminLogin(email, password) {
  try {
    console.log('validateAdminLogin called for email:', email);
    
    // Validate inputs
    if (!email || !password) {
      return createCORSResponse({
        status: 'error',
        authenticated: false,
        message: 'Email and password are required'
      });
    }
    
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    let usersSheet = spreadsheet.getSheetByName('Manage Users & Roles');
    
    // If sheet doesn't exist, no users can login
    if (!usersSheet) {
      console.log('Users sheet not found');
      return createCORSResponse({
        status: 'error',
        authenticated: false,
        message: 'Authentication system not initialized'
      });
    }
    
    // Get all users
    const data = usersSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    
    if (data.length <= 1) {
      console.log('No users found in sheet');
      return createCORSResponse({
        status: 'error',
        authenticated: false,
        message: 'No users found'
      });
    }
    
    // Find user by email (skip header row)
    const userRow = data.slice(1).find(row => {
      const userEmail = String(row[2] || '').trim().toLowerCase();
      return userEmail === email.trim().toLowerCase();
    });
    
    if (!userRow) {
      console.log('User not found:', email);
      return createCORSResponse({
        status: 'error',
        authenticated: false,
        message: 'Invalid email or password'
      });
    }
    
    // Decrypt and validate password
    let storedPassword = String(userRow[3] || '').trim();
    try {
      // Try to decode Base64 encrypted password
      const decoded = Utilities.base64Decode(storedPassword);
      storedPassword = Utilities.newBlob(decoded).getDataAsString();
    } catch (e) {
      // Password not encrypted, use as is
      console.log('Password not encrypted for user:', email);
    }
    
    // Compare passwords
    if (storedPassword !== password.trim()) {
      console.log('Invalid password for user:', email);
      return createCORSResponse({
        status: 'error',
        authenticated: false,
        message: 'Invalid email or password'
      });
    }
    
    // Authentication successful - return user data WITHOUT password
    const userData = {
      id: String(userRow[0] || '').trim(),
      name: String(userRow[1] || '').trim(),
      email: String(userRow[2] || '').trim(),
      role: String(userRow[4] || '').trim(),
      createdAt: userRow[5] || '',
      lastLogin: userRow[6] || '',
      passwordChangedBy: userRow[7] || '',
      passwordChangedAt: userRow[8] || ''
    };
    
    console.log('Authentication successful for:', email);
    
    return createCORSResponse({
      status: 'success',
      authenticated: true,
      message: 'Login successful',
      user: userData
    });
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error validating login:', error);
    return createCORSResponse({
      status: 'error',
      authenticated: false,
      message: 'Authentication error: ' + error.toString()
    });
  }
}

function addUser(userData) {
  try {
    console.log('addUser called with:', userData);
    
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    let usersSheet = spreadsheet.getSheetByName('Manage Users & Roles');
    
    if (!usersSheet) {
      // Create sheet if it doesn't exist
      getUsersAndRoles();
      usersSheet = spreadsheet.getSheetByName('Manage Users & Roles');
    }
    
    // Check if email already exists
    const data = usersSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (data[i][2] === userData.email) {
        return createCORSResponse({
          status: 'error',
          message: 'Email already exists'
        });
      }
    }
    
    // Generate user ID
    const userId = 'USER' + String(data.length).padStart(3, '0');
    
    // Encrypt password using Base64
    const encryptedPassword = Utilities.base64Encode(userData.password);
    
    // Add new user
    const newRow = [
      userId,
      userData.name,
      userData.email,
      encryptedPassword,
      userData.role,
      new Date().toISOString(),
      '',
      '',
      ''
    ];
    
    usersSheet.appendRow(newRow);
    
    console.log('User added successfully');
    return createCORSResponse({
      status: 'success',
      message: 'User added successfully',
      data: { id: userId }
    });
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error adding user:', error);
    return createCORSResponse({
      status: 'error',
      message: error.toString()
    });
  }
}

function deleteUser(userId) {
  try {
    console.log('deleteUser called for:', userId);
    
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    const usersSheet = spreadsheet.getSheetByName('Manage Users & Roles');
    
    if (!usersSheet) {
      return createCORSResponse({
        status: 'error',
        message: 'Users sheet not found'
      });
    }
    
    const data = usersSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    
    // Find the user row
    for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (data[i][0] === userId) {
        usersSheet.deleteRow(i + 1);
        console.log('User deleted successfully');
        return createCORSResponse({
          status: 'success',
          message: 'User deleted successfully'
        });
      }
    }
    
    return createCORSResponse({
      status: 'error',
      message: 'User not found'
    });
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error deleting user:', error);
    return createCORSResponse({
      status: 'error',
      message: error.toString()
    });
  }
}

function updateUserLastLogin(email) {
  try {
    console.log('updateUserLastLogin called for:', email);
    
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    let usersSheet = spreadsheet.getSheetByName('Manage Users & Roles');
    
    if (!usersSheet) {
      console.log('Users sheet not found, creating it first');
      getUsersAndRoles();
      usersSheet = spreadsheet.getSheetByName('Manage Users & Roles');
    }
    
    const data = usersSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    
    // Find the user row and update last login
    for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (data[i][2] === email) {
        const now = new Date();
        const timestamp = Utilities.formatDate(now, "Asia/Kolkata", "yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss");
        usersSheet.getRange(i + 1, 7).setValue(timestamp);
        console.log('Last login updated for:', email);
        return { success: true };
      }
    }
    
    console.log('User not found in sheet:', email);
    return { success: false, message: 'User not found' };
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error updating last login:', error);
    return { success: false, message: error.toString() };
  }
}

function changeUserPassword(userId, newPassword, changedByEmail) {
  try {
    console.log('changeUserPassword called for:', userId, 'by:', changedByEmail);
    
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    const usersSheet = spreadsheet.getSheetByName('Manage Users & Roles');
    
    if (!usersSheet) {
      return createCORSResponse({
        status: 'error',
        message: 'Users sheet not found'
      });
    }
    
    const data = usersSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    
    // Find the user row and update password
    for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (data[i][0] === userId) {
        // Encrypt new password using Base64
        const encryptedPassword = Utilities.base64Encode(newPassword);
        const now = new Date();
        const timestamp = Utilities.formatDate(now, "Asia/Kolkata", "yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss");
        
        // Update password (column 4), changed by (column 8), and changed at (column 9)
        usersSheet.getRange(i + 1, 4).setValue(encryptedPassword);
        usersSheet.getRange(i + 1, 8).setValue(changedByEmail || 'System');
        usersSheet.getRange(i + 1, 9).setValue(timestamp);
        
        console.log('Password updated successfully for user:', userId, 'by:', changedByEmail);
        return createCORSResponse({
          status: 'success',
          message: 'Password updated successfully'
        });
      }
    }
    
    return createCORSResponse({
      status: 'error',
      message: 'User not found'
    });
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error changing password:', error);
    return createCORSResponse({
      status: 'error',
      message: error.toString()
    });
  }
}

/**
 * Action Handlers
 */
function handleApproveAction(appointment, actionData) {
  console.log('handleApproveAction called');
  
  // Send approval email first
  sendNewApprovalEmail(appointment, actionData?.notes || '');
  
  // CRITICAL FIX: Update client status after approval using proper Session ID
  const appointmentId = getAppointmentId(appointment);
  console.log('Using appointment ID for status update:', appointmentId);
  
  const clientStatus = appointment.clientStatus || appointment['clientStatus'] || appointment['Client Status'] || '';
  
  // If this was a rescheduled appointment, update the client status to show approval
  if (clientStatus.includes('New Time Slot Chosen')) {
    console.log('Updating client status for approved rescheduled appointment');
    updateClientStatus(appointmentId, 'Approved - Awaiting Response', null);
  } else {
    console.log('Updating client status for approved new appointment');
    updateClientStatus(appointmentId, 'Approved - Awaiting Response', null);
  }
}

function handleRejectAction(appointment, actionData) {
  sendRejectionEmail(appointment, actionData.reason);
}

function handleRequestRebookingAction(appointment, actionData) {
  sendRequestRebookingEmail(appointment, actionData);
}

function handleRescheduleAction(appointment, actionData) {
  sendRescheduleEmail(appointment, actionData);
}

function handleRescheduleWithCalendarAction(appointment, actionData) {
  // Update the appointment with new date/time
  const sheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
  const appointmentId = appointment.appointmentId || appointment['Appointment ID'];
  
  if (!appointmentId) {
    throw new Error('Appointment ID not found');
  }
  
  // Find the appointment row
  const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];
  
  let appointmentRowIndex = -1;
  for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
    const rowAppointmentId = data[i][headers.indexOf('Appointment ID')] || 
                           data[i][headers.indexOf('appointmentId')];
    if (rowAppointmentId === appointmentId) {
      appointmentRowIndex = i + 1; // +1 because sheet rows are 1-indexed
      break;
    }
  }
  
  if (appointmentRowIndex === -1) {
    throw new Error('Appointment not found');
  }
  
  // Update the appointment data
  const selectedDateIndex = headers.indexOf('Selected Date') !== -1 ? 
                          headers.indexOf('Selected Date') : 
                          headers.indexOf('selectedDate');
  const selectedTimeIndex = headers.indexOf('Selected Time') !== -1 ? 
                          headers.indexOf('Selected Time') : 
                          headers.indexOf('selectedTime');
  
  if (selectedDateIndex !== -1) {
    sheet.getRange(appointmentRowIndex, selectedDateIndex + 1).setValue(actionData.newDate);
  }
  if (selectedTimeIndex !== -1) {
    sheet.getRange(appointmentRowIndex, selectedTimeIndex + 1).setValue(actionData.newTime);
  }
  
  // Create new appointment data for email
  const updatedAppointment = {
    ...appointment,
    selectedDate: actionData.newDate,
    selectedTime: actionData.newTime,
    'Selected Date': actionData.newDate,
    'Selected Time': actionData.newTime
  };
  
  // Send rescheduling confirmation email
  sendRescheduleWithCalendarEmail(updatedAppointment, actionData);
  
  // Create new calendar event if needed
  try {
    createCalendarEvent(updatedAppointment);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error creating calendar event:', error);
    // Continue even if calendar creation fails
  }
}

  sendCancellationEmail(appointment, actionData.reason);
}

function handlePaymentAction(appointment, actionData) {
  // Send payment email first
  sendPaymentEmail(appointment, actionData);

  const appointmentId = getAppointmentId(appointment);
  
  // Update client status to indicate waiting for payment proof upload

}

  // Mark client status so payment acknowledgement action is not offered again.
  const appointmentId = getAppointmentId(appointment);
  if (appointmentId) {
    updateClientStatus(appointmentId, 'Payment Acknowledged', null);
  }
}

}

/**
 * Schedule automatic feedback reminder emails after marking a session done.
 * Reminders are sent at Day 3, Day 7, and Day 14 until feedback is received.
 */
function scheduleFeedbackReminder(appointmentId) {
  try {
    const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    // Store: reminderCount|scheduledTimestamp
    props.setProperty('feedbackReminder_' + appointmentId, '0|' + new Date().getTime());
    // Trigger first reminder check in 3 days
    ScriptApp.newTrigger('sendPendingFeedbackReminders')
      .timeBased()
      .after(3 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000)
      .create();
    console.log('Feedback reminder scheduled for appointment:', appointmentId);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error scheduling feedback reminder (non-critical):', error);
  }
}

/**
 * Time-based trigger handler. Sweeps all pending feedback appointments and sends
 * reminder emails. Re-schedules itself if more reminders are still pending.
 * Reminders: Day 3 (automatic), Day 7, Day 14 — max 3 total.
 */
function sendPendingFeedbackReminders() {
  try {
    const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    const allProps = props.getProperties();
    const now = new Date().getTime();
    // Time since session completion that each reminder fires
    const REMINDER_INTERVALS_MS = [
      3  * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000,  // Day 3
      7  * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000,  // Day 7
      14 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000   // Day 14
    ];
    const MAX_REMINDERS = 3;
    let hasPending = false;

    for (const key in allProps) {
      if (!key.startsWith('feedbackReminder_')) continue;
      const appointmentId = key.replace('feedbackReminder_', '');
      const parts = allProps[key].split('|');
      const reminderCount = parseInt(parts[0]) || 0;
      const scheduledTime  = parseInt(parts[1]) || 0;

      if (reminderCount >= MAX_REMINDERS) {
        props.deleteProperty(key);
        continue;
      }

      // Only fire if enough time has elapsed since session completion
      if ((now - scheduledTime) < REMINDER_INTERVALS_MS[reminderCount]) {
        hasPending = true;
        continue;
      }

      try {
        const appointment = getAppointmentData(appointmentId);
        if (!appointment) { props.deleteProperty(key); continue; }

        const clientStatus = appointment.clientStatus || appointment['Client Status'] || '';
        if (clientStatus === 'Feedback Received') {
          props.deleteProperty(key);
          continue;
        }

        sendFeedbackReminderEmail(appointment, reminderCount + 1);
        const newCount = reminderCount + 1;
        if (newCount >= MAX_REMINDERS) {
          props.deleteProperty(key);
        } else {
          props.setProperty(key, newCount + '|' + scheduledTime); // keep original scheduledTime
          hasPending = true;
        }
      } catch (apptError) {
        console.error('Error processing feedback reminder for:', appointmentId, apptError);
        hasPending = true;
      }
    }

    // Re-schedule a daily check if reminders are still pending
    if (hasPending) {
      ScriptApp.newTrigger('sendPendingFeedbackReminders')
        .timeBased()
        .after(24 * 60 * 60 * 1000)
        .create();
    }

    // Clean up duplicate old triggers for this function (keep only the new one)
    const allTriggers = ScriptApp.getProjectTriggers()
      .filter(t => t.getHandlerFunction() === 'sendPendingFeedbackReminders');
    allTriggers.slice(0, allTriggers.length - 1).forEach(t => ScriptApp.deleteTrigger(t));

  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error in sendPendingFeedbackReminders:', error);
  }
}

/**
 * Send a single feedback reminder email.
 * reminderNumber: 1 = 1st auto, 2 = 2nd auto, 3 = 3rd auto, 0 = manual from admin.
 */
function sendFeedbackReminderEmail(appointment, reminderNumber) {
  const appointmentId = getAppointmentId(appointment);
  const baseUrl = getPublicWebAppUrl();
  const feedbackUrl = `${baseUrl}?appointmentId=${encodeURIComponent(String(appointmentId))}&submitFeedback=true`;
  const labels = ['Reminder', '1st Reminder', '2nd Reminder', '3rd Reminder'];
  const label = labels[reminderNumber] || `Reminder ${reminderNumber}`;

  const subject = `Feedback ${label} - ${appointment.name}`;
  const body = `
<p>Dear ${appointment.name},</p>

<p>We noticed we haven't received your feedback for the recent consultation session yet. Your feedback is very important to us and helps us improve our services.</p>

<div style="text-align: center; margin: 30px 0;">
  <a href="${feedbackUrl}" style="background: #28a745; color: white; padding: 15px 30px; text-decoration: none; border-radius: 8px; font-size: 16px; font-weight: 600; display: inline-block;">
    📝 Send Feedback Now
  </a>
</div>

<p style="font-size: 14px; color: #666; text-align: center;">
  It only takes a minute. We truly appreciate your time.
</p>

<p>Best regards,<br>
${CONFIG.FROM_NAME}<br>
📧 ${CONFIG.OWNER_EMAIL}</p>

<hr style="margin: 30px 0; border: none; border-top: 1px solid #eee;">
<p style="font-size: 12px; color: #999; text-align: center;">
  Once you submit your feedback, you will not receive further reminders.
</p>
  `;

  MailApp.sendEmail({ to: appointment.email, subject: subject, htmlBody: body });
  console.log(`Feedback reminder (${label}) sent to:`, appointment.email);
}

function handleMarkSessionDoneAction(appointment, actionData) {
  try {
    console.log('handleMarkSessionDoneAction called for appointment:', appointment.rowIndex || appointment.id);
    
    // Use helper function to get proper appointment ID
    const appointmentId = getAppointmentId(appointment);
    console.log('Using appointment ID for status update:', appointmentId);
    
    // Send completion email with feedback link FIRST
    sendSessionCompletionEmail(appointment, actionData);
    console.log('Session completion email sent successfully');
    
    // Update main appointment status to "Session Completed"
    updateAppointmentStatus(appointmentId, 'markSessionDone', actionData);
    console.log('Main status updated to Session Completed');
    
    // Update client status to "Feedback Pending"
    console.log('About to update client status to Feedback Pending for appointment ID:', appointmentId);
    updateClientStatus(appointmentId, 'Feedback Pending', null);
    console.log('Client status updated to Feedback Pending');

    // Schedule automatic feedback reminder emails (Day 3, Day 7, Day 14)
    scheduleFeedbackReminder(appointmentId);
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error in handleMarkSessionDoneAction:', error);
    throw error;
  }
}

function handleSendFeedbackReminderAction(appointment, actionData) {
