  sendFeedbackReminderEmail(appointment, 0); // 0 = manual, label as 'Reminder'
  console.log('Manual feedback reminder sent for:', appointmentId);
}

/**
 * Handle admin query resolution with optional document upload
 */
function handleAdminQueryResolution(params) {
  try {
    console.log('handleAdminQueryResolution called with:', params);
    
    const { appointmentId, resolution, adminName = 'Admin' } = params;
    
    if (!appointmentId || !resolution) {
      return createCORSResponse({
        status: 'error',
        message: 'Missing appointment ID or resolution text'
      });
    }
    
    // Get appointment data
    const appointment = getAppointmentData(appointmentId);
    if (!appointment) {
      return createCORSResponse({
        status: 'error',
        message: 'Appointment not found'
      });
    }
    
    // Handle file upload if present
    let fileLink = '';
    if (params.adminDocument && params.adminDocumentName && params.adminDocumentType) {
      try {
        console.log('Processing admin document upload:', params.adminDocumentName);
        
        // Create blob with proper base64 decoding and MIME type (EXACTLY like payment proof)
        const fileBlob = Utilities.newBlob(
          Utilities.base64Decode(params.adminDocument),
          params.adminDocumentType,
          params.adminDocumentName
        );
        
        const uploadedFile = uploadAdminQueryDocument(appointmentId, fileBlob, adminName);
        fileLink = uploadedFile.url;
        console.log('Admin query document uploaded:', uploadedFile);
        
        // Update admin query documents column
        updateAdminQueryDocuments(appointmentId, fileLink);
      } catch (fileError) {
        console.error('Error uploading admin query document:', fileError);
        // Continue without file upload
      }
    }
    
    // Add resolution to query history with file link if present
    const resolutionText = fileLink 
      ? `${resolution} [Admin Response Document: ${fileLink}]`
      : resolution;
    
    addQueryResolutionToHistory(appointmentId, resolutionText);
    
    // Send query resolution email to client
    sendQueryResolutionEmail(appointment, resolution, fileLink);
    
    // Update client status
    updateClientStatus(appointmentId, 'Query Resolved - Awaiting Response', null);
    
    return createCORSResponse({
      status: 'success',
      message: 'Query resolved successfully' + (fileLink ? ' with document attached' : '')
    });
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error handling admin query resolution:', error);
    return createCORSResponse({
      status: 'error',
      message: error.toString()
    });
  }
}

function handleQueryResolvedAction(appointment, actionData) {
  try {
    console.log('handleQueryResolvedAction called for appointment:', appointment.rowIndex || appointment.id);
    
    // Use helper function to get proper appointment ID
    const appointmentId = getAppointmentId(appointment);
    console.log('Using appointment ID for status update:', appointmentId);
    const resolution = actionData.resolution || 'Query resolved by admin';
    
    // Handle admin document upload if present
    let fileLink = '';
    if (actionData.adminDocument) {
      try {
        console.log('Processing admin document upload for query resolution');
        
        // Create blob from base64 data
        const fileBlob = Utilities.newBlob(
          Utilities.base64Decode(actionData.adminDocument.fileContent),
          actionData.adminDocument.fileType,
          actionData.adminDocument.fileName
        );
        
        const adminName = 'Admin'; // You can make this dynamic if needed
        const uploadedFile = uploadAdminQueryDocument(appointmentId, fileBlob, adminName);
        fileLink = uploadedFile.url;
        console.log('Admin query document uploaded:', uploadedFile);
        
        // Update admin query documents column in spreadsheet
        updateAdminQueryDocuments(appointmentId, fileLink);
      } catch (fileError) {
        console.error('Error uploading admin query document:', fileError);
        // Continue without file - don't fail the entire operation
      }
    }
    
    // Create resolution text with file link if present
    const resolutionText = fileLink 
      ? `${resolution} [Admin Response Document: ${fileLink}]`
      : resolution;
    
    // Send query resolution email to client FIRST with file link
    sendQueryResolutionEmail(appointment, resolution, fileLink);
    console.log('Query resolution email sent to client');
    
    // Get current query count
    const currentQueryCount = getQueryCountFromHistory(appointment);
    console.log('Current query count:', currentQueryCount);
    
    // Add resolution to query history with file link
    addQueryResolutionToHistory(appointmentId, resolutionText);
    console.log('Resolution added to query history');
    
    // Determine new client status based on query count and main status
    let newClientStatus;
    const mainStatus = appointment.status || 'Pending';
    
    if (currentQueryCount >= 3) {
      // After 3 queries, set to appropriate resolved status
      if (mainStatus === 'Approved') {
        newClientStatus = 'Query Resolved - Awaiting Response';
      } else if (mainStatus === 'Session Scheduled') {
        newClientStatus = 'Query Resolved - Awaiting Response';
      } else {
        newClientStatus = 'Query Resolved - Awaiting Response';
      }
      console.log('Max queries reached, setting client status to:', newClientStatus);
    } else {
      // Still allow more queries, set to resolved but responsive status
      newClientStatus = 'Query Resolved - Awaiting Response';
      console.log('Queries still allowed, setting client status to:', newClientStatus);
    }
    
    // Update client status
    updateClientStatus(appointmentId, newClientStatus, null);
    console.log('Client status updated to:', newClientStatus);
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error in handleQueryResolvedAction:', error);
    throw error;
  }
}

/**
 * Update appointment status in spreadsheet
 */
function updateAppointmentStatus(appointmentId, action, actionData) {
  try {
    console.log(`DEBUG: updateAppointmentStatus called with action: "${action}"`);
    
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = spreadsheet.getActiveSheet();
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    
    if (data.length <= 1) return;
    
    const headers = data[0];
    const rowIndex = findRowIndexBySessionId(appointmentId);
    
    console.log(`DEBUG: Processing row ${rowIndex} for action "${action}"`);
    
    // Define statusMap at function scope
    const statusMap = {
      'approve': 'Approved',
      'reject': 'Rejected',
      'reschedule': 'Requested Rescheduling',
      'cancel': 'Cancelled',
      'payment': 'Payment Sent',
      'paymentAcknowledgement': 'Session Scheduled',
      'sendConsent': 'Consent Email Sent',
      'sendSessionReminder': 'Session Reminder Sent',
      'markSessionDone': 'Session Completed',
      'requestRebooking': 'Requested Rebooking',
      'queryResolved': 'Query Resolved'
    };
    
    if (rowIndex >= 2 && rowIndex <= data.length) {
      let statusColIndex = headers.indexOf('Status');
      let notesColIndex = headers.indexOf('Admin Notes');
      
      console.log(`DEBUG: Status column index: ${statusColIndex}`);
      
      if (statusColIndex !== -1) {
        const mappedStatus = statusMap[action];
        const finalStatus = mappedStatus || action;
        
        console.log(`DEBUG: Action "${action}" -> Mapped Status: "${mappedStatus}" -> Final Status: "${finalStatus}"`);
        
        // Set the status
        sheet.getRange(rowIndex, statusColIndex + 1).setValue(finalStatus);
        
        // Force save to ensure persistence
        SpreadsheetApp.flush();
        
        // Verify the write
        const verifyStatus = sheet.getRange(rowIndex, statusColIndex + 1).getValue();
        console.log(`DEBUG: Verification - Status written to spreadsheet: "${verifyStatus}"`);
      }
      
      if (notesColIndex !== -1 && actionData && actionData.notes) {
        sheet.getRange(rowIndex, notesColIndex + 1).setValue(actionData.notes);
      }
      
      console.log(`Status update completed for action: ${action} -> ${statusMap[action] || action}`);
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error updating appointment status:', error);
    throw error;
  }
}

  const queryUrl = `${baseUrl}?appointmentId=${appointmentId}&response=query`;

  const serviceCategory = appointment['service-category'] || appointment.serviceCategory || '';
  const sessionType = appointment['session-type'] || appointment.sessionType || '';

  const isRescheduled = clientStatus.includes('New Time Slot Chosen');
  
  const subject = isRescheduled ? 
    `Rescheduled Session Confirmed - ${appointment.name}` :

  </p>
</div>
` : '';

  // Determine session type description for the brochure link text
  let brochureDescription = 'Service Brochure';

    brochureDescription = 'Advisory Services Brochure';
  } else if (sessionType) {

      case 'Generalized':
      case 'generalized':
        brochureDescription = 'Generalized Session Brochure';

      case 'Specialized (Virtual)':
      case 'specialized':
        brochureDescription = 'Specialized Session Brochure';
        break;
      case 'Super-Specialized (In-Person)':
      case 'super-specialized':
        brochureDescription = 'Super-Specialized Session Brochure';
        break;
      case 'Long-term Projects':
      case 'long-term-engagement':
        brochureDescription = 'Long-term Engagement Brochure';
        break;

  }
  
  const body = `
<p>Dear ${appointment.name},</p>

<p>Thank you for booking a session.</p>

${rescheduledMessage}

<h3>📋 Important Documents:</h3>
<p>Please find the following documents for your reference:</p>
<ul style="line-height: 1.6;">
  <li><a href="${brochureUrl}" target="_blank">${brochureDescription}</a></li>
  <li><a href="${CONFIG.DOCUMENTS.PRIVACY_POLICY_URL}" target="_blank">Privacy Policy</a></li>
  <li><a href="${CONFIG.DOCUMENTS.REFUND_POLICY_URL}" target="_blank">Refund & Cancellation Policy</a></li>
</ul>

<h3>🚀 Next Steps:</h3>
<p>Please choose one of the following options:</p>
<div style="text-align: center; margin: 20px 0;">
  <a href="${proceedUrl}" style="background: #28a745; color: white; padding: 12px 24px; text-decoration: none; border-radius: 5px; margin: 0 10px; display: inline-block;">✅ Proceed</a>
  <a href="${queryUrl}" style="background: #007bff; color: white; padding: 12px 24px; text-decoration: none; border-radius: 5px; margin: 0 10px; display: inline-block;">❓ Query</a>
</div>

<p style="font-size: 14px; color: #666;">
• Click <strong>Proceed</strong> if you are ready to continue with the session as planned<br>
• Click <strong>Query</strong> if you have questions or need clarification (up to 100 words)
</p>

<p>Best regards,<br>
${CONFIG.FROM_NAME}<br>
📧 ${CONFIG.OWNER_EMAIL}</p>

/**
 * Send reschedule email
 */
function sendRescheduleEmail(appointment, actionData) {
  const clientName = appointment.name || appointment['name'] || appointment['Full Name *'] || appointment.clientName || 'Valued Client';
  const subject = `Session Rescheduling Request - ${clientName}`;
  const appointmentId = getAppointmentId(appointment);
  console.log('sendRescheduleEmail using appointmentId:', appointmentId);
  
  // Build booking form URL with pre-filled parameters (manual encoding for Apps Script)
  const bookingFormBaseUrl = "http://theanuragsharma.com/booksession.html";
  
  // Helper function to encode URI component
  function encodeParam(value) {
    return encodeURIComponent(value || '');
  }
  
  // Build query parameters manually - get all possible field variations
  const params = [];
  params.push('mode=reschedule');
  params.push('sessionId=' + encodeParam(appointmentId));
  params.push('name=' + encodeParam(appointment['Full Name *'] || appointment.name || appointment.clientName || ''));
  params.push('email=' + encodeParam(appointment['Email Address *'] || appointment.email || appointment.emailAddress || ''));
  params.push('phone=' + encodeParam(appointment['Phone Number *'] || appointment.phone || appointment.phoneNumber || ''));
  
  // Extract country code from potentially formatted string like "+91 (India)"
  let countryCode = appointment['Country Code'] || appointment['country-code'] || '';
  if (countryCode && countryCode.includes('(')) {
    countryCode = countryCode.split('(')[0].trim(); // Extract "+91" from "+91 (India)"
  }
  params.push('countryCode=' + encodeParam(countryCode));
  
  params.push('organization=' + encodeParam(appointment['Organization *'] || appointment.organization || appointment.organizationName || ''));
  params.push('designation=' + encodeParam(appointment['Designation *'] || appointment.designation || appointment.clientDesignation || ''));
  
  // Extract location/region code from potentially formatted string
  let location = appointment['Region *'] || appointment.location || '';
  // Map display text back to value codes
  const locationMapping = {
    'Middle East / West Asia': 'middle-east',
    'Europe': 'europe',
    'United States': 'us',
    'India': 'india',
    'Japan': 'japan',
    'Others': 'others'
  };
  if (locationMapping[location]) {
    location = locationMapping[location];
  }
  params.push('location=' + encodeParam(location));
  
  // Extract service category (consultancy/advisory)
  let serviceCategory = appointment['Category *'] || appointment['service-category'] || appointment['Service Category'] || appointment['Service Category *'] || appointment.serviceCategory || '';
  const serviceCategoryMapping = {
    'Consultancy': 'consultancy',
    'Advisory': 'advisory',
    'consultancy': 'consultancy',
    'advisory': 'advisory'
  };
  if (serviceCategoryMapping[serviceCategory]) {
    serviceCategory = serviceCategoryMapping[serviceCategory];
  }
  params.push('serviceCategory=' + encodeParam(serviceCategory));
  
  // Extract session type and map display text to value
  let sessionType = appointment['Type of Session *'] || appointment['session-type'] || appointment['Session Type *'] || appointment['Session Type'] || appointment.sessionType || '';
  const sessionTypeMapping = {
    'Generalized': 'generalized',
    'Specialized (Virtual)': 'specialized',
    'Super-Specialized (In-Person)': 'super-specialized',
    'Long-term Projects': 'long-term-engagement',
    'Advisory': 'advisory-service',
    'generalized': 'generalized',
    'specialized': 'specialized',
    'super-specialized': 'super-specialized',
    'long-term-engagement': 'long-term-engagement',
    'advisory-service': 'advisory-service'
  };
  if (sessionTypeMapping[sessionType]) {
    sessionType = sessionTypeMapping[sessionType];
  }
  params.push('sessionType=' + encodeParam(sessionType));
  
  // Add domains and regions if they exist
  params.push('selectedDomains=' + encodeParam(appointment['Domain(s) *'] || appointment['selected-domains'] || ''));
  params.push('customDomain=' + encodeParam(appointment['Other Domain *'] || appointment['custom-domain-input'] || ''));
  params.push('selectedRegions=' + encodeParam(appointment['Region(s) *'] || appointment['selected-regions'] || ''));
  params.push('customRegion=' + encodeParam(appointment['Other Region(s) *'] || appointment['custom-region-domain-input'] || ''));
  
  params.push('topic=' + encodeParam(appointment['What do you want to talk about? *'] || appointment['Consultation Topic *'] || appointment.topic || appointment.consultationTopic || ''));

  // Preserve selected timezone during reschedule flow
  const selectedTimezone = appointment['Selected Timezone'] || appointment['timezone-selector'] || appointment.timezoneSelector || '';
  if (selectedTimezone) {
    params.push('timezoneSelector=' + encodeParam(selectedTimezone));
  }
  
  // Add dynamic session questions if they exist - check both field names and question text column headers
  const dynamicFieldsMapping = {
    'space-policy-area': ['space-policy-area', 'What specific area of space policy interests you most?'],
    'guidance-type': ['guidance-type', 'Are you looking for general guidance or specific insights? *'],
    'specific-insights-details': ['specific-insights-details', 'If Specific insights, Details'],
    'policy-directive': ['policy-directive', 'Is there any policy directive you are concerned with? *'],
    'policy-directive-details': ['policy-directive-details', 'If Yes, Policy Directive Details'],
    'geopolitical-situation': ['geopolitical-situation', 'Is there any specific Geopolitical development/ situation you are concerned with? *'],
    'geopolitical-details': ['geopolitical-details', 'If Yes, Geopolitical Development/Situation Details'],
    'use-case': ['use-case', 'Is there any particular "Use Case" related to your work profile/project you are concerned with? *'],
    'use-case-details': ['use-case-details', 'If Yes, Use Case Details'],
    'additional-info': ['additional-info', 'Is there any other specific information you would like to discuss before the consultancy session to make the session more personalized? *'],
    'additional-info-details': ['additional-info-details', 'If Yes, Additional Information Details'],
    'specific-entity': ['specific-entity', 'Is there any specific Entity you are already dealing with? *'],
    'entity-details': ['entity-details', 'If Yes, Entity Details'],
    'detail-level': ['detail-level', 'What level of detail are you expecting from this consultation? *'],
    'strategic-objectives': ['strategic-objectives', 'What are your primary strategic objectives for this engagement? *'],
    'expected-outcomes': ['expected-outcomes', 'Which specific outcomes are you hoping to achieve over the 2-6 month period? *'],
    'engagement-model': ['engagement-model', 'What is your preferred engagement model (weekly/bi-weekly consultations)? *'],
    'deliverables-needed': ['deliverables-needed', 'Do you need deliverables like reports, frameworks, or policy recommendations? *'],
    'complex-challenges': ['complex-challenges', 'What complex challenges or strategic decisions are you currently facing? *'],
    'relevant-regional-dynamics': ['relevant-regional-dynamics', 'Which regional dynamics are most relevant to your current situation? *'],
    'analysis-type': ['analysis-type', 'Are you looking for comprehensive analysis or strategic planning assistance? *'],
    'customized-frameworks': ['customized-frameworks', 'Do you need customized frameworks or policy recommendations? *']
  };
  
  Object.keys(dynamicFieldsMapping).forEach(function(fieldKey) {
    const possibleColumns = dynamicFieldsMapping[fieldKey];
    let value = '';
    for (var i = 0; i < possibleColumns.length; i++) {
      if (appointment[possibleColumns[i]]) {
        value = appointment[possibleColumns[i]];
        break;
      }
    }
    if (value) {
      // Map display text back to form values for dynamic questions
      let mappedValue = value;
      
      // Mapping for guidance-type field
      if (fieldKey === 'guidance-type') {
        const guidanceTypeMapping = {
          'General': 'general',
          'Specific insights': 'specific',
          'general': 'general',
          'specific': 'specific'
        };
        mappedValue = guidanceTypeMapping[value] || value.toLowerCase();
      }
      
      // Mapping for yes/no questions
      if (fieldKey.includes('directive') || fieldKey.includes('geopolitical') || 
          fieldKey.includes('use-case') || fieldKey.includes('additional-info') || 
          fieldKey.includes('specific-entity')) {
        const yesNoMapping = {
          'Yes': 'yes',
          'No': 'no',
          'yes': 'yes',
          'no': 'no'
        };
        mappedValue = yesNoMapping[value] || value.toLowerCase();
      }
      
      // Mapping for detail-level field
      if (fieldKey === 'detail-level') {
        const detailLevelMapping = {
          'Basic overview': 'basic',
          'Detailed analysis': 'detailed', 
          'Comprehensive report': 'comprehensive',
          'basic': 'basic',
          'detailed': 'detailed',
          'comprehensive': 'comprehensive'
        };
        mappedValue = detailLevelMapping[value] || value.toLowerCase();
      }
      
      // Mapping for analysis-type field
      if (fieldKey === 'analysis-type') {
        const analysisTypeMapping = {
          'Comprehensive analysis': 'comprehensive',
          'Strategic planning assistance': 'strategic',
          'comprehensive': 'comprehensive',
          'strategic': 'strategic'
        };
        mappedValue = analysisTypeMapping[value] || value.toLowerCase();
      }
      
      // Mapping for engagement-model field
      if (fieldKey === 'engagement-model') {
        const engagementModelMapping = {
          'Weekly consultations': 'weekly',
          'Bi-weekly consultations': 'bi-weekly',
          'Monthly consultations': 'monthly',
          'weekly': 'weekly',
          'bi-weekly': 'bi-weekly', 
          'monthly': 'monthly'
        };
        mappedValue = engagementModelMapping[value] || value.toLowerCase();
      }
      
      // Mapping for deliverables-needed field
      if (fieldKey === 'deliverables-needed' || fieldKey === 'customized-frameworks') {
        const yesNoMapping = {
          'Yes': 'yes',
          'No': 'no',
          'yes': 'yes',
          'no': 'no'
        };
        mappedValue = yesNoMapping[value] || value.toLowerCase();
      }
      
      params.push(fieldKey + '=' + encodeParam(mappedValue));
    }
  });
  
  // Add consent fields if they exist - try multiple column name variations
  let dataConsent = appointment['Data Consent'] || appointment['data-consent'] || appointment['dataConsent'] || '';
  let termsConsent = appointment['Terms Consent'] || appointment['terms-consent'] || appointment['termsConsent'] || '';
  
  // Log for debugging
  console.log('Consent fields found:', {
    'Data Consent': appointment['Data Consent'],
    'data-consent': appointment['data-consent'], 
    'dataConsent': appointment['dataConsent'],
    'Terms Consent': appointment['Terms Consent'],
    'terms-consent': appointment['terms-consent'],
    'termsConsent': appointment['termsConsent']
  });
  
  // If consent fields are empty or off, default to 'on' for reschedule
  if (!dataConsent || dataConsent === 'off') dataConsent = 'on';
  if (!termsConsent || termsConsent === 'off') termsConsent = 'on';
  
  params.push('dataConsent=' + encodeParam(dataConsent));
  params.push('termsConsent=' + encodeParam(termsConsent));
  
  // Dynamic fields are already handled above in dynamicFieldsMapping to avoid duplicates
  
  if (actionData.reason) {
    params.push('rescheduleReason=' + encodeParam(actionData.reason));
  }
  
  const rescheduleUrl = bookingFormBaseUrl + '?' + params.join('&');
  
  // DEBUG: Log all available fields in the appointment object
  console.log('=== RESCHEDULE EMAIL DEBUG ===');
  console.log('All appointment fields:');
  Object.keys(appointment).forEach(key => {
    console.log(`${key}: ${appointment[key]}`);
  });
  console.log('Reschedule URL:', rescheduleUrl);
  console.log('===============================');
  
  // Always prioritize the latest "Selected Date" and "Selected Time" columns
  // Check multiple field name variants (capital, lowercase, dashes)
  let displayDate = appointment['Selected Date'] || appointment['selected-date'] || 
                    appointment.selectedDate || appointment['SelectedDate'] || 'Not specified';
  let displayTime = appointment['Selected Time'] || appointment['selected-time'] || 
                    appointment.selectedTime || appointment['SelectedTime'] || 'Not specified';
  const selectedSlotValue = appointment['Selected Slot'] || appointment['selected-slot'] || appointment.selectedSlot || '';
  const slotTimezoneMatch = String(selectedSlotValue).trim().match(/\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}\s+\d{2}:\d{2}(?::\d{2})?\s+(.+)$/);
  const currentTimezoneLabel = slotTimezoneMatch ? slotTimezoneMatch[1].trim() : (appointment['Selected Timezone'] || appointment['timezone-selector'] || '');
  
  // Get session type for display (use original appointment data, not the mapped value)
  const displaySessionType = appointment['session-type'] || appointment.sessionType || 
                      appointment['Session Type'] || appointment.consultationType || 
                      appointment['Consultation Type'] || 'Consultation';
  
  // Format date for better display
  const formatDisplayDate = (dateStr) => {
    if (!dateStr || dateStr === 'Not specified') return 'Not specified';
    try {
      const date = new Date(dateStr);
      if (isNaN(date.getTime())) return dateStr;
      return date.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { 
        weekday: 'long', 
        year: 'numeric', 
        month: 'long', 
        day: 'numeric' 
      });
    } catch (error) {
      return dateStr;
    }
  };
  
  // Format time for better display
  const formatDisplayTime = (timeStr) => {
    if (!timeStr || timeStr === 'Not specified') return 'Not specified';
    if (timeStr.includes('-')) return timeStr;
    if (timeStr.includes(':')) {
      try {
        const [hours, minutes] = timeStr.split(':');
        const hour = parseInt(hours);
        const min = minutes || '00';
        const ampm = hour >= 12 ? 'PM' : 'AM';
        const displayHour = hour > 12 ? hour - 12 : (hour === 0 ? 12 : hour);
        return `${displayHour}:${min} ${ampm}`;
      } catch (error) {
        return timeStr;
      }
    }
    return timeStr;
  };
  
  const body = `
<p>Dear ${clientName},</p>

<p>I hope this message finds you well. I am writing to request a rescheduling of your upcoming session due to unforeseen circumstances on my end.</p>

${actionData.reason && actionData.reason.trim() ? `<p><strong>Additional Information:</strong> ${actionData.reason}</p>` : ''}

<h3>📅 Current Session Details:</h3>
<div style="background: #f8f9fa; padding: 15px; border-radius: 8px; margin: 15px 0; border-left: 4px solid #dc3545;">
  <p><strong>Date:</strong> ${formatDisplayDate(displayDate)}</p>
  <p><strong>Time:</strong> ${formatDisplayTime(displayTime)}${currentTimezoneLabel ? ' ' + currentTimezoneLabel : ''}</p>
  <p><strong>Session Type:</strong> ${displaySessionType}</p>
  <p><strong>Client:</strong> ${clientName}</p>
  <p><strong>Organization:</strong> ${appointment.organization || appointment.organizationName || 'Not specified'}</p>
</div>

<h3>🆕 Choose Your New Schedule:</h3>
<p>Please click the button below to select a new date and time that works better for you. Your existing booking information has been pre-filled for your convenience, and you just need to select a new date and time from the available slots.</p>

<div style="text-align: center; margin: 30px 0;">
  <a href="${rescheduleUrl}" style="background: #007bff; color: white; padding: 15px 30px; text-decoration: none; border-radius: 8px; font-size: 16px; display: inline-block; box-shadow: 0 4px 8px rgba(0,123,255,0.3);">
    📅 Reschedule My Session
  </a>
</div>

<h3>💡 What to Expect:</h3>
<ul style="line-height: 1.6;">
  <li>Click the button above to access the booking form</li>
  <li>Your existing information will be pre-filled (non-editable)</li>
  <li>Select your preferred new date and time from available slots in the calendar</li>
  <li>Submit to confirm your new appointment time</li>
  <li>You'll receive a confirmation email with the updated details</li>
</ul>

<p>I sincerely apologize for any inconvenience this may cause and appreciate your understanding and flexibility.</p>

<p>Best regards,<br>
${CONFIG.FROM_NAME}<br>
📧 ${CONFIG.OWNER_EMAIL}</p>
  `;
  
  try {
    MailApp.sendEmail({
      to: appointment.email || appointment.emailAddress,
      subject: subject,
      htmlBody: body
    });
    console.log('Reschedule email sent successfully');
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error sending reschedule email:', error);
    throw error;
  }
}

/**
 * Send payment email
 */
function sendPaymentEmail(appointment, actionData) {
  try {
    console.log('=== PAYMENT EMAIL DEBUG START ===');
    console.log('sendPaymentEmail called with appointment:', appointment);
    console.log('sendPaymentEmail called with actionData:', actionData);
    
    const appointmentId = getAppointmentId(appointment);
    console.log('sendPaymentEmail using appointmentId:', appointmentId);
    
    if (!appointmentId) {
      console.error('No appointment ID found - cannot send payment email');
      throw new Error('Unable to determine appointment ID for payment email');
    }
    
    if (!appointment.email) {
      console.error('No email address found in appointment:', appointment);
      throw new Error('No email address found for payment email');
    }
    
    console.log('Sending payment email to:', appointment.email);
    
    const baseUrl = getPublicWebAppUrl();
    const uploadPaymentUrl = `${baseUrl}?appointmentId=${appointmentId}&response=uploadPayment`;
    
    console.log('Payment upload URL:', uploadPaymentUrl);
    
    const subject = `Payment Invoice - ${appointment.name}`;
    const body = `
<h2>Payment Invoice</h2>
<p>Dear ${appointment.name},</p>

<p>Thank you for your consultation session. Please find your payment information below.</p>

${actionData.notes ? `<p><strong>Payment Notes:</strong> ${actionData.notes}</p>` : ''}

<p>As you have chosen to proceed, please send the payment and attach the payment proof using the link below:</p>

<div style="text-align: center; margin: 20px 0;">
  <a href="${uploadPaymentUrl}" style="background: #28a745; color: white; padding: 12px 24px; text-decoration: none; border-radius: 5px; display: inline-block;"> 📤 Upload Payment Proof</a>
</div>

<p style="font-size: 14px; color: #666;">
• Please process the payment according to the instructions provided<br>
• After payment, click the button above to upload your payment proof<br>
• Accepted formats: PDF, JPG, PNG (Max 10MB)
</p>

<p>Best regards,<br>
${CONFIG.FROM_NAME}<br>
📧 ${CONFIG.OWNER_EMAIL}</p>
    `;
    
    let emailOptions = {
      to: appointment.email,
      subject: subject,
      htmlBody: body
    };
    
    console.log('Email options prepared:', {
      to: emailOptions.to,
      subject: emailOptions.subject,
      hasHtmlBody: !!emailOptions.htmlBody
    });
    
    if (actionData.fileContent && actionData.fileName) {
      try {
        console.log('Processing attachment:', actionData.fileName);
        const fileBlob = Utilities.newBlob(
          Utilities.base64Decode(actionData.fileContent),
          'application/pdf',
          actionData.fileName
        );
        emailOptions.attachments = [fileBlob];
        console.log('Attachment added successfully');
      } catch (attachmentError) {
        console.error('Error processing attachment:', attachmentError);
      }
    }
    
    console.log('Attempting to send email...');
    MailApp.sendEmail(emailOptions);
    console.log('Payment email sent successfully to:', appointment.email);
    console.log('=== PAYMENT EMAIL DEBUG END ===');
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error sending payment email:', error);
    console.error('Error details:', error.toString());
    console.error('=== PAYMENT EMAIL DEBUG END (WITH ERROR) ===');
    throw error;
  }
}

function getFormattedSessionDateTime(appointment) {
  const selectedDate = appointment['selected-date'] || appointment.selectedDate || appointment['selectedDate'] || appointment['Selected Date'];
  const selectedTime = appointment['selected-time'] || appointment.selectedTime || appointment['selectedTime'] || appointment['Selected Time'];
  const selectedSlot = appointment['selected-slot'] || appointment.selectedSlot || appointment['selectedSlot'] || appointment['Selected Slot'];

  let appointmentDateTime = null;
  let formattedDate = 'Not specified';
  let formattedTime = 'Not specified';
  let formattedDateTime = 'Not specified';

  if (selectedSlot && selectedSlot !== 'N/A') {
    const slotValue = selectedSlot.toString().trim();
    const slotWithTimezone = slotValue.match(/(\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2})\s+(\d{2}:\d{2}(?::\d{2})?)\s+(.+)/);

    if (slotWithTimezone) {
      const datePart = slotWithTimezone[1];
      const timePart = slotWithTimezone[2].length === 5 ? `${slotWithTimezone[2]}:00` : slotWithTimezone[2];
      const timezonePart = slotWithTimezone[3].trim();

      appointmentDateTime = new Date(`${datePart}T${timePart}`);
      formattedDate = formatDateForDisplay(datePart);
      formattedTime = `${formatTimeForDisplay(timePart)} ${timezonePart}`;
      formattedDateTime = `${formattedDate} at ${formattedTime}`;

      return { formattedDate, formattedTime, formattedDateTime, appointmentDateTime };
    }
  }

  if (selectedDate && selectedTime && selectedDate !== 'N/A' && selectedTime !== 'N/A') {
    const cleanDate = selectedDate.toString().trim();
    const cleanTime = selectedTime.toString().trim();
    appointmentDateTime = new Date(`${cleanDate}T${cleanTime}`);

    if (!isNaN(appointmentDateTime.getTime())) {
      formattedDate = formatDateForDisplay(cleanDate);
      formattedTime = formatTimeForDisplay(cleanTime);
      formattedDateTime = `${formattedDate} at ${formattedTime}`;
      return { formattedDate, formattedTime, formattedDateTime, appointmentDateTime };
    }
  }

  if (selectedSlot && selectedSlot !== 'N/A') {
    const slotValue = selectedSlot.toString().trim();
    const slotMatch = slotValue.match(/(\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2})\s+(\d{2}:\d{2}(?::\d{2})?)/);
    if (slotMatch) {
      const datePart = slotMatch[1];
      const timePart = slotMatch[2].length === 5 ? `${slotMatch[2]}:00` : slotMatch[2];
      appointmentDateTime = new Date(`${datePart}T${timePart}`);
      formattedDate = formatDateForDisplay(datePart);
      formattedTime = formatTimeForDisplay(timePart);
      formattedDateTime = `${formattedDate} at ${formattedTime}`;
      return { formattedDate, formattedTime, formattedDateTime, appointmentDateTime };
    }

    formattedDateTime = slotValue;
  }

  return { formattedDate, formattedTime, formattedDateTime, appointmentDateTime };
}

/**
 * Send payment acknowledgement email with Google Meet link
 */
function sendPaymentAcknowledgementEmail(appointment, actionData) {
  try {
    console.log('sendPaymentAcknowledgementEmail called');
    
    const sessionDateTimeInfo = getFormattedSessionDateTime(appointment);
    let appointmentDateTime = sessionDateTimeInfo.appointmentDateTime;
    
    if (!appointmentDateTime || isNaN(appointmentDateTime.getTime())) {
      // Fallback to current date + 1 day if parsing fails
      appointmentDateTime = new Date();
      appointmentDateTime.setDate(appointmentDateTime.getDate() + 1);
      appointmentDateTime.setHours(10, 0, 0, 0); // Default to 10 AM
      console.log('Could not parse appointment date/time, using fallback:', appointmentDateTime);
    }
    
    // Set end time to 1 hour later
    const endDateTime = new Date(appointmentDateTime.getTime() + (60 * 60 * 1000));
    
    // Create Google Calendar event with Google Meet
    let calendarEvent;
    let meetLink;
    
    try {
      // Generate a unique meeting code for this session
      const appointmentId = getAppointmentId(appointment);
      const clientName = (appointment.name || '').replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g, '').toLowerCase();
      const dateCode = appointmentDateTime.getFullYear().toString() + 
                      String(appointmentDateTime.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0') + 
                      String(appointmentDateTime.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
      
      // Create a unique meeting room code
      const meetingCode = `${clientName}-${dateCode}-${appointmentId}`.substring(0, 20);
      
      // Use Google Meet room format (this will create a persistent room)
      meetLink = `https://meet.google.com/${meetingCode}`;
      
      // Create the calendar event
      calendarEvent = CalendarApp.getDefaultCalendar().createEvent(
        `Consultation Session - ${appointment.name}`,
        appointmentDateTime,
        endDateTime,
        {
          description: `Consultation session with ${appointment.name} from ${appointment.organization || 'N/A'}.
          
Session Type: ${appointment['session-type'] || appointment.sessionType || 'N/A'}
          
Client will be asked to give consent 10 minutes before starting the session.`,
          guests: appointment.email,
          sendInvites: true
        }
      );
      
      console.log('Calendar event created successfully');
      console.log('Event ID:', calendarEvent.getId());
      console.log('Meeting code generated:', meetingCode);
      console.log('Meet link:', meetLink);
      
    } catch (calendarError) {
      console.error('Error creating calendar event:', calendarError);
      // Use a timestamped fallback link
      meetLink = `https://meet.google.com/session-${Date.now()}`;
    }
    
    const subject = `Payment Confirmed - Meeting Details - ${appointment.name}`;
    const formattedDate = sessionDateTimeInfo.formattedDate !== 'Not specified'
      ? sessionDateTimeInfo.formattedDate
      : formatDateForDisplay(appointmentDateTime);
    const formattedTime = sessionDateTimeInfo.formattedTime !== 'Not specified'
      ? sessionDateTimeInfo.formattedTime
      : formatTimeForDisplay(appointmentDateTime);
    
    const body = `
<h2>Payment Confirmed - Session Details</h2>
<p>Dear ${appointment.name},</p>

<p>Thank you for the payment.</p>

<h3>📅 Session Details:</h3>
<p><strong>Date:</strong> ${formattedDate}</p>
<p><strong>Time:</strong> ${formattedTime}</p>
<p><strong>Duration:</strong> 1 hour</p>

<h3>⚠️ Important Information:</h3>
<div style="background: #fff3cd; padding: 15px; border-radius: 8px; margin: 15px 0; border-left: 4px solid #ffc107;">
  <p style="margin: 0; font-size: 14px; color: #856404;">
    <strong>📋 Please Note:</strong> You will be asked to give consent 10 minutes before starting the session.
  </p>
</div>

<h3>📋 Session Preparation:</h3>
<ul style="line-height: 1.6;">
  <li>Please join the meeting 5 minutes before the scheduled time</li>
  <li>Ensure you have a stable internet connection</li>
  <li>Have your questions and discussion points ready</li>
  <li>A calendar invitation has been sent to your email</li>
</ul>

<p>We look forward to our consultation session!</p>

<p>Best regards,<br>
${CONFIG.FROM_NAME}<br>
📧 ${CONFIG.OWNER_EMAIL}</p>
    `;
    
    // Send the email
    MailApp.sendEmail({
      to: appointment.email,
      subject: subject,
      htmlBody: body
    });
    
    console.log('Payment acknowledgement email sent successfully to:', appointment.email);
    
    return {
      status: 'success',
      meetingLink: meetLink,
      calendarEventId: calendarEvent ? calendarEvent.getId() : null
    };
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error sending payment acknowledgement email:', error);
    throw error;
  }
}

/**
 * Send consent email before session
 */
function sendConsentEmail(appointment, actionData) {
  try {
    console.log('sendConsentEmail called');
    
    const appointmentId = getAppointmentId(appointment);
    console.log('sendConsentEmail using appointmentId:', appointmentId);
    
    const baseUrl = getPublicWebAppUrl();
    const encodedAppointmentId = encodeURIComponent(String(appointmentId));
    const consentUrl = `${baseUrl}?appointmentId=${encodedAppointmentId}&giveConsent=true`;
    console.log('Generated consent URL:', consentUrl);
    
    const sessionDateTimeInfo = getFormattedSessionDateTime(appointment);
    const formattedDate = sessionDateTimeInfo.formattedDate;
    const formattedTime = sessionDateTimeInfo.formattedTime;
    
    const subject = `Consent Required - Upcoming Session - ${appointment.name}`;
    const body = `
<h2>📋 Consent Required for Your Upcoming Session</h2>
<p>Dear ${appointment.name},</p>

<p>Your consultation session is approaching. Before we can proceed, we need your consent for the session.</p>

<h3>📅 Session Details:</h3>
<div style="background: #f8f9fa; padding: 15px; border-radius: 8px; margin: 15px 0; border-left: 4px solid #007bff;">
  <p><strong>Date:</strong> ${formattedDate}</p>
  <p><strong>Time:</strong> ${formattedTime}</p>
  <p><strong>Duration:</strong> 1 hour</p>
  <p><strong>Type:</strong> ${appointment['session-type'] || appointment.sessionType || appointment['sessiontype'] || appointment['Type of Session *'] || 'Not specified'}</p>
</div>

<h3>⚠️ Important:</h3>
<div style="background: #fff3cd; padding: 15px; border-radius: 8px; margin: 15px 0; border-left: 4px solid #ffc107;">
  <p style="margin: 0; font-size: 14px; color: #856404;">
    <strong>Please provide your consent before the session starts by clicking the button below.</strong>
  </p>
</div>

<h3>🔒 Consent Declaration:</h3>
<p>By giving consent, you acknowledge that:</p>
<ul style="line-height: 1.6;">
  <li>You agree to participate in this consultation session</li>
  <li>You understand the nature and scope of the consultation services</li>
  <li>You have reviewed our privacy policy and terms of service</li>
  <li>You consent to the recording/documentation of the session if applicable</li>
</ul>

<div style="text-align: center; margin: 30px 0;">
  <a href="${consentUrl}" style="background: #28a745; color: white; padding: 15px 30px; text-decoration: none; border-radius: 8px; font-size: 16px; font-weight: 600; display: inline-block;">
    ✅ Give Consent
  </a>
</div>



${actionData && actionData.notes ? `
<h3>📝 Additional Notes:</h3>
<div style="background: #e3f2fd; padding: 15px; border-radius: 8px; margin: 15px 0;">
  <p style="margin: 0;">${actionData.notes}</p>
</div>
` : ''}

<p>If you have any questions or concerns, please contact us immediately.</p>

<p>Best regards,<br>
${CONFIG.FROM_NAME}<br>
📧 ${CONFIG.OWNER_EMAIL}</p>
    `;
    
    // Send the email
    MailApp.sendEmail({
      to: appointment.email,
      subject: subject,
      htmlBody: body
    });
    
    console.log('Consent email sent successfully to:', appointment.email);
    
    return {
      status: 'success',
      consentUrl: consentUrl
    };
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error sending consent email:', error);
    throw error;
  }
}

/**
 * Send session reminder email to client
 */
function sendSessionReminderEmail(appointment, actionData) {
  try {
    console.log('sendSessionReminderEmail called');
    
    const sessionDateTimeInfo = getFormattedSessionDateTime(appointment);
    const appointmentDateTime = sessionDateTimeInfo.appointmentDateTime;

    let formattedDate = sessionDateTimeInfo.formattedDate;
    let formattedTime = sessionDateTimeInfo.formattedTime;
    let timeRemaining = '';
    
    if (appointmentDateTime && !isNaN(appointmentDateTime.getTime())) {
      if (formattedDate === 'Not specified') {
        formattedDate = formatDateForDisplay(appointmentDateTime);
      }
      if (formattedTime === 'Not specified') {
        formattedTime = formatTimeForDisplay(appointmentDateTime);
      }
      
      // Calculate time remaining
      const now = new Date();
      const timeDiff = appointmentDateTime - now;
      const hoursRemaining = Math.floor(timeDiff / (1000 * 60 * 60));
      const minutesRemaining = Math.floor((timeDiff % (1000 * 60 * 60)) / (1000 * 60));
      
      if (timeDiff > 0) {
        if (hoursRemaining > 24) {
          const daysRemaining = Math.floor(hoursRemaining / 24);
          timeRemaining = `${daysRemaining} day(s) and ${hoursRemaining % 24} hour(s)`;
        } else if (hoursRemaining > 0) {
          timeRemaining = `${hoursRemaining} hour(s) and ${minutesRemaining} minute(s)`;
        } else {
          timeRemaining = `${minutesRemaining} minute(s)`;
        }
      } else {
        timeRemaining = 'Session time has passed';
      }
    }
    
    const subject = `Session Reminder - Starting Soon! - ${appointment.name}`;
    const body = `
<h2>🚀 Session Starting Soon!</h2>
<p>Dear ${appointment.name},</p>

<p>This is a friendly reminder that your consultation session is starting soon.</p>

<h3>📅 Session Details:</h3>
<div style="background: #e3f2fd; padding: 20px; border-radius: 8px; margin: 20px 0; border-left: 4px solid #2196f3;">
  <p><strong>📅 Date:</strong> ${formattedDate}</p>
  <p><strong>⏰ Time:</strong> ${formattedTime}</p>
  <p><strong>⏳ Time Remaining:</strong> ${timeRemaining}</p>
  <p><strong>📋 Type:</strong> ${appointment['session-type'] || appointment.sessionType || appointment['sessiontype'] || appointment['Type of Session *'] || 'Not specified'}</p>
  <p><strong>👤 Consultant:</strong> Anurag Sharma</p>
</div>

<h3>⚠️ Important Reminders:</h3>
<div style="background: #fff3cd; padding: 20px; border-radius: 8px; margin: 20px 0; border-left: 4px solid #ffc107;">
  <ul style="margin: 0; padding-left: 20px; line-height: 1.8;">
    <li><strong>🕐 Join Early:</strong> Please join the session <strong>5-10 minutes before</strong> the scheduled time to avoid any delays</li>
    <li><strong>🌐 Check Connection:</strong> Ensure you have a stable internet connection</li>
    <li><strong>📝 Prepare Questions:</strong> Have your discussion points and questions ready</li>
    <li><strong>📱 Test Audio/Video:</strong> Check your microphone and camera beforehand</li>
    <li><strong>🔇 Quiet Environment:</strong> Find a quiet space for the best consultation experience</li>
  </ul>
</div>

<h3>📞 Meeting Access:</h3>
<div style="background: #d4edda; padding: 20px; border-radius: 8px; margin: 20px 0; border-left: 4px solid #28a745;">
  <p style="margin: 0;">
    <strong>📧 Meeting Link:</strong> Check your email for the Google Calendar invitation with the meeting link.<br>
    <strong>📅 Calendar:</strong> The meeting details have been added to your calendar.<br>
    <strong>🔔 Notifications:</strong> Enable calendar notifications so you don't miss the session.
  </p>
</div>

${actionData && actionData.notes ? `
<h3>📝 Additional Notes from Consultant:</h3>
<div style="background: #f8f9fa; padding: 20px; border-radius: 8px; margin: 20px 0; border-left: 4px solid #6c757d;">
  <p style="margin: 0; font-style: italic;">"${actionData.notes}"</p>
</div>
` : ''}

<h3>🆘 Need Help?</h3>
<p>If you have any technical issues or need to reschedule:</p>
<ul style="line-height: 1.6;">
  <li>📧 Email us immediately: <a href="mailto:${CONFIG.OWNER_EMAIL}">${CONFIG.OWNER_EMAIL}</a></li>
  <li>📱 Contact us as soon as possible for urgent matters</li>
</ul>

<div style="background: #e8f5e8; padding: 20px; border-radius: 8px; margin: 30px 0; text-align: center; border-left: 4px solid #28a745;">
  <p style="margin: 0; font-size: 18px; font-weight: 600; color: #155724;">
    🎯 We're excited to speak with you and help you achieve your objectives!
  </p>
</div>

<p>Looking forward to our consultation session!</p>

<p>Best regards,<br>
${CONFIG.FROM_NAME}<br>
📧 ${CONFIG.OWNER_EMAIL}</p>

<hr style="margin: 30px 0; border: none; border-top: 1px solid #eee;">
<p style="font-size: 12px; color: #666; text-align: center;">
  This is an automated reminder for your scheduled consultation session.<br>
  Anurag Sharma - Strategic Consultation Services
</p>
    `;
    
    // Send the email
    MailApp.sendEmail({
      to: appointment.email,
      subject: subject,
      htmlBody: body
    });
    
    console.log('Session reminder email sent successfully to:', appointment.email);
    
    return {
      status: 'success',
      message: 'Session reminder sent successfully'
    };
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error sending session reminder email:', error);
    throw error;
  }
}

/**
 * Show payment proof upload form
 */
function showPaymentUploadForm(appointmentId) {
  try {
    // Check if payment proof already uploaded
    const existingResponse = getClientResponseStatus(appointmentId);
    if (existingResponse === 'Payment Proof Uploaded') {
      return showPaymentAlreadyUploadedPage(appointmentId);
    }
    
    const scriptUrl = getPublicWebAppUrl();
    
    const htmlTemplate = HtmlService.createTemplate(`
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
  <title>Upload Payment Proof - Anurag Sharma Consultation</title>
  <meta charset="utf-8">
  <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1">
  <style>
    body { 
      font-family: 'Segoe UI', Tahoma, Geneva, Verdana, sans-serif; 
      background: linear-gradient(135deg, #667eea 0%, #764ba2 100%);
      min-height: 100vh;
      margin: 0;
      display: flex;
      align-items: center;
      justify-content: center;
      padding: 20px;
    }
    .container {
      background: white;
      padding: 40px;
      border-radius: 15px;
      box-shadow: 0 10px 30px rgba(0,0,0,0.2);
      max-width: 500px;
      width: 100%;
    }
    .title {
      color: #333;
      font-size: 24px;
      font-weight: 600;
      margin-bottom: 20px;
      text-align: center;
    }
    .message { 
      font-size: 16px; 
      line-height: 1.6; 
      color: #555; 
      margin-bottom: 20px;
      text-align: center;
    }
    .form-group {
      margin-bottom: 20px;
    }
    label {
      display: block;
      margin-bottom: 8px;
      font-weight: 600;
      color: #333;
    }
    input[type="file"] {
      width: 100%;
      padding: 12px;
      border: 2px dashed #ddd;
      border-radius: 8px;
      background: #f8f9fa;
      cursor: pointer;
    }
    input[type="file"]:hover {
      border-color: #0d6efd;
      background: #e3f2fd;
    }
    .submit-btn {
      width: 100%;
      padding: 12px;
      background: #28a745;
      color: white;
      border: none;
      border-radius: 8px;
      font-size: 16px;
      font-weight: 600;
      cursor: pointer;
      transition: background 0.3s;
    }
    .submit-btn:hover {
      background: #218838;
    }
    .submit-btn:disabled {
      background: #6c757d;
      cursor: not-allowed;
    }
    .file-info {
      font-size: 14px;
      color: #666;
      margin-top: 8px;
    }
    .loading {
      display: none;
      text-align: center;
      margin-top: 20px;
    }
    .spinner {
      border: 4px solid #f3f3f3;
      border-top: 4px solid #0d6efd;
      border-radius: 50%;
      width: 40px;
      height: 40px;
      animation: spin 1s linear infinite;
      margin: 0 auto 10px;
    }
    @keyframes spin {
      0% { transform: rotate(0deg); }
      100% { transform: rotate(360deg); }
    }
    .success-icon {
      font-size: 48px;
      color: #28a745;
      text-align: center;
      margin-bottom: 20px;
    }
    .error-icon {
      font-size: 48px;
      color: #d32f2f;
      text-align: center;
      margin-bottom: 20px;
    }
  </style>
</head>
<body>
  <div class="container">
    <div class="title">💳 Upload Payment Proof</div>
    <div class="message">
      <p>Please upload your payment proof document.</p>
      <p>Accepted formats: PDF, JPG, PNG (Max 10MB)</p>
    </div>
    
    <form id="uploadForm">
      <input type="hidden" name="action" value="uploadPaymentProof">
      <input type="hidden" name="appointmentId" value="${appointmentId}">
      
      <div class="form-group">
        <label for="paymentFile">Payment Proof Document:</label>
        <input type="file" id="paymentFile" name="paymentFile" accept=".pdf,.jpg,.jpeg,.png" required>
        <div class="file-info">
          Maximum file size: 10MB. Supported formats: PDF, JPG, PNG
        </div>
      </div>
      
      <button type="submit" class="submit-btn" id="submitBtn">
        📤 Upload Payment Proof
      </button>
    </form>
    
    <div class="loading" id="loading">
      <div class="spinner"></div>
      <p>Uploading your payment proof...</p>
    </div>
  </div>

  <script>
    document.getElementById('uploadForm').addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      
      const fileInput = document.getElementById('paymentFile');
      const file = fileInput.files[0];
      
      if (!file) {
        alert('Please select a file to upload.');
        return;
      }
      
      // Check file size (10MB limit)
      if (file.size > 10 * 1024 * 1024) {
        alert('File size must be less than 10MB.');
        return;
      }
      
      // Check file type
      const allowedTypes = ['application/pdf', 'image/jpeg', 'image/jpg', 'image/png'];
      if (!allowedTypes.includes(file.type)) {
        alert('Please upload a PDF, JPG, or PNG file.');
        return;
      }
      
      // Show loading
      document.getElementById('uploadForm').style.display = 'none';
      document.getElementById('loading').style.display = 'block';
      
      // Convert file to base64
      const reader = new FileReader();
      reader.onload = function(e) {
        const base64Data = e.target.result.split(',')[1];
        
        // Prepare form data
        const formData = new FormData();
        formData.append('action', 'uploadPaymentProof');
        formData.append('appointmentId', '${appointmentId}');
        formData.append('fileName', file.name);
        formData.append('fileType', file.type);
        formData.append('fileData', base64Data);
        
        // Submit to Google Apps Script
        fetch('${scriptUrl}', {
          method: 'POST',
          body: formData
        })
        .then(response => response.text())
        .then(data => {
          console.log('Server response:', data);
          
          // Try to parse response as JSON
          let result;
          try {
            result = JSON.parse(data);
          } catch (parseError) {
            console.error('Failed to parse response as JSON:', parseError);
            // If can't parse as JSON, treat as error
            throw new Error('Invalid server response format');
          }
          
          // Check if upload was successful
          if (result.status === 'success') {
            // Show success page
            document.body.innerHTML = \`
              <div class="container">
                <div class="success-icon">✅</div>
                <div class="title">Upload Successful!</div>
                <div class="message">
                  <p>Your payment proof has been uploaded successfully.</p>
                  <p>Your status has been updated to <strong>"Payment Proof Uploaded"</strong>.</p>
                  <p>We will review your payment and contact you soon.</p>
                </div>
              </div>
            \`;
          } else {
            // Show error message from server
            throw new Error(result.message || 'Upload failed');
          }
        })
        .catch(error => {
          console.error('Error:', error);
          
          // Show error page instead of just alert
          document.body.innerHTML = \`
            <div class="container">
              <div class="error-icon">❌</div>
              <div class="title">Upload Failed!</div>
              <div class="message">
                <p style="color: #d32f2f;">\${error.message || 'Upload failed. Please try again.'}</p>
                <button onclick="window.location.href = window.location.href" style="
                  background: #1976d2; 
                  color: white; 
                  border: none; 
                  padding: 12px 24px; 
                  border-radius: 5px; 
                  cursor: pointer; 
                  margin-top: 15px;
                ">Try Again</button>
              </div>
            </div>
          \`;
        });
      };
      
      reader.readAsDataURL(file);
    });
    
    // Update file info when file is selected
    document.getElementById('paymentFile').addEventListener('change', function(e) {
      const file = e.target.files[0];
      if (file) {
        const sizeInMB = (file.size / (1024 * 1024)).toFixed(2);
        document.querySelector('.file-info').textContent = 
          \`Selected: \${file.name} (\${sizeInMB}MB)\`;
      }
    });
  </script>
</body>
</html>`);
    
    return htmlTemplate.evaluate()
      .setTitle('Upload Payment Proof')
      .setXFrameOptionsMode(HtmlService.XFrameOptionsMode.ALLOWALL);
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error showing payment upload form:', error);
    return createCORSResponse({
      status: 'error',
      message: error.toString()
    });
  }
}

/**
 * Handle payment proof upload
 */
function handlePaymentProofUpload(params) {
  try {
    console.log('handlePaymentProofUpload called with params:', params);
    
    const { appointmentId, fileName, fileType, fileData } = params;
    
    if (!appointmentId || !fileName || !fileData) {
      return createCORSResponse({
        status: 'error',
        message: 'Missing required upload parameters'
      });
    }
    
    // Check if already uploaded
    const existingResponse = getClientResponseStatus(appointmentId);
    if (existingResponse === 'Payment Proof Uploaded') {
      return createCORSResponse({
        status: 'error',
        message: 'Payment proof already uploaded'
      });
    }
    
    // Get appointment details for file naming
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = spreadsheet.getActiveSheet();
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    
    if (data.length <= 1) {
      return createCORSResponse({
        status: 'error',
        message: 'No appointment data found'
      });
    }
    
    const headers = data[0];
    const rowIndex = findRowIndexBySessionId(appointmentId);
    
    if (rowIndex < 2 || rowIndex > data.length) {
      return createCORSResponse({
        status: 'error',
        message: 'Invalid appointment ID'
      });
    }
    
    const row = data[rowIndex - 1];
    const appointment = {};
    headers.forEach((header, index) => {
      const fieldKey = getFieldKey(header);
      appointment[fieldKey] = row[index] || '';
    });
    appointment.rowIndex = rowIndex;
    
    // Get proper appointment ID for file naming
    const properAppointmentId = getAppointmentId(appointment);
    
    // Create file in Google Drive with proper Session ID format
    const fileBlob = Utilities.newBlob(
      Utilities.base64Decode(fileData),
      fileType,
      `${properAppointmentId}_${appointment.name}_${fileName}`
    );
    
    // Save to Drive folder with comprehensive error handling and fallback
    let driveFile;
    let uploadLocation = 'payment folder';
    
    try {
      // First, test basic Drive access
      console.log('Testing Drive access...');
      const rootFolder = DriveApp.getRootFolder(); // This will fail if no Drive access
      console.log('Drive access confirmed');
      
      // Try to upload to specific payment folder first
      try {
        console.log('Accessing payment folder...');
        const folder = DriveApp.getFolderById(CONFIG.PAYMENT_PROOF_FOLDER_ID);
        console.log('Creating file in payment folder...');
        driveFile = folder.createFile(fileBlob);
        console.log('File uploaded successfully to payment folder:', driveFile.getId());
      } catch (folderError) {
        console.log('Payment folder failed, trying root folder fallback...');
        console.error('Folder error:', folderError.message);
        
        // Fallback: Create file in root folder with clear naming
        const fallbackFileName = `PAYMENT_PROOF_${properAppointmentId}_${appointment.name}_${fileName}`;
        const fallbackBlob = Utilities.newBlob(
          Utilities.base64Decode(fileData),
          fileType,
          fallbackFileName
        );
        
        driveFile = rootFolder.createFile(fallbackBlob);
        uploadLocation = 'root folder (fallback)';
        console.log('File uploaded successfully to root folder:', driveFile.getId());
      }
      
    } catch (driveError) {
      console.error('Complete Drive failure:', driveError);
      console.error('Error type:', driveError.name);
      console.error('Error message:', driveError.message);
      
      // Provide specific error messages based on the error type
      let errorMessage = 'Complete Drive access failure.';
      
      if (driveError.message.includes('Access denied') || driveError.message.includes('Permission denied')) {
        errorMessage = 'Google Apps Script has no Drive permissions. Go to Google Apps Script → Run authorizeDriveAccess() function → Accept ALL permissions → Redeploy web app.';
      } else {
        errorMessage = `Drive system error: ${driveError.message}. Contact admin for assistance.`;
      }
      
      return createCORSResponse({
        status: 'error',
        message: errorMessage
      });
    }
    
    // Update client status in spreadsheet (without passing file ID to query field)
    updateClientStatus(appointmentId, 'Payment Proof Uploaded', null);
    
    // Update payment proof hyperlink in separate column
    updatePaymentProofLink(appointmentId, driveFile.getId(), fileName);
    
    // Send notification email to admin
    sendPaymentProofNotificationEmail(appointment, driveFile);
    
    return createCORSResponse({
      status: 'success',
      message: `Payment proof uploaded successfully to ${uploadLocation}`,
      fileId: driveFile.getId(),
      uploadLocation: uploadLocation
    });
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error handling payment proof upload:', error);
    return createCORSResponse({
      status: 'error',
      message: error.toString()
    });
  }
}

/**
 * Show consent form for client
 */
function showConsentForm(appointmentId) {
  try {
    // Check if consent already given
    const existingResponse = getClientResponseStatus(appointmentId);
    if (existingResponse === 'Consent Given') {
      return showConsentAlreadyGivenPage(appointmentId);
    }
    
    // Get appointment details for display
    const appointment = getAppointmentData(appointmentId);
    if (!appointment) {
      return createConsentErrorResponse('Appointment not found');
    }
    
    const scriptUrl = getPublicWebAppUrl();
    
    // Parse the appointment date and time for display with better debugging
    const selectedDate = appointment['selected-date'] || appointment.selectedDate || appointment['selectedDate'] || appointment['Selected Date'];
    const selectedTime = appointment['selected-time'] || appointment.selectedTime || appointment['selectedTime'] || appointment['Selected Time'];
    const selectedSlot = appointment['selected-slot'] || appointment.selectedSlot || appointment['selectedSlot'] || appointment['Selected Slot'];
    
    console.log('Date/Time Debug - selectedDate:', selectedDate);
    console.log('Date/Time Debug - selectedTime:', selectedTime);
    console.log('Date/Time Debug - selectedSlot:', selectedSlot);
    console.log('Date/Time Debug - all appointment keys:', Object.keys(appointment));
    
    let appointmentDateTime;
    let formattedDate = 'Not specified';
    let formattedTime = 'Not specified';
    
    // Strategy 1: Try parsing from separate date and time fields
    if (selectedDate && selectedTime && selectedDate !== 'N/A' && selectedTime !== 'N/A') {
      try {
        // Clean the date and time values
        let cleanDate = selectedDate.toString().trim();
        let cleanTime = selectedTime.toString().trim();
        
        // Handle date formats
        if (cleanDate.includes('/')) {
          // Convert MM/DD/YYYY to YYYY-MM-DD
          const dateParts = cleanDate.split('/');
          if (dateParts.length === 3) {
            cleanDate = `${dateParts[2]}-${dateParts[0].padStart(2, '0')}-${dateParts[1].padStart(2, '0')}`;
          }
        }
        
        // Parse the combined date and time
        appointmentDateTime = new Date(`${cleanDate}T${cleanTime}`);
        
        if (!isNaN(appointmentDateTime.getTime())) {
          console.log('Successfully parsed from separate date/time:', appointmentDateTime);
          formattedDate = appointmentDateTime.toLocaleDateString('en-US', {
            weekday: 'short',
            year: 'numeric',
            month: 'short',
            day: 'numeric'
          });
          formattedTime = appointmentDateTime.toLocaleTimeString('en-US', {
            hour: '2-digit',
            minute: '2-digit',
            hour12: true
          });
        }
      } catch (e) {
        console.log('Failed to parse from separate date/time:', e);
      }
    }
    
    // Strategy 2: Try parsing from selectedSlot if separate date/time failed
    if ((!appointmentDateTime || isNaN(appointmentDateTime.getTime())) && selectedSlot && selectedSlot !== 'N/A') {
      try {
        let slotValue = selectedSlot.toString().trim();
        
        // Try to extract date and time from various slot formats
        // Format: "YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS" or "YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM"
        let slotMatch = slotValue.match(/(\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2})\s+(\d{1,2}:\d{2})/);
        
        if (!slotMatch) {
          // Try format: "MM/DD/YYYY HH:MM"
          slotMatch = slotValue.match(/(\d{1,2}\/\d{1,2}\/\d{4})\s+(\d{1,2}:\d{2})/);
          if (slotMatch) {
            // Convert MM/DD/YYYY to YYYY-MM-DD
            const dateParts = slotMatch[1].split('/');
            slotMatch[1] = `${dateParts[2]}-${dateParts[0].padStart(2, '0')}-${dateParts[1].padStart(2, '0')}`;
          }
        }
        
        if (slotMatch) {
          appointmentDateTime = new Date(`${slotMatch[1]}T${slotMatch[2]}`);
          console.log('Parsed from selectedSlot pattern:', appointmentDateTime);
        } else {
          // Try direct parsing after cleaning
          slotValue = slotValue.replace(/IST|GMT\+\d{4}|GMT.*?\)/g, '').trim();
          appointmentDateTime = new Date(slotValue);
          console.log('Direct parsed from cleaned selectedSlot:', appointmentDateTime);
        }
        
        if (appointmentDateTime && !isNaN(appointmentDateTime.getTime())) {
          formattedDate = appointmentDateTime.toLocaleDateString('en-US', {
            weekday: 'short',
            year: 'numeric',
            month: 'short',
            day: 'numeric'
          });
          formattedTime = appointmentDateTime.toLocaleTimeString('en-US', {
            hour: '2-digit',
            minute: '2-digit',
            hour12: true
          });
        }
      } catch (e) {
        console.log('Failed to parse from selectedSlot:', e);
      }
    }
    
    // Strategy 3: Fallback to raw values with basic formatting
    if ((!appointmentDateTime || isNaN(appointmentDateTime.getTime()))) {
      console.log('Using fallback formatting');
      
      if (selectedDate && selectedDate !== 'N/A') {
        try {
          const fallbackDate = new Date(selectedDate);
          if (!isNaN(fallbackDate.getTime())) {
            formattedDate = fallbackDate.toLocaleDateString('en-US', {
              weekday: 'short',
              year: 'numeric',
              month: 'short',
              day: 'numeric'
            });
          } else {
            formattedDate = selectedDate.toString();
          }
        } catch (e) {
          formattedDate = selectedDate.toString();
        }
      }
      
      if (selectedTime && selectedTime !== 'N/A') {
        try {
          // Try to parse time and format it properly
          const timeMatch = selectedTime.toString().match(/(\d{1,2}):(\d{2})/);
          if (timeMatch) {
            const hours = parseInt(timeMatch[1]);
            const minutes = parseInt(timeMatch[2]);
            const timeObj = new Date();
            timeObj.setHours(hours, minutes, 0, 0);
            formattedTime = timeObj.toLocaleTimeString('en-US', {
              hour: '2-digit',
              minute: '2-digit',
              hour12: true
            });
          } else {
            formattedTime = selectedTime.toString();
          }
        } catch (e) {
          formattedTime = selectedTime.toString();
        }
      }
      
      console.log('Fallback formatting - Date:', formattedDate, 'Time:', formattedTime);
    }
    
    const htmlTemplate = HtmlService.createTemplate(`
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
  <title>Session Consent - Anurag Sharma Consultation</title>
  <meta charset="utf-8">
  <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1">
  <style>
    body { 
      font-family: 'Segoe UI', Tahoma, Geneva, Verdana, sans-serif; 
      background: linear-gradient(135deg, #667eea 0%, #764ba2 100%);
      min-height: 100vh;
      margin: 0;
      display: flex;
      align-items: center;
      justify-content: center;
      padding: 15px;
    }
    .container {
      background: white;
      padding: 25px;
      border-radius: 12px;
      box-shadow: 0 8px 25px rgba(0,0,0,0.15);
      max-width: 550px;
      width: 100%;
    }
    .icon {
      font-size: 36px;
      text-align: center;
      margin-bottom: 15px;
    }
    .title {
      color: #333;
      font-size: 24px;
      font-weight: 600;
      margin-bottom: 15px;
      text-align: center;
    }
    .session-details {
      background: #f8f9fa;
      padding: 15px;
      border-radius: 6px;
      margin: 15px 0;
      border-left: 4px solid #007bff;
    }
    .session-details h3 {
      margin: 0 0 10px 0;
      color: #007bff;
      font-size: 16px;
    }
    .session-details p {
      margin: 5px 0;
      font-size: 14px;
    }
    .consent-section {
      background: #e8f5e8;
      padding: 15px;
      border-radius: 6px;
      margin: 15px 0;
      border-left: 4px solid #28a745;
    }
    .consent-section h3 {
      margin: 0 0 10px 0;
      color: #28a745;
      font-size: 16px;
    }
    .consent-section p {
      margin: 8px 0;
      font-size: 14px;
    }
    .consent-list {
      list-style: none;
      padding: 0;
      margin: 10px 0;
    }
    .consent-list li {
      padding: 4px 0;
      font-size: 13px;
      line-height: 1.4;
    }
    .consent-list li::before {
      content: "✓ ";
      color: #28a745;
      font-weight: bold;
      margin-right: 6px;
    }
    .checkbox-container {
      display: flex;
      align-items: flex-start;
      margin: 15px 0;
      padding: 12px;
      background: #fff3cd;
      border-radius: 6px;
      border-left: 4px solid #ffc107;
    }
    .checkbox-container input[type="checkbox"] {
      margin-right: 10px;
      margin-top: 2px;
      transform: scale(1.1);
      flex-shrink: 0;
    }
    .checkbox-container label {
      font-weight: 500;
      color: #856404;
      cursor: pointer;
      font-size: 13px;
      line-height: 1.4;
    }
    .consent-btn {
      width: 100%;
      padding: 12px;
      background: #28a745;
      color: white;
      border: none;
      border-radius: 6px;
      font-size: 16px;
      font-weight: 600;
      cursor: pointer;
      transition: all 0.3s;
      margin-top: 15px;
    }
    .consent-btn:hover:not(:disabled) {
      background: #218838;
      transform: translateY(-1px);
      box-shadow: 0 3px 10px rgba(40, 167, 69, 0.3);
    }
    .consent-btn:disabled {
      background: #6c757d;
      cursor: not-allowed;
      transform: none;
      box-shadow: none;
    }
    .footer {
      text-align: center;
      font-size: 12px;
      color: #666;
      margin-top: 20px;
      padding-top: 15px;
      border-top: 1px solid #eee;
    }
    .loading {
      display: none;
      text-align: center;
      margin-top: 15px;
    }
    .spinner {
      border: 3px solid #f3f3f3;
      border-top: 3px solid #28a745;
      border-radius: 50%;
      width: 30px;
      height: 30px;
      animation: spin 1s linear infinite;
      margin: 0 auto 8px;
    }
    @keyframes spin {
      0% { transform: rotate(0deg); }
      100% { transform: rotate(360deg); }
    }
    /* Mobile responsiveness */
    @media (max-width: 600px) {
      .container {
        padding: 20px;
        margin: 10px;
      }
      .title {
        font-size: 20px;
      }
      .session-details h3, .consent-section h3 {
        font-size: 15px;
      }
    }
  </style>
</head>
<body>
  <div class="container">
    <div class="icon">📋</div>
    <div class="title">Session Consent</div>
    
    <div class="session-details">
      <h3>📅 Your Session Details</h3>
      <p><strong>Client Name:</strong> <?= clientName ?></p>
      <p><strong>Date:</strong> <?= sessionDate ?></p>
      <p><strong>Time:</strong> <?= sessionTime ?></p>
      <p><strong>Type:</strong> <?= sessionType ?></p>
    </div>
    
    <div class="consent-section">
      <h3>🔒 Consent Declaration</h3>
      <p>By providing your consent, you acknowledge and agree to the following:</p>
      <ul class="consent-list">
        <li>You agree to participate in this consultation session</li>
        <li>You understand the nature and scope of the consultation services</li>
        <li>You have reviewed our privacy policy and terms of service</li>
        <li>You consent to the recording/documentation of the session if applicable</li>
        <li>You understand that the consultation is for informational purposes</li>
        <li>You agree to maintain confidentiality of sensitive information shared</li>
      </ul>
    </div>
    
    <form id="consentForm">
      <input type="hidden" name="action" value="giveConsent">
      <input type="hidden" name="appointmentId" value="<?= appointmentId ?>">
      
      <div class="checkbox-container">
        <input type="checkbox" id="consentCheckbox" required>
        <label for="consentCheckbox">
          I have read, understood, and agree to all the terms mentioned above. I hereby give my consent for the consultation session.
        </label>
      </div>
      
      <button type="submit" class="consent-btn" id="consentBtn" disabled>
        ✅ Give Consent and Proceed
      </button>
    </form>
    
    <div class="loading" id="loading">
      <div class="spinner"></div>
      <p>Processing your consent...</p>
    </div>
    
    <div class="footer">
      <p>Anurag Sharma - Strategic Consultation Services</p>
      <p>For support, contact: <?= supportEmail ?></p>
    </div>
  </div>

  <script>
    const consentCheckbox = document.getElementById('consentCheckbox');
    const consentBtn = document.getElementById('consentBtn');
    
    // Enable/disable button based on checkbox
    consentCheckbox.addEventListener('change', function() {
      consentBtn.disabled = !this.checked;
    });
    
    // Handle form submission
    document.getElementById('consentForm').addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      
      if (!consentCheckbox.checked) {
        alert('Please check the consent box to proceed.');
        return;
      }
      
      // Show loading
      document.getElementById('consentForm').style.display = 'none';
      document.getElementById('loading').style.display = 'block';
      
      // Prepare form data
      const formData = new FormData();
      formData.append('action', 'giveConsent');
      formData.append('appointmentId', '<?= appointmentId ?>');
      formData.append('timestamp', new Date().toISOString());
      
      // Submit consent
      fetch('<?= scriptUrl ?>', {
        method: 'POST',
        body: formData
      })
      .then(response => response.text())
      .then(data => {
        // Show success page
        document.body.innerHTML = \`
          <div class="container">
            <div class="icon" style="color: #28a745;">✅</div>
            <div class="title">Consent Given Successfully!</div>
            <div style="text-align: center; padding: 20px;">
              <p style="font-size: 18px; margin-bottom: 20px;">
                Thank you for providing your consent.
              </p>
              <p style="font-size: 16px; color: #666;">
                Your consent has been recorded and your status has been updated to 
                <strong style="color: #28a745;">"Consent Given"</strong>.
              </p>
              <p style="margin-top: 30px;">
                You're all set for your consultation session. We look forward to speaking with you!
              </p>
            </div>
            <div class="footer">
              <p>Anurag Sharma - Strategic Consultation Services</p>
            </div>
          </div>
        \`;
      })
      .catch(error => {
        console.error('Error:', error);
        alert('Error processing consent. Please try again.');
        document.getElementById('consentForm').style.display = 'block';
        document.getElementById('loading').style.display = 'none';
      });
    });
  </script>
</body>
</html>`);
    
    htmlTemplate.appointmentId = appointmentId;
    htmlTemplate.clientName = appointment.name || appointment['name'] || appointment['Full Name *'] || 'N/A';
    htmlTemplate.sessionDate = formattedDate;
    htmlTemplate.sessionTime = formattedTime;
    htmlTemplate.sessionType = appointment['session-type'] || appointment.sessionType || appointment['sessiontype'] || appointment['Type of Session *'] || 'Not specified';
    htmlTemplate.supportEmail = CONFIG.OWNER_EMAIL;
    htmlTemplate.scriptUrl = scriptUrl;
    
    return htmlTemplate.evaluate()
      .setTitle('Session Consent')
      .setXFrameOptionsMode(HtmlService.XFrameOptionsMode.ALLOWALL);
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error showing consent form:', error);
    return createConsentErrorResponse(error.toString());
  }
}

/**
 * Handle consent submission
 */
function handleConsentSubmission(params) {
  try {
    console.log('handleConsentSubmission called with:', params);
    
    const { appointmentId, timestamp } = params;
    
    if (!appointmentId) {
      console.error('Missing appointment ID');
      return createConsentErrorResponse('Missing appointment ID');
    }
    
    // Check if consent already given
    const existingResponse = getClientResponseStatus(appointmentId);
    if (existingResponse === 'Consent Given') {
      return showConsentAlreadyGivenPage(appointmentId);
    }
    
    console.log('Updating client status to Consent Given...');
    
    // Update client status in spreadsheet
    try {
      updateClientStatus(appointmentId, 'Consent Given', timestamp || new Date().toISOString());
      console.log('Client status updated successfully');
    } catch (statusError) {
      console.error('Error updating client status:', statusError);
      return createConsentErrorResponse('Error updating consent status');
    }
    
    console.log('Sending notification to admin...');
    
    // Send notification to admin
    try {
      sendConsentNotificationToAdmin(appointmentId);
      console.log('Admin notification sent successfully');
    } catch (notificationError) {
      console.error('Error sending admin notification:', notificationError);
      // Continue to show success even if notification fails
    }
    
    // Return success response
    return createCORSResponse({
      status: 'success',
      message: 'Consent given successfully'
    });
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error handling consent submission:', error);
    return createConsentErrorResponse(error.toString());
  }
}
