/**
 * Send consent notification to admin
 */
function sendConsentNotificationToAdmin(appointmentId) {
  try {
    console.log('sendConsentNotificationToAdmin called:', { appointmentId });
    
    const appointment = getAppointmentData(appointmentId);
    if (!appointment) {
      console.error('No appointment data found for consent notification');
      return;
    }
    
    // Get properly formatted client name
    const clientName = appointment.name || appointment['name'] || appointment['Full Name *'] || 'Unknown';
    
    // Get properly formatted session type
    const sessionType = appointment['session-type'] || appointment.sessionType || appointment['sessiontype'] || appointment['Type of Session *'] || 'Not specified';
    
    const sessionDateTimeInfo = getFormattedSessionDateTime(appointment);
    const formattedDateTime = sessionDateTimeInfo.formattedDateTime;
    
    const subject = `Client Consent Given - ${clientName}`;
    const body = `
<h2>✅ Client Consent Received</h2>
<p>A client has provided consent for their upcoming session:</p>

<h3>Client Details:</h3>
<p><strong>Name:</strong> ${clientName}</p>
<p><strong>Email:</strong> ${appointment.email || appointment['email'] || appointment['Email Address *'] || 'Unknown'}</p>
<p><strong>Country Code:</strong> ${appointment['country-code'] || appointment.countryCode || appointment['Country Code *'] || 'Not specified'}</p>
<p><strong>Phone:</strong> ${appointment.phone || appointment['phone'] || appointment['Phone Number *'] || 'Not specified'}</p>
<p><strong>Organization:</strong> ${appointment.organization || appointment['organization'] || appointment['Organization *'] || 'Unknown'}</p>
<p><strong>Session ID:</strong> ${appointment.sessionId || appointment['Session ID'] || 'Not specified'}</p>

<h3>Session Details:</h3>
<div style="background: #f8f9fa; padding: 15px; border-radius: 8px; margin: 15px 0; border-left: 4px solid #007bff;">
  <p><strong>Session Type:</strong> ${sessionType}</p>
  <p><strong>Scheduled Date & Time:</strong> ${formattedDateTime}</p>
</div>

<h3>Status Update:</h3>
<div style="background: #d4edda; padding: 15px; border-radius: 8px; margin: 15px 0; border-left: 4px solid #28a745;">
  <p style="margin: 0; color: #155724;">
    <strong>✅ Client Status:</strong> Consent Given
  </p>
</div>

<p>The client is now ready for their consultation session.</p>

<p><a href="http://theanuragsharma.com/admin-login.html" style="background: #007bff; color: white; padding: 10px 20px; text-decoration: none; border-radius: 5px;">Manage Appointments</a></p>
    `;
    
    MailApp.sendEmail({
      to: CONFIG.OWNER_EMAIL,
      subject: subject,
      htmlBody: body
    });
    
    console.log('Consent notification sent to admin successfully');
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error sending consent notification:', error);
    throw error;
  }
}

/**
 * Create error response for consent submissions
 */
function createConsentErrorResponse(message) {
  const errorHtml = `
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
  <title>Consent Error</title>
  <meta charset="utf-8">
  <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1">
  <style>
    body { 
      font-family: 'Segoe UI', Tahoma, Geneva, Verdana, sans-serif; 
      background: linear-gradient(135deg, #dc3545 0%, #bd2130 100%);
      min-height: 100vh;
      margin: 0;
      display: flex;
      align-items: center;
      justify-content: center;
    }
    .container {
      background: white;
      padding: 40px;
      border-radius: 15px;
      box-shadow: 0 10px 30px rgba(0,0,0,0.2);
      max-width: 500px;
      width: 90%;
      text-align: center;
    }
    .error { 
      color: #dc3545; 
      font-size: 48px; 
      margin-bottom: 20px; 
    }
    .title {
      color: #333;
      font-size: 24px;
      font-weight: 600;
      margin-bottom: 20px;
    }
    .message { 
      font-size: 16px; 
      line-height: 1.6; 
      color: #555; 
      margin-bottom: 30px;
    }
    .retry-btn {
      background: #dc3545;
      color: white;
      padding: 10px 20px;
      text-decoration: none;
      border-radius: 5px;
      display: inline-block;
    }
  </style>
</head>
<body>
  <div class="container">
    <div class="error">❌</div>
    <div class="title">Consent Processing Error</div>
    <div class="message">
      <p>We're sorry, but there was an error processing your consent:</p>
      <p><strong>${message}</strong></p>
      <p>Please try again or contact us directly at ${CONFIG.OWNER_EMAIL}</p>
    </div>
    <a href="javascript:history.back()" class="retry-btn">← Go Back and Try Again</a>
  </div>
</body>
</html>`;

  return HtmlService.createHtmlOutput(errorHtml)
    .setTitle('Consent Error')
    .setXFrameOptionsMode(HtmlService.XFrameOptionsMode.ALLOWALL);
}

/**
 * Send notification email to admin about payment proof upload
 */
function sendPaymentProofNotificationEmail(appointment, driveFile) {
  try {
    // Get the appointment ID to retrieve fresh data
    const appointmentId = getAppointmentId(appointment);
    console.log('sendPaymentProofNotificationEmail using appointmentId:', appointmentId);
    if (!appointmentId) {
      throw new Error("Appointment ID not found in the provided appointment object.");
    }

    // Get fresh, complete data directly from the spreadsheet using the ID
    const freshAppointmentData = getAppointmentData(appointmentId);
    if (!freshAppointmentData) {
        throw new Error(`Could not retrieve fresh data for appointment ID: ${appointmentId}`);
    }

    // --- START OF CORRECTION ---

    const sessionDateTimeInfo = getFormattedSessionDateTime(freshAppointmentData);
    const formattedDateTime = sessionDateTimeInfo.formattedDateTime;

    // --- END OF CORRECTION ---

    // Get other client details from the fresh data
    const clientName = freshAppointmentData['Full Name *'] || 'Unknown Client';
    const sessionType = freshAppointmentData['Type of Session *'] || 'Not specified';
    const clientEmail = freshAppointmentData['Email Address *'] || 'Unknown';
    const clientCountryCode = freshAppointmentData['Country Code *'] || 'Not specified';
    const clientPhone = freshAppointmentData['Phone Number *'] || 'Not specified';


    const subject = `Payment Proof Uploaded - ${clientName}`;
    const fileUrl = `https://drive.google.com/file/d/${driveFile.getId()}/view`;

    const body = `
<h2>Payment Proof Uploaded</h2>

<p>A client has uploaded their payment proof:</p>

<h3>Client Details:</h3>
<p><strong>Name:</strong> ${clientName}</p>
<p><strong>Email:</strong> ${clientEmail}</p>
<p><strong>Country Code:</strong> ${clientCountryCode}</p>
<p><strong>Phone:</strong> ${clientPhone}</p>
<p><strong>Session Type:</strong> ${sessionType}</p>
<p><strong>Scheduled Date & Time:</strong> ${formattedDateTime}</p>

<h3>Payment Proof:</h3>
<p><strong>File Name:</strong> ${driveFile.getName()}</p>
<p><strong>View File:</strong> <a href="${fileUrl}" target="_blank">Click here to view payment proof</a></p>

<p>Please review the payment proof and take appropriate action.</p>

<p>Best regards,<br>
${CONFIG.FROM_NAME}<br>
📧 ${CONFIG.OWNER_EMAIL}</p>
    `;

    MailApp.sendEmail({
      to: CONFIG.OWNER_EMAIL,
      subject: subject,
      htmlBody: body
    });

    console.log('Payment proof notification email sent to admin');

  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error sending payment proof notification email:', error);
  }
}

/**

function showFeedbackForm(appointmentId) {
  try {

      return showFeedbackAlreadySubmittedPage(appointmentId);

    if (!appointment) {

    }
    
    const scriptUrl = getPublicWebAppUrl();

      color: #856404;
      font-size: 16px;
    }

      display: flex;
      justify-content: center;
      margin: 15px 0;

    .star {
      font-size: 30px;

  </style>

<body>
  <div class="container">
    <div class="icon">🌟</div>
    <div class="title">Session Feedback</div>
    
    <div class="feedback-section">
      <h3>💭 Your Experience Matters</h3>
      <p>Thank you for your active engagement during the session. It was a pleasure to consult with you.</p>
      <p>I hope you found the inputs useful. Please share your feedback to help us improve our services.</p>
    </div>
    
    <form id="feedbackForm">
      <input type="hidden" name="action" value="submitFeedback">
      <input type="hidden" name="appointmentId" value="<?= appointmentId ?>">
      <input type="hidden" name="rating" id="ratingValue" value="">
      
      <div class="rating-section">
        <h4>⭐ Overall Session Rating</h4>
        <div class="star-rating" id="starRating">
          <span class="star" data-rating="1">☆</span>
          <span class="star" data-rating="2">☆</span>
          <span class="star" data-rating="3">☆</span>
          <span class="star" data-rating="4">☆</span>
          <span class="star" data-rating="5">☆</span>
        </div>
        <p style="text-align: center; font-size: 12px; color: #666; margin: 5px 0;">Click stars to rate your experience</p>
      </div>
      
      <div class="form-group">
        <label for="feedback">Your Feedback:</label>
        <textarea name="feedback" id="feedback" rows="6" maxlength="1000" 
                  placeholder="Please share your thoughts about the session, what was most valuable, and any suggestions for improvement... (Optional)"></textarea>
        <div class="char-count" id="charCount">0 / 200 words</div>
      </div>
      
      <button type="submit" class="feedback-btn" id="feedbackBtn">
        📝 Submit Feedback
      </button>
    </form>
    
    <div class="loading" id="loading">
      <div class="spinner"></div>
      <p>Submitting your feedback...</p>
    </div>
  </div>

  <script>
    let selectedRating = 0;
    
    const stars = document.querySelectorAll('.star');
    const ratingValue = document.getElementById('ratingValue');
    const feedbackTextarea = document.getElementById('feedback');
    const charCount = document.getElementById('charCount');
    const feedbackBtn = document.getElementById('feedbackBtn');
    
    // Star rating functionality
    stars.forEach(star => {
      star.addEventListener('click', function() {
        selectedRating = parseInt(this.dataset.rating);
        ratingValue.value = selectedRating;
        
        // Update star display
        stars.forEach((s, index) => {
          if (index < selectedRating) {
            s.classList.add('active');
            s.textContent = '⭐';
          } else {
            s.classList.remove('active');
            s.textContent = '☆';
          }
        });
        
        updateSubmitButton();
      });
      
      // Add hover effect for preview
      star.addEventListener('mouseenter', function() {
        const hoverRating = parseInt(this.dataset.rating);
        stars.forEach((s, index) => {
          if (index < hoverRating) {
            s.textContent = '⭐';
          } else if (index < selectedRating) {
            s.textContent = '⭐';
          } else {
            s.textContent = '☆';
          }
        });
      });
      
      star.addEventListener('mouseleave', function() {
        // Reset to selected rating
        stars.forEach((s, index) => {
          if (index < selectedRating) {
            s.textContent = '⭐';
          } else {
            s.textContent = '☆';
          }
        });
      });
    });
    
    // Character/word count functionality
    feedbackTextarea.addEventListener('input', function() {
      const words = this.value.trim().split(/\\s+/).filter(word => word.length > 0);
      const wordCount = this.value.trim() === '' ? 0 : words.length;
      charCount.textContent = wordCount + ' / 200 words';
      
      if (wordCount > 200) {
        charCount.style.color = '#dc3545';
        this.setCustomValidity('Feedback must not exceed 200 words');
      } else {
        charCount.style.color = '#666';
        this.setCustomValidity('');
      }
      
      updateSubmitButton();
    });
    
    // Update submit button state (Corrected Version)
    function updateSubmitButton() {
      const hasRating = selectedRating > 0;
      // The feedback word count validation remains, but it's no longer required to enable the button
      const feedbackValid = !feedbackTextarea.validity.customError;
      
      // THE FIX: The button is now enabled as long as a star rating is selected
      // and the (optional) feedback text is not over the word limit.
      feedbackBtn.disabled = !(hasRating && feedbackValid);
    }
    
    // Handle form submission
    document.getElementById('feedbackForm').addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      
      if (selectedRating === 0) {
        alert('Please provide a rating for your session.');
        return;
      }
      
      // Feedback is now optional - no validation needed
      
      // Show loading
      document.getElementById('feedbackForm').style.display = 'none';
      document.getElementById('loading').style.display = 'block';
      
      // Prepare form data
      const formData = new FormData();
      formData.append('action', 'submitFeedback');
      formData.append('appointmentId', '<?= appointmentId ?>');
      formData.append('rating', selectedRating);
      formData.append('feedback', feedbackTextarea.value || ''); // Use empty string if no feedback
      formData.append('timestamp', new Date().toISOString());
      
      // Submit feedback
      fetch('<?= scriptUrl ?>', {
        method: 'POST',
        body: formData
      })
      .then(response => response.text())
      .then(data => {
        // Show success page
        document.body.innerHTML = \`
          <div class="container">
            <div class="icon" style="color: #28a745;">✅</div>
            <div class="title">Feedback Submitted Successfully!</div>
            <div style="text-align: center; padding: 20px;">
              <p style="font-size: 18px; margin-bottom: 20px;">
                Thank you for your valuable feedback!
              </p>
              <p style="font-size: 16px; color: #666;">
                Your feedback has been recorded with a rating of <strong>\${selectedRating} stars</strong>.
              </p>
              <p style="margin-top: 30px;">
                We truly appreciate your time and insights. Your feedback helps us improve our consultation services.
              </p>
              <p style="margin-top: 20px; color: #28a745; font-weight: 600;">
                We look forward to future engagements!
              </p>
            </div>
          </div>
        \`;
      })
      .catch(error => {
        console.error('Error:', error);
        alert('Error submitting feedback. Please try again.');
        document.getElementById('feedbackForm').style.display = 'block';
        document.getElementById('loading').style.display = 'none';
      });
    });
    
    // Initial button state
    updateSubmitButton();
  </script>
</body>
</html>`);
    
    htmlTemplate.appointmentId = appointmentId;
    htmlTemplate.scriptUrl = scriptUrl;
    
    return htmlTemplate.evaluate()
      .setTitle('Session Feedback')
      .setXFrameOptionsMode(HtmlService.XFrameOptionsMode.ALLOWALL);
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error showing feedback form:', error);
    return createFeedbackErrorResponse(error.toString());
  }
}

/**
 * Handle submitted client feedback
 */
function handleFeedbackSubmission(params) {
  try {
    console.log('handleFeedbackSubmission called with:', params);
    
    const { appointmentId, rating, feedback, timestamp } = params;
    
    if (!appointmentId || !rating) {
      console.error('Missing feedback submission parameters');
      return createFeedbackErrorResponse('Missing appointment ID or rating');
    }
    
    // Check if feedback already submitted
    const existingResponse = getClientResponseStatus(appointmentId);
    if (existingResponse === 'Feedback Received') {
      return showFeedbackAlreadySubmittedPage(appointmentId);
    }
    
    // Validate word count only if feedback is provided
    if (feedback && feedback.trim()) {
      const wordCount = feedback.trim().split(/\s+/).filter(word => word.length > 0).length;
      if (wordCount > 200) {
        console.error('Feedback exceeds word limit:', wordCount);
        return createFeedbackErrorResponse('Feedback exceeds 200 words limit');
      }
    }
    
    // Validate rating
    const ratingNum = parseInt(rating);
    if (isNaN(ratingNum) || ratingNum < 1 || ratingNum > 5) {
      console.error('Invalid rating:', rating);
      return createFeedbackErrorResponse('Invalid rating. Please provide a rating between 1-5 stars');
    }
    
    console.log('Updating client status with feedback...');
    
    // Update client status with feedback in spreadsheet
    try {
      const feedbackText = (feedback && feedback.trim()) ? feedback : 'No additional feedback provided';
      const feedbackData = `Rating: ${ratingNum}/5 stars | ${feedbackText}`;
      updateClientFeedback(appointmentId, 'Feedback Received', feedbackData);
      console.log('Client feedback updated successfully');
    } catch (statusError) {
      console.error('Error updating client feedback:', statusError);
      // Continue to send notification even if status update fails
    }
    
    console.log('Sending feedback notification to admin...');
    
    // Send notification to admin
    try {
      sendFeedbackNotificationToAdmin(appointmentId, ratingNum, feedback || 'No additional feedback provided');
      console.log('Admin feedback notification sent successfully');
    } catch (notificationError) {
      console.error('Error sending admin feedback notification:', notificationError);
      // Continue to show success page even if notification fails
    }
    
    // Return success response
    return createCORSResponse({
      status: 'success',
      message: 'Feedback submitted successfully'
    });
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error handling feedback submission:', error);
    return createFeedbackErrorResponse(error.toString());
  }
}

/**
 * Update client feedback in spreadsheet
 */
function updateClientFeedback(appointmentId, status, feedbackData) {
  try {
    console.log('updateClientFeedback called:', { appointmentId, status, feedbackData: !!feedbackData });
    
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = spreadsheet.getActiveSheet();
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    
    if (data.length <= 1) {
      console.error('No appointment data found in spreadsheet');
      return;
    }
    
    const headers = data[0];
    
    // Find the Session ID column index
    let sessionIdColIndex = -1;
    headers.forEach((header, index) => {
      if (header === 'Session ID') {
        sessionIdColIndex = index;
      }
    });
    
    if (sessionIdColIndex === -1) {
      console.error('Session ID column not found in spreadsheet');
      return;
    }
    
    // Find the row with matching Session ID
    let targetRowIndex = -1;
    for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (data[i][sessionIdColIndex] === appointmentId) {
        targetRowIndex = i + 1; // Convert to 1-based index for sheet operations
        break;
      }
    }
    
    if (targetRowIndex === -1) {
      console.error('Appointment with Session ID not found:', appointmentId);
      return;
    }
    
    console.log('Found appointment at row:', targetRowIndex, 'for Session ID:', appointmentId);
    
    // Find the Client Status and Client Feedback column indices
    let clientStatusColIndex = -1;
    let clientFeedbackColIndex = -1;
    
    headers.forEach((header, index) => {
      if (header === 'Client Status') {
        clientStatusColIndex = index;
      }
      if (header === 'Client Feedback') {
        clientFeedbackColIndex = index;
      }
    });
    
    // Add columns if they don't exist
    if (clientStatusColIndex === -1) {
      headers.push('Client Status');
      clientStatusColIndex = headers.length - 1;
      sheet.getRange(1, clientStatusColIndex + 1).setValue('Client Status');
    }
    
    if (clientFeedbackColIndex === -1) {
      headers.push('Client Feedback');
      clientFeedbackColIndex = headers.length - 1;
      sheet.getRange(1, clientFeedbackColIndex + 1).setValue('Client Feedback');
    }
    
    // Update the client status and feedback
    sheet.getRange(targetRowIndex, clientStatusColIndex + 1).setValue(status);
    if (feedbackData && clientFeedbackColIndex !== -1) {
      sheet.getRange(targetRowIndex, clientFeedbackColIndex + 1).setValue(feedbackData);
    }
    
    console.log('Client feedback update completed successfully for row:', targetRowIndex);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error updating client feedback:', error);
    throw error;
  }
}

/**
 * Send feedback notification to admin
 */
function sendFeedbackNotificationToAdmin(appointmentId, rating, feedback) {
  try {
    console.log('sendFeedbackNotificationToAdmin called:', { appointmentId, rating });
    
    const appointment = getAppointmentData(appointmentId);
    if (!appointment) {
      console.error('No appointment data found for feedback notification');
      return;
    }

    // DEBUG: Log the entire appointment object to see what fields are available
    console.log('DEBUG - Full appointment object:', JSON.stringify(appointment, null, 2));
    console.log('DEBUG - Object keys:', Object.keys(appointment));
    
    // Try different approaches to get the data
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = spreadsheet.getActiveSheet();
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const headers = data[0];
    const rowIndex = findRowIndexBySessionId(appointmentId);
    
    console.log('DEBUG - Headers:', headers);
    console.log('DEBUG - Row index:', rowIndex);
    
    if (rowIndex >= 2 && rowIndex <= data.length) {
      const row = data[rowIndex - 1];
      console.log('DEBUG - Raw row data:', row);
      
      // Create appointment object manually to see what we get
      const manualAppointment = {};
      headers.forEach((header, index) => {
        manualAppointment[header] = row[index] || '';
      });
      console.log('DEBUG - Manual appointment object:', JSON.stringify(manualAppointment, null, 2));
    }

    // Get properly formatted client name - try all possible variations
    const clientName = appointment.name || 
                      appointment['name'] || 
                      appointment['Full Name *'] || 
                      manualAppointment?.['Full Name *'] ||
                      'Unknown';
    
    console.log('DEBUG - Client name result:', clientName);
    
    // Get email
    const clientEmail = appointment.email || 
                       appointment['email'] || 
                       appointment['Email Address *'] || 
                       manualAppointment?.['Email Address *'] ||
                       'Unknown';
    
    console.log('DEBUG - Client email result:', clientEmail);
    
    // Get other fields
    const clientCountryCode = appointment['country-code'] || 
                             appointment.countryCode || 
                             appointment['Country Code *'] || 
                             manualAppointment?.['Country Code *'] ||
                             'Not specified';
    
    const clientPhone = appointment.phone || 
                       appointment['phone'] || 
                       appointment['Phone Number *'] || 
                       manualAppointment?.['Phone Number *'] ||
                       'Not specified';
    
    const clientOrganization = appointment.organization || 
                              appointment['organization'] || 
                              appointment['Organization *'] || 
                              manualAppointment?.['Organization *'] ||
                              'Unknown';
    
    const sessionType = appointment['session-type'] || 
                       appointment.sessionType || 
                       appointment['sessiontype'] || 
                       appointment['Type of Session *'] || 
                       manualAppointment?.['Type of Session *'] ||
                       'Not specified';

    const subject = `Client Feedback Received (${rating}/5 stars) - ${clientName}`;
    const body = `
<h2>⭐ Client Feedback Received</h2>
<p>A client has submitted feedback for their consultation session:</p>

<h3>Client Details:</h3>
<p><strong>Name:</strong> ${clientName}</p>
<p><strong>Email:</strong> ${clientEmail}</p>
<p><strong>Country Code:</strong> ${clientCountryCode}</p>
<p><strong>Phone:</strong> ${clientPhone}</p>
<p><strong>Organization:</strong> ${clientOrganization}</p>
<p><strong>Session ID:</strong> ${appointment.sessionId || appointment['Session ID'] || 'Not specified'}</p>
<p><strong>Session Type:</strong> ${sessionType}</p><h3>Feedback Details:</h3>
<div style="background: #fff3cd; padding: 15px; border-radius: 8px; margin: 15px 0; border-left: 4px solid #ffc107;">
  <p><strong>Rating:</strong> ${rating}/5 stars ${'⭐'.repeat(rating)}${'☆'.repeat(5-rating)}</p>
</div>

<div style="background: #f8f9fa; padding: 15px; border-radius: 8px; margin: 15px 0; border-left: 4px solid #007bff;">
  <h4>Client Feedback:</h4>
  <p style="margin: 0; font-style: italic;">"${feedback}"</p>
</div>

<h3>Status Update:</h3>
<div style="background: #d4edda; padding: 15px; border-radius: 8px; margin: 15px 0; border-left: 4px solid #28a745;">
  <p style="margin: 0; color: #155724;">
    <strong>✅ Client Status:</strong> Feedback Received
  </p>
</div>

<p>The client's consultation journey is now complete with their valuable feedback.</p>

<p><a href="http://theanuragsharma.com/admin-login.html" style="background: #007bff; color: white; padding: 10px 20px; text-decoration: none; border-radius: 5px;">Manage Appointments</a></p>
    `;
    
    MailApp.sendEmail({
      to: CONFIG.OWNER_EMAIL,
      subject: subject,
      htmlBody: body
    });
    
    console.log('Feedback notification sent to admin successfully');
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error sending feedback notification:', error);
    throw error;
  }
}

    if (data.length > 0) {
      const headers = data[0];
      console.log('✓ Headers found:', headers.length, 'columns');
      console.log('Headers:', headers);
      
      // Check for Client Status and Client Feedback columns
      const clientStatusIndex = headers.indexOf('Client Status');
      const clientFeedbackIndex = headers.indexOf('Client Feedback');
      console.log('Client Status column index:', clientStatusIndex);
      console.log('Client Feedback column index:', clientFeedbackIndex);
      
      // If appointments exist, show their current client status
      if (data.length > 1) {
        console.log('Current appointments client status:');
        for (let i = 1; i < Math.min(data.length, 6); i++) { // Show first 5 appointments
          const row = data[i];
          const name = row[1] || 'Unknown'; // Assuming name is in column 2
          const clientStatus = clientStatusIndex >= 0 ? row[clientStatusIndex] : 'No Status Column';
          const clientFeedback = clientFeedbackIndex >= 0 ? row[clientFeedbackIndex] : 'No Feedback Column';
          console.log(`  Row ${i + 1} (${name}): Status="${clientStatus}", Feedback="${clientFeedback}"`);
        }
      }
    }
    
    // Test 3: Field mapping
    console.log('Test 3: Testing field mapping...');
    const testHeader = 'Client Status';
    const mappedField = getFieldKey(testHeader);
    console.log(`✓ Field mapping: "${testHeader}" -> "${mappedField}"`);

/**
 * Test client query functionality
 */
function testClientQueryFunctionality() {
  try {
    console.log('=== CLIENT QUERY FUNCTIONALITY TEST ===');
    
    // Test 1: Check spreadsheet structure for Client Query column
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = spreadsheet.getActiveSheet();
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    
    if (data.length > 0) {
      const headers = data[0];
      const clientQueryIndex = headers.indexOf('Client Query');
      console.log('Client Query column index:', clientQueryIndex);
      
      if (clientQueryIndex === -1) {
        console.log('Client Query column not found, will be created when needed');
      } else {
        console.log('Client Query column exists at position:', clientQueryIndex + 1);
        
        // Show existing queries if any
        if (data.length > 1) {
          console.log('Existing client queries:');
          for (let i = 1; i < Math.min(data.length, 6); i++) {
            const row = data[i];
            const name = row[1] || 'Unknown';
            const query = row[clientQueryIndex] || 'No query';
            console.log(`  Row ${i + 1} (${name}): "${query}"`);
          }
        }
      }
    }
    
    // Test 2: Test updateClientStatus function with query
    if (data.length > 1) {
      console.log('Test 2: Testing updateClientStatus with query...');
      const testRowIndex = 2;
      const testQuery = 'Test query from debug function';
      
      try {
        updateClientStatus(testRowIndex, 'Query', testQuery);
        console.log('✓ updateClientStatus with query executed successfully');
        
        // Read back the updated data
        const updatedData = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
        const updatedHeaders = updatedData[0];
        const queryColIndex = updatedHeaders.indexOf('Client Query');
        const statusColIndex = updatedHeaders.indexOf('Client Status');
        
        if (queryColIndex >= 0) {
          const queryValue = updatedData[1][queryColIndex];
          console.log('Query value written:', queryValue);
        }
        
        if (statusColIndex >= 0) {
          const statusValue = updatedData[1][statusColIndex];
          console.log('Status value written:', statusValue);
        }
        
        // Clean up - restore original values
        updateClientStatus(testRowIndex, 'Pending', '');
        console.log('Test data cleaned up');
        
      } catch (updateError) {
        console.error('! updateClientStatus with query failed:', updateError);
      }
    }
    
    console.log('=== CLIENT QUERY FUNCTIONALITY TEST COMPLETED ===');
    return 'Client query test completed successfully. Check logs for details.';
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('=== CLIENT QUERY FUNCTIONALITY TEST FAILED ===');
    console.error('Error:', error.toString());
    return `Client query test failed: ${error.toString()}`;
  }
}

  }

/**
 * Date Blocking Management Functions
 * ==================================
 */

/**
 * Handle blocking dates
 */
function handleBlockDates(params) {
  try {
    console.log('handleBlockDates called with params:', params);
    
    const startDate = params.startDate;
    const endDate = params.endDate;
    const reason = params.reason || 'Date blocked by admin';
    
    console.log('Parsed parameters:', { startDate, endDate, reason });
    
    if (!startDate) {
      console.log('Error: Start date is required');
      return createCORSResponse({
        success: false,
        error: 'Start date is required'
      });
    }
    
    // Get or create blocked dates sheet
    const blockedDatesSheet = getOrCreateBlockedDatesSheet();
    console.log('Got blocked dates sheet');
    
    // Generate unique ID for this blocked date range
    const blockId = Utilities.getUuid();
    console.log('Generated block ID:', blockId);
    
    // Add blocked date entry
    const timestamp = new Date();
    blockedDatesSheet.appendRow([
      blockId,
      startDate,
      endDate,
      reason,
      timestamp,
      'Admin'
    ]);
    
    console.log('Blocked dates successfully:', { startDate, endDate, reason });
    
    return createCORSResponse({
      success: true,
      message: 'Dates blocked successfully'
    });
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error blocking dates:', error);
    return createCORSResponse({
      success: false,
      error: error.toString()
    });
  }
}

/**
 * Handle unblocking dates
 */
function handleUnblockDate(params) {
  try {
    console.log('handleUnblockDate called with params:', params);
    
    const dateId = params.dateId;
    console.log('Parsed dateId:', dateId);
    
    if (!dateId) {
      console.log('Error: Date ID is required');
      return createCORSResponse({
        success: false,
        error: 'Date ID is required'
      });
    }
    
    const blockedDatesSheet = getOrCreateBlockedDatesSheet();
    const data = blockedDatesSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    console.log('Got blocked dates data, rows:', data.length);
    
    // Find and remove the blocked date row
    for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (data[i][0] === dateId || data[i][1] === dateId) { // Check both ID and start date
        console.log('Found matching row at index:', i);
        blockedDatesSheet.deleteRow(i + 1);
        console.log('Unblocked date successfully:', dateId);
        
        return createCORSResponse({
          success: true,
          message: 'Date unblocked successfully'
        });
      }
    }
    
    console.log('Blocked date not found:', dateId);
    return createCORSResponse({
      success: false,
      error: 'Blocked date not found'
    });
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error unblocking date:', error);
    return createCORSResponse({
      success: false,
      error: error.toString()
    });
  }
}

/**
 * Get all blocked dates
 */
function getBlockedDates() {
  try {
    const blockedDatesSheet = getOrCreateBlockedDatesSheet();
    const data = blockedDatesSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    
    if (data.length <= 1) {
      return createCORSResponse({
        success: true,
        data: []
      });
    }
    
    const headers = data[0];
    const blockedDates = [];
    
    for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
      const row = data[i];
      if (row[0] && row[1]) { // Has ID and start date
        // **FIX: Convert dates to YYYY-MM-DD strings to prevent timezone conversion**
        let startDateStr, endDateStr;
        
        if (row[1] instanceof Date) {
          const year = row[1].getFullYear();
          const month = String(row[1].getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');
          const day = String(row[1].getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
          startDateStr = `${year}-${month}-${day}`;
        } else {
          startDateStr = row[1].toString().split('T')[0];
        }
        
        if (row[2]) {
          if (row[2] instanceof Date) {
            const year = row[2].getFullYear();
            const month = String(row[2].getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');
            const day = String(row[2].getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
            endDateStr = `${year}-${month}-${day}`;
          } else {
            endDateStr = row[2].toString().split('T')[0];
          }
        } else {
          endDateStr = startDateStr;
        }
        
        blockedDates.push({
          id: row[0],
          startDate: startDateStr,
          endDate: endDateStr,
          reason: row[3] || 'No reason provided',
          createdAt: row[4],
          createdBy: row[5] || 'Admin'
        });
      }
    }
    
    // Sort by start date (newest first)
    blockedDates.sort((a, b) => new Date(b.startDate) - new Date(a.startDate));
    
    return createCORSResponse({
      success: true,
      data: blockedDates
    });
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error getting blocked dates:', error);
    return createCORSResponse({
      success: false,
      error: error.toString(),
      data: []
    });
  }
}

/**
 * Get or create blocked dates sheet
 */
function getOrCreateBlockedDatesSheet() {
  const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
  let blockedDatesSheet = spreadsheet.getSheetByName('Blocked Dates');
  
  if (!blockedDatesSheet) {
    // Create new sheet for blocked dates
    blockedDatesSheet = spreadsheet.insertSheet('Blocked Dates');
    
    // Set up headers
    const headers = [
      'ID',
      'Start Date',
      'End Date',
      'Reason',
      'Created At',
      'Created By'
    ];
    
    blockedDatesSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length).setValues([headers]);
    
    // Format headers
    const headerRange = blockedDatesSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length);
    headerRange.setBackground('#4285f4');
    headerRange.setFontColor('#ffffff');
    headerRange.setFontWeight('bold');
    
    console.log('Created new Blocked Dates sheet');
  }
  
  return blockedDatesSheet;
}

/**
 * Check if a date is blocked
 * This function can be used by the booking system to validate date availability
 */
function isDateBlocked(dateToCheck) {
  try {
    const blockedDatesSheet = getOrCreateBlockedDatesSheet();
    const data = blockedDatesSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    
    if (data.length <= 1) {
      return false; // No blocked dates
    }
    
    const checkDate = new Date(dateToCheck);
    
    for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
      const row = data[i];
      const startDate = new Date(row[1]);
      const endDate = row[2] ? new Date(row[2]) : startDate;
      
      // Check if the date falls within the blocked range
      if (checkDate >= startDate && checkDate <= endDate) {
        return true;
      }
    }
    
    return false;
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error checking if date is blocked:', error);
    return false; // Default to not blocked on error
  }
}

/**
 * Handle unblocking specific dates from a range
 */
function handleUnblockSpecificDates(params) {
  try {
    console.log('handleUnblockSpecificDates called with params:', params);
    
    const rangeId = params.rangeId;
    const selectedDates = JSON.parse(params.selectedDates || '[]');
    
    console.log('Parsed parameters:', { rangeId, selectedDates });
    
    if (!rangeId || !selectedDates.length) {
      console.log('Error: Range ID and selected dates are required');
      return createCORSResponse({
        success: false,
        error: 'Range ID and selected dates are required'
      });
    }
    
    const blockedDatesSheet = getOrCreateBlockedDatesSheet();
    const data = blockedDatesSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    
    // Find the range to modify
    let rangeRowIndex = -1;
    let rangeData = null;
    
    for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (data[i][0] === rangeId) {
        rangeRowIndex = i;
        rangeData = data[i];
        break;
      }
    }
    
    if (rangeRowIndex === -1) {
      console.log('Range not found:', rangeId);
      return createCORSResponse({
        success: false,
        error: 'Blocked date range not found'
      });
    }
    
    console.log('Found range at row:', rangeRowIndex, 'Data:', rangeData);
    
    const originalStartDate = new Date(rangeData[1]);
    const originalEndDate = new Date(rangeData[2] || rangeData[1]);
    const reason = rangeData[3];
    
    // Generate all dates in the original range
    const allDatesInRange = [];
    for (let d = new Date(originalStartDate); d <= originalEndDate; d.setDate(d.getDate() + 1)) {
      allDatesInRange.push(d.toISOString().split('T')[0]);
    }
    
    // Find dates that should remain blocked
    const remainingBlockedDates = allDatesInRange.filter(date => !selectedDates.includes(date));
    
    console.log('Original range dates:', allDatesInRange);
    console.log('Dates to unblock:', selectedDates);
    console.log('Remaining blocked dates:', remainingBlockedDates);
    
    // Delete the original range
    blockedDatesSheet.deleteRow(rangeRowIndex + 1);
    
    // Create new entries for remaining blocked dates if any
    if (remainingBlockedDates.length > 0) {
      // Group consecutive dates into ranges
      const newRanges = groupConsecutiveDates(remainingBlockedDates);
      
      console.log('New ranges to create:', newRanges);
      
      // Add new blocked date entries for each range
      newRanges.forEach(range => {
        const newBlockId = Utilities.getUuid();
        const timestamp = new Date();
        
        blockedDatesSheet.appendRow([
          newBlockId,
          range.start,
          range.end,
          reason + ' (Modified)',
          timestamp,
          'Admin'
        ]);
      });
    }
    
    console.log('Successfully unblocked specific dates:', selectedDates);
    
    return createCORSResponse({
      success: true,
      message: `Successfully unblocked ${selectedDates.length} date(s)`
    });
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error unblocking specific dates:', error);
    return createCORSResponse({
      success: false,
      error: error.toString()
    });
  }
}

/**
 * Handle manual unblocking of dates (independent of existing blocked ranges)
 */
/**
 * Group consecutive dates into ranges
 */
function groupConsecutiveDates(dates) {
  if (!dates.length) return [];
  
  // Sort dates
  const sortedDates = dates.sort();
  const ranges = [];
  let currentRangeStart = sortedDates[0];
  let currentRangeEnd = sortedDates[0];
  
  for (let i = 1; i < sortedDates.length; i++) {
    const currentDate = new Date(sortedDates[i]);
    const previousDate = new Date(sortedDates[i - 1]);
    
    // Check if current date is consecutive to previous
    const daysDiff = (currentDate - previousDate) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24);
    
    if (daysDiff === 1) {
      // Extend current range
      currentRangeEnd = sortedDates[i];
    } else {
      // Start new range
      ranges.push({
        start: currentRangeStart,
        end: currentRangeStart === currentRangeEnd ? currentRangeStart : currentRangeEnd
      });
      currentRangeStart = sortedDates[i];
      currentRangeEnd = sortedDates[i];
    }
  }
  
  // Add the last range
  ranges.push({
    start: currentRangeStart,
    end: currentRangeStart === currentRangeEnd ? currentRangeStart : currentRangeEnd
  });
  
  return ranges;
}

// Helper function to format dates for comparison
function formatDateForComparison(date) {
  if (!date) return '';
  
  // If it's already a string in YYYY-MM-DD format, return as is
  if (typeof date === 'string' && date.match(/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/)) {
    return date;
  }
  
  // If it's a Date object, convert to YYYY-MM-DD
  if (date instanceof Date) {
    return date.toISOString().split('T')[0];
  }
  
  // Try to parse as date and convert
  try {
    const parsedDate = new Date(date);
    if (isNaN(parsedDate.getTime())) {
      return date.toString(); // Return original if can't parse
    }
    return parsedDate.toISOString().split('T')[0];
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error formatting date:', error);
    return date.toString();
  }
}

// Simple handler for manual unblock of a single date
function handleManualUnblockDate(params) {
  try {
    console.log('handleManualUnblockDate called with params:', params);
    
    if (!params.date) {
      throw new Error('No date provided for unblocking');
    }
    
    const dateToUnblock = params.date;
    console.log('Attempting to unblock date:', dateToUnblock);
    
    // Get the correct spreadsheet by ID (not by name)
    const spreadsheet = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SHEET_ID);
    let sheet = spreadsheet.getSheetByName(BLOCKED_DATES_SHEET);
    
    if (!sheet) {
      // Create the blocked dates sheet if it doesn't exist
      sheet = spreadsheet.insertSheet(BLOCKED_DATES_SHEET);
      
      // Set up headers
      const headers = [
        'ID',
        'Start Date', 
        'End Date',
        'Reason',
        'Created At',
        'Created By'
      ];
      sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length).setValues([headers]);
      
      return ContentService.createTextOutput(
        JSON.stringify({
          success: false,
          error: 'No blocked dates found. Blocked dates sheet was created.'
        })
      ).setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON);
    }
    
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    
    if (data.length <= 1) {
      return ContentService.createTextOutput(
        JSON.stringify({
          success: false,
          error: 'No blocked dates found'
        })
      ).setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON);
    }
    
    // Find and remove the specific date
    let dateFound = false;
    const updatedData = [data[0]]; // Keep header row
    
    for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
      const startDate = formatDateForComparison(data[i][1]); // Start Date is column B (index 1)
      const endDate = formatDateForComparison(data[i][2]);   // End Date is column C (index 2)
      const targetDate = formatDateForComparison(dateToUnblock);
      
      console.log(`Checking row ${i}: startDate=${startDate}, endDate=${endDate}, targetDate=${targetDate}`);
      
      // Check if target date falls within this blocked range
      if (startDate === targetDate || endDate === targetDate || 
          (endDate && targetDate >= startDate && targetDate <= endDate)) {
        
        dateFound = true;
        console.log('Found date in range, processing row:', data[i]);
        
        // If it's a single date (start === end) or target matches start/end exactly
        if (!endDate || endDate === '' || startDate === endDate) {
          // Single date - just remove it completely
          console.log('Removing single date:', startDate);
          // Skip this row (don't add to updatedData)
        } else if (startDate === targetDate && endDate !== targetDate) {
          // Target is the start date of a range - keep the rest of the range
          const nextDay = new Date(targetDate);
          nextDay.setDate(nextDay.getDate() + 1);
          const newStartDate = nextDay.toISOString().split('T')[0];
          
          console.log(`Splitting range: removing start date ${targetDate}, new range: ${newStartDate} to ${endDate}`);
          
          // Create new row with updated start date
          const newRow = [...data[i]];
          newRow[1] = newStartDate; // Update start date
          updatedData.push(newRow);
          
        } else if (endDate === targetDate && startDate !== targetDate) {
          // Target is the end date of a range - keep the beginning of the range
          const prevDay = new Date(targetDate);
          prevDay.setDate(prevDay.getDate() - 1);
          const newEndDate = prevDay.toISOString().split('T')[0];
          
          console.log(`Splitting range: removing end date ${targetDate}, new range: ${startDate} to ${newEndDate}`);
          
          // Create new row with updated end date
          const newRow = [...data[i]];
          newRow[2] = newEndDate; // Update end date
          updatedData.push(newRow);
          
        } else {
          // Target is in the middle of a range - split into two ranges
          const prevDay = new Date(targetDate);
          prevDay.setDate(prevDay.getDate() - 1);
          const nextDay = new Date(targetDate);
          nextDay.setDate(nextDay.getDate() + 1);
          
          const beforeEndDate = prevDay.toISOString().split('T')[0];
          const afterStartDate = nextDay.toISOString().split('T')[0];
          
          console.log(`Splitting range: removing middle date ${targetDate}`);
          console.log(`New range 1: ${startDate} to ${beforeEndDate}`);
          console.log(`New range 2: ${afterStartDate} to ${endDate}`);
          
          // Create first range (before target date)
          if (startDate <= beforeEndDate) {
            const firstRow = [...data[i]];
            firstRow[2] = beforeEndDate; // Update end date
            updatedData.push(firstRow);
          }
          
          // Create second range (after target date)
          if (afterStartDate <= endDate) {
            const secondRow = [...data[i]];
            secondRow[1] = afterStartDate; // Update start date
            // Generate new ID for the second range
            secondRow[0] = data[i][0] + '_split_' + Date.now();
            updatedData.push(secondRow);
          }
        }
      } else {
        // Date not in this range - keep the row as is
        updatedData.push(data[i]);
      }
    }
    
    if (!dateFound) {
      return ContentService.createTextOutput(
        JSON.stringify({
          success: false,
          error: 'Date not found in blocked dates list'
        })
      ).setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON);
    }
    
    // Clear the sheet and write updated data
    sheet.clear();
    if (updatedData.length > 0) {
      sheet.getRange(1, 1, updatedData.length, updatedData[0].length).setValues(updatedData);
    }
    
    console.log('Successfully unblocked date:', dateToUnblock);
    
    return ContentService.createTextOutput(
      JSON.stringify({
        success: true,
        message: `Successfully unblocked date: ${dateToUnblock}`
      })
    ).setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON);
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error in handleManualUnblockDate:', error);
    return ContentService.createTextOutput(
      JSON.stringify({
        success: false,
        error: error.toString()
      })
    ).setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON);
  }
}

/**
 * Get available dates from the sheet
 */
function getAvailableDates() {
  try {
    const availableDatesSheet = getOrCreateAvailableDatesSheet();
    const data = availableDatesSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    
    if (data.length <= 1) {
      return createCORSResponse({
        success: true,
        data: []
      });
    }
    
    const headers = data[0];
    const availableDates = [];
    
    for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
      const row = data[i];
      if (row[0] && row[1]) { // Has ID and date
        // **FIX: Convert date to YYYY-MM-DD string to prevent timezone conversion**
        let dateStr;
        if (row[1] instanceof Date) {
          // If it's a Date object, format it using local timezone
          const year = row[1].getFullYear();
          const month = String(row[1].getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');
          const day = String(row[1].getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
          dateStr = `${year}-${month}-${day}`;
        } else {
          // If it's already a string, use it as-is
          dateStr = row[1].toString().split('T')[0]; // Remove time component if present
        }
        
        availableDates.push({
          id: row[0],
          date: dateStr,
          reason: row[2] || 'Manually made available',
          createdAt: row[3],
          createdBy: row[4] || 'Admin'
        });
      }
    }
    
    // Sort by date (newest first)
    availableDates.sort((a, b) => new Date(b.date) - new Date(a.date));
    
    return createCORSResponse({
      success: true,
      data: availableDates
    });
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error getting available dates:', error);
    return createCORSResponse({
      success: false,
      error: error.toString(),
      data: []
    });
  }
}

/**
 * Handle making multiple dates available
 */
function handleMakeMultipleDatesAvailable(params) {
  try {
    console.log('handleMakeMultipleDatesAvailable called with params:', params);
    
    let dates;
    const reason = params.reason || 'Dates made available by admin';
    
    // Handle dates parameter - could be JSON string or array
    if (params.dates) {
      if (typeof params.dates === 'string') {
        try {
          dates = JSON.parse(params.dates);
        } catch (parseError) {
          console.error('Error parsing dates JSON:', parseError);
          return createCORSResponse({
            success: false,
            error: 'Invalid dates format'
          });
        }
      } else if (Array.isArray(params.dates)) {
        dates = params.dates;
      } else {
        dates = [params.dates]; // Single date
      }
    } else {
      // Fallback: check for startDate/endDate (legacy support)
      const startDate = params.startDate;
      const endDate = params.endDate || params.startDate;
      
      if (!startDate) {
        return createCORSResponse({
          success: false,
          error: 'Dates array or start date is required'
        });
      }
      
      // Generate date range
      dates = [];
      const start = new Date(startDate);
      const end = new Date(endDate);
      
      // Create a new date object for each iteration to avoid mutation issues
      const currentDate = new Date(start);
      while (currentDate <= end) {
        dates.push(currentDate.toISOString().split('T')[0]);
        currentDate.setDate(currentDate.getDate() + 1);
      }
    }
    
    console.log('Parsed parameters:', { dates, reason });
    
    if (!dates || !Array.isArray(dates) || dates.length === 0) {
      console.log('Error: Dates array is required');
      return createCORSResponse({
        success: false,
        error: 'Dates array is required'
      });
    }
    
    // Get or create available dates sheet
    const availableDatesSheet = getOrCreateAvailableDatesSheet();
    console.log('Got available dates sheet');
    
    // Get existing dates to check for duplicates
    const existingData = availableDatesSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const existingDates = new Set();
    
    // Skip header row and collect existing dates
    for (let i = 1; i < existingData.length; i++) {
      if (existingData[i][1]) { // Column B contains the date
        existingDates.add(existingData[i][1].toString());
      }
    }
    
    const timestamp = new Date();
    const rowsToAdd = [];
    const duplicates = [];
    const newDates = [];
    
    // Prepare rows to add, filtering out duplicates
    for (const date of dates) {
      if (date && date.trim()) {
        const dateStr = date.trim();
        if (existingDates.has(dateStr)) {
          duplicates.push(dateStr);
        } else {
          const availableId = Utilities.getUuid();
          rowsToAdd.push([
            availableId,
            dateStr,
            reason,
            timestamp,
            'Admin'
          ]);
          newDates.push(dateStr);
          existingDates.add(dateStr); // Add to set to prevent duplicates within this batch
        }
      }
    }
    
    if (rowsToAdd.length > 0) {
      // Add all rows at once for efficiency
      const startRow = availableDatesSheet.getLastRow() + 1;
      availableDatesSheet.getRange(startRow, 1, rowsToAdd.length, 5).setValues(rowsToAdd);
      
      console.log('Available dates successfully added:', newDates);
      if (duplicates.length > 0) {
        console.log('Duplicate dates skipped:', duplicates);
      }
      
      let message = `${rowsToAdd.length} date(s) made available successfully`;
      if (duplicates.length > 0) {
        message += `. ${duplicates.length} duplicate(s) skipped: ${duplicates.join(', ')}`;
      }
      
      return createCORSResponse({
        success: true,
        message: message,
        newDates: newDates,
        duplicates: duplicates
      });
    } else if (duplicates.length > 0) {
      return createCORSResponse({
        success: true,
        message: `All ${duplicates.length} date(s) were already available. No new dates added.`,
        newDates: [],
        duplicates: duplicates
      });
    } else {
      return createCORSResponse({
        success: false,
        error: 'No valid dates provided'
      });
    }
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error making multiple dates available:', error);
    return createCORSResponse({
      success: false,
      error: error.toString()
    });
  }
}

/**
 * Handle making a single date available
 */
function handleMakeDateAvailable(params) {
  try {
    console.log('handleMakeDateAvailable called with params:', params);
    
    const dateInput = params.date;
    const reason = params.reason || 'Date made available by admin';
    
    if (!dateInput || !dateInput.trim()) {
      console.log('Error: Date is required');
      return createCORSResponse({
        success: false,
        error: 'Date is required'
      });
    }
    
    // **FIX: Ensure date is stored in YYYY-MM-DD format without timezone conversion**
    // The input from the frontend is already in YYYY-MM-DD format (from date input field)
    // Just store it as-is without creating a Date object which can cause timezone shifts
    const dateToStore = dateInput.trim();
    
    console.log('Parsed parameters:', { dateToStore, reason });
    
    // Get or create available dates sheet
    const availableDatesSheet = getOrCreateAvailableDatesSheet();
    console.log('Got available dates sheet');
    
    // Check for duplicate
    const existingData = availableDatesSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    for (let i = 1; i < existingData.length; i++) {
      if (existingData[i][1] && existingData[i][1].toString() === dateToStore) {
        console.log('Date already exists:', dateToStore);
        return createCORSResponse({
          success: true,
          message: 'This date is already available',
          duplicate: true
        });
      }
    }
    
    // Generate unique ID for this available date
    const availableId = Utilities.getUuid();
    console.log('Generated available ID:', availableId);
    
    // Add available date entry with timestamp
    const timestamp = new Date();
    availableDatesSheet.appendRow([
      availableId,
      dateToStore,  // Store as YYYY-MM-DD string
      reason,
      timestamp,
      'Admin'
    ]);
    
    console.log('Date made available successfully:', dateToStore);
    
    return createCORSResponse({
      success: true,
      message: 'Date made available successfully'
    });
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error making date available:', error);
    return createCORSResponse({
      success: false,
      error: error.toString()
    });
  }
}

/**
 * Handle removing an available date
 */
function handleRemoveAvailableDate(params) {
  try {
    console.log('handleRemoveAvailableDate called with params:', params);
    
    const dateId = params.dateId;
    
    if (!dateId) {
      return createCORSResponse({
        success: false,
        error: 'Date ID is required'
      });
    }
    
    // Get available dates sheet
    const availableDatesSheet = getOrCreateAvailableDatesSheet();
    const data = availableDatesSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    
    if (data.length <= 1) {
      return createCORSResponse({
        success: false,
        error: 'No available dates found'
      });
    }
    
    // Find and remove the row with matching ID
    let foundRow = -1;
    for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (data[i][0] === dateId) {
        foundRow = i + 1; // Sheet rows are 1-indexed
        break;
      }
    }
    
    if (foundRow === -1) {
      return createCORSResponse({
        success: false,
        error: 'Available date not found'
      });
    }
    
    // Delete the row
    availableDatesSheet.deleteRow(foundRow);
    
    console.log('Available date removed successfully:', dateId);
    
    return createCORSResponse({
      success: true,
      message: 'Available date removed successfully'
    });
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error removing available date:', error);
    return createCORSResponse({
      success: false,
      error: error.toString()
    });
  }
}

 * Get or create Booked Sessions sheet
 */

/**
 * Get or create available dates sheet
 */
function getOrCreateAvailableDatesSheet() {
  const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
  let availableDatesSheet = spreadsheet.getSheetByName(AVAILABLE_DATES_SHEET);
  
  if (!availableDatesSheet) {
    // Create new sheet for available dates
    availableDatesSheet = spreadsheet.insertSheet(AVAILABLE_DATES_SHEET);
    
    // Set up headers
    const headers = [
      'ID',
      'Date',
      'Reason',
      'Created At',
      'Created By'
    ];
    
    availableDatesSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length).setValues([headers]);
    
    // Format headers
    const headerRange = availableDatesSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length);
    headerRange.setBackground('#28a745');
    headerRange.setFontColor('#ffffff');
    headerRange.setFontWeight('bold');
    
    console.log('Created new Available Dates sheet');
  }
  
  return availableDatesSheet;
}

                <!-- Calendar will be populated by JavaScript -->

                Select a date to view available times
              </div>

                <div class="no-slots">
                  <i class="fas fa-arrow-left"></i><br>
                  Please select a date from the calendar
