  <script>
    // JavaScript for calendar functionality
    let currentDate = new Date();
    let selectedDate = null;
    let selectedTime = null;
    let availableSlots = {};
    const sessionType = '<?= sessionType ?>';
    const clientLocation = '<?= clientLocation ?>';
    
    // Blocked and Available dates data from server
    // Using <?!= ?> (force-print scriptlet) to avoid HTML escaping of JSON
    // Ensure they are always arrays with fallback
    const blockedDatesData = <?!= JSON.stringify(blockedDates) ?> || [];
    const availableDatesData = <?!= JSON.stringify(availableDates) ?> || [];
    
    /**
     * Converts a Date object to a timezone-safe "YYYY-MM-DD" string.
     * This avoids the UTC conversion issues caused by .toISOString().
     * @param {Date} date The date to convert.
     * @returns {string} The formatted date string.
     */
    function getLocalDateKey(date) {
      const year = date.getFullYear();
      const month = date.getMonth() + 1; // getMonth() is 0-indexed
      const day = date.getDate();

      // Pad with a leading zero if necessary
      const monthPadded = String(month).padStart(2, '0');
      const dayPadded = String(day).padStart(2, '0');

      return year + '-' + monthPadded + '-' + dayPadded;
    }
    
    // Initialize calendar on page load
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
      // Initialize calendar to start from appropriate month based on session type
      const today = new Date();
      const startDaysAfter = (sessionType === 'generalized') ? 3 : 7;
      const minDate = new Date(today);
      minDate.setDate(today.getDate() + startDaysAfter);
      
      // If minimum date is in next month, start calendar from that month
      if (minDate.getMonth() !== today.getMonth() || minDate.getFullYear() !== today.getFullYear()) {
        currentDate = new Date(minDate.getFullYear(), minDate.getMonth(), 1);
      }
      
      initializeCalendar();
      loadAvailabilityData();
      
      // Navigation event listeners with restrictions
      document.getElementById('prevMonth').addEventListener('click', () => {
        const today = new Date();
        const startDaysAfter = (sessionType === 'generalized') ? 3 : 7;
        const minDate = new Date(today);
        minDate.setDate(today.getDate() + startDaysAfter);
        
        const prevMonth = new Date(currentDate);
        prevMonth.setMonth(currentDate.getMonth() - 1);
        
        // Don't allow navigation to months before the minimum allowed date's month
        if (prevMonth.getFullYear() > minDate.getFullYear() || 
            (prevMonth.getFullYear() === minDate.getFullYear() && prevMonth.getMonth() >= minDate.getMonth())) {
          currentDate.setMonth(currentDate.getMonth() - 1);
          updateCalendarDisplay();
        }
      });
      
      document.getElementById('nextMonth').addEventListener('click', () => {
        const today = new Date();
        const maxDate = new Date(today);
        maxDate.setMonth(today.getMonth() + 3); // Allow up to 3 months ahead
        
        const nextMonth = new Date(currentDate);
        nextMonth.setMonth(currentDate.getMonth() + 1);
        
        // Don't allow navigation beyond 3 months from today
        if (nextMonth.getFullYear() < maxDate.getFullYear() || 
            (nextMonth.getFullYear() === maxDate.getFullYear() && nextMonth.getMonth() <= maxDate.getMonth())) {
          currentDate.setMonth(currentDate.getMonth() + 1);
          updateCalendarDisplay();
        }
      });
      
      // Form submission
      document.getElementById('rescheduleForm').addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        
        if (!selectedDate || !selectedTime) {
          alert('Please select both a date and time for your new appointment.');
          return;
        }
        
        const submitBtn = document.getElementById('submitBtn');
        const originalText = submitBtn.innerHTML;
        
        // Show loading state
        submitBtn.disabled = true;
        submitBtn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> Processing...';
        
        // Prepare form data using URLSearchParams for no-cors submission
        const formData = new URLSearchParams();
        formData.append('action', 'submitReschedule');
        formData.append('appointmentId', '<?= appointmentId ?>');
        formData.append('selectedDate', document.getElementById('selectedDate').value);
        formData.append('selectedTime', document.getElementById('selectedTime').value);
        formData.append('selectedSlot', document.getElementById('selectedSlot').value);
        formData.append('additionalNotes', document.getElementById('additionalNotes').value);
        
        fetch('<?= scriptUrl ?>', {
          method: 'POST',
          body: formData,
          mode: 'no-cors'  // Important for external client access
        })
        .then(() => {
          // Because of no-cors, we can't read the response
          // Show success message and redirect after short delay
          submitBtn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-check"></i> Success!';
          submitBtn.style.background = '#28a745';
          
          setTimeout(() => {
            // Show success page
            document.body.innerHTML = createSuccessPageHTML();
          }, 1500);
        })
        .catch(error => {
          console.error('Error submitting reschedule:', error);
          alert('Sorry, there was an error processing your request. Please try again or contact us directly.');
          
          // Restore button
          submitBtn.disabled = false;
          submitBtn.innerHTML = originalText;
        });
      });
    });
    
    function initializeCalendar() {
      const calendarGrid = document.getElementById('calendarGrid');
      
      // Add day headers
      const dayHeaders = ['Sun', 'Mon', 'Tue', 'Wed', 'Thu', 'Fri', 'Sat'];
      dayHeaders.forEach(day => {
        const dayElement = document.createElement('div');
        dayElement.className = 'calendar-day header';
        dayElement.textContent = day;
        calendarGrid.appendChild(dayElement);
      });
      
      updateCalendarDisplay();
    }
    
    function updateCalendarDisplay() {
      const titleElement = document.getElementById('calendarTitle');
      const calendarGrid = document.getElementById('calendarGrid');
      
      // Update month/year title
      const monthNames = ['January', 'February', 'March', 'April', 'May', 'June',
          'July', 'August', 'September', 'October', 'November', 'December'];
      titleElement.textContent = monthNames[currentDate.getMonth()] + ' ' + currentDate.getFullYear();
      
      // Clear previous calendar (keep headers)
      const dayElements = calendarGrid.querySelectorAll('.calendar-day:not(.header)');
      dayElements.forEach(element => element.remove());
      
      // Get first day of month and number of days
      const firstDay = new Date(currentDate.getFullYear(), currentDate.getMonth(), 1);
      const lastDay = new Date(currentDate.getFullYear(), currentDate.getMonth() + 1, 0);
      const daysInMonth = lastDay.getDate();
      const startingDayOfWeek = firstDay.getDay();
      
      const today = new Date();
      today.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
      
      // Calculate minimum allowed date based on session type
      // Same logic as booking page: generalized = 3 days, others = 7 days
      const minDate = new Date(today);
      const startDaysAfter = (sessionType === 'generalized') ? 3 : 7;
      minDate.setDate(today.getDate() + startDaysAfter);
      
      // Add empty cells for days before the first day of month
      for (let i = 0; i < startingDayOfWeek; i++) {
        const emptyDay = document.createElement('div');
        emptyDay.className = 'calendar-day';
        calendarGrid.appendChild(emptyDay);
      }
      
      // Add days of the month
      for (let day = 1; day <= daysInMonth; day++) {
        const dayElement = document.createElement('div');
        dayElement.className = 'calendar-day';
        dayElement.textContent = day;
        
        const currentDateObj = new Date(currentDate.getFullYear(), currentDate.getMonth(), day);
        currentDateObj.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
        const dateString = getLocalDateKey(currentDateObj); // Use local date key to avoid timezone conversion issues
        
        // Check if date is in the past
        if (currentDateObj < today) {
          dayElement.classList.add('past');
          dayElement.title = 'This date is in the past';
        }
        // Check if date is too soon based on session type minimum days requirement
        else if (currentDateObj < minDate) {
          dayElement.classList.add('past');
          dayElement.title = 'Minimum ' + startDaysAfter + ' days advance booking required for this session type';
        }
        // Check availability based on session type rules and blocked/available dates
        else if (isDateAvailable(currentDateObj)) {
          dayElement.classList.add('available');
          dayElement.addEventListener('click', () => selectDate(currentDateObj, dayElement));
        }
        else {
          dayElement.classList.add('blocked');
          dayElement.title = 'This date is not available for booking';
        }
        
        calendarGrid.appendChild(dayElement);
      }
    }
    
    function isDateAvailable(date) {
      const dayOfWeek = date.getDay(); // 0 = Sunday, 6 = Saturday
      
      // STEP 1: If a date is manually made available, it overrides all other rules.
      if (isDateManuallyAvailable(date)) {
        return true;
      }

      // STEP 2: If a date is blocked (and not manually overridden), it is unavailable.
      if (isDateBlocked(date)) {
        return false;
      }

      // STEP 3: Apply default business rules based on the day of the week.
      if (sessionType === 'super-specialized') {
        // For "Super-Specialized" sessions, only weekends (Saturday and Sunday) are available.
        return dayOfWeek === 0 || dayOfWeek === 6;
      } else {
        // For all other session types, only weekdays are available.
        return dayOfWeek !== 0 && dayOfWeek !== 6;
      }
    }
    
    // Helper function to check if date is manually made available
    function isDateManuallyAvailable(date) {
      const dateString = getLocalDateKey(date);
      
      return availableDatesData.some(availableDate => {
        if (availableDate.startDate && availableDate.endDate) {
          return dateString >= availableDate.startDate && dateString <= availableDate.endDate;
        } else if (availableDate.date) {
          return dateString === availableDate.date;
        }
        return false;
      });
    }
    
    // Helper function to check if date is blocked
    function isDateBlocked(date) {
      const dateString = getLocalDateKey(date);
      
      return blockedDatesData.some(blockedDate => {
        if (blockedDate.startDate && blockedDate.endDate) {
          return dateString >= blockedDate.startDate && dateString <= blockedDate.endDate;
        } else if (blockedDate.date) {
          return dateString === blockedDate.date;
        }
        return false;
      });
    }
    
    function selectDate(date, element) {
      // Remove previous selection
      document.querySelectorAll('.calendar-day.selected').forEach(el => {
        el.classList.remove('selected');
      });
      
      // Add selection to clicked element
      element.classList.add('selected');
      selectedDate = date;
      
      // Update form using local date key to avoid timezone conversion issues
      document.getElementById('selectedDate').value = getLocalDateKey(date);
      
      // Update display
      const dateString = date.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { 
        weekday: 'long', 
        year: 'numeric', 
        month: 'long', 
        day: 'numeric' 
      });
      document.getElementById('newDateDisplay').textContent = dateString;
      document.getElementById('newSessionDisplay').style.display = 'block';
      
      // Generate and display time slots
      generateTimeSlots(date);
    }
    
    function generateTimeSlots(date) {
      const timeSlotsContainer = document.getElementById('timeSlots');
      const headerElement = document.getElementById('timeSlotsHeader');
      
      // Update header
      const dateString = date.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { 
        weekday: 'long', 
        month: 'short', 
        day: 'numeric' 
      });
      headerElement.textContent = 'Available times for ' + dateString;
      
      // Clear existing slots
      timeSlotsContainer.innerHTML = '';
      
      // For in-person sessions, show message
      if (sessionType === 'super-specialized' || sessionType === 'long-term-engagement') {
        timeSlotsContainer.innerHTML = '<div class="no-slots"><i class="fas fa-handshake"></i><br>Time will be coordinated for in-person session</div>';
        
        // Auto-select a default time using local date key to avoid timezone conversion issues
        selectedTime = 'TBD';
        document.getElementById('selectedTime').value = 'TBD';
        document.getElementById('selectedSlot').value = getLocalDateKey(date) + '_TBD';
        document.getElementById('newTimeDisplay').textContent = 'To be coordinated';
        document.getElementById('submitBtn').disabled = false;
        return;
      }
      
      // Generate time slots for virtual sessions based on session type
      let timeSlots;
      
      // Use the same time slots as the booking page
      if (sessionType === 'generalized' || sessionType === 'specialized') {
        // Standard consultation time slots
        timeSlots = ['05:00', '07:00', '09:00', '11:00', '14:00', '16:00', '18:00', '20:00', '22:00'];
      } else {
        // Advisory and other session types - more flexible hours
        timeSlots = [
          '09:00', '10:00', '11:00', '12:00', '13:00', '14:00', 
          '15:00', '16:00', '17:00', '18:00', '19:00', '20:00'
        ];
      }
      
      timeSlots.forEach(time => {
        const slotElement = document.createElement('div');
        slotElement.className = 'time-slot';
        slotElement.textContent = formatTime(time);
        
        slotElement.addEventListener('click', () => {
          // Remove previous selection
          timeSlotsContainer.querySelectorAll('.time-slot.selected').forEach(el => {
            el.classList.remove('selected');
          });
          
          // Select this slot
          slotElement.classList.add('selected');
          selectedTime = time;
          
          // Update form using local date key to avoid timezone conversion issues
          document.getElementById('selectedTime').value = time;
          document.getElementById('selectedSlot').value = getLocalDateKey(date) + '_' + time;
          document.getElementById('newTimeDisplay').textContent = formatTime(time);
          document.getElementById('submitBtn').disabled = false;
        });
        
        timeSlotsContainer.appendChild(slotElement);
      });
    }
    
    function formatTime(timeString) {
      const [hours, minutes] = timeString.split(':').map(Number);
      const date = new Date();
      date.setHours(hours, minutes, 0, 0);
      
      return date.toLocaleTimeString('en-US', {
        hour: '2-digit',
        minute: '2-digit',
        hour12: true
      });
    }
    
    function loadAvailabilityData() {
      // This would typically load blocked dates and available dates from the server
      // For now, we'll use the simple logic in isDateAvailable()
      console.log('Loading availability data...');
    }
    
    function createSuccessPageHTML() {
      const newDate = selectedDate ? selectedDate.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { 
        weekday: 'long', 
        year: 'numeric', 
        month: 'long', 
        day: 'numeric' 
      }) : 'Selected Date';
      
      const newTime = selectedTime ? formatTime(selectedTime) : 'Selected Time';
      
      return \`
<div style="
  font-family: 'Segoe UI', Tahoma, Geneva, Verdana, sans-serif;
  background: linear-gradient(135deg, #28a745 0%, #20c997 100%);
  min-height: 100vh;
  margin: 0;
  display: flex;
  align-items: center;
  justify-content: center;
  padding: 20px;
">
  <div style="
    background: white;
    padding: 40px;
    border-radius: 20px;
    box-shadow: 0 20px 60px rgba(0,0,0,0.3);
    max-width: 600px;
    width: 100%;
    text-align: center;
  ">
    <div style="
      color: #28a745;
      font-size: 64px;
      margin-bottom: 20px;
      animation: bounce 1s;
    ">
      ✅
    </div>
    
    <div style="
      color: #333;
      font-size: 28px;
      font-weight: 600;
      margin-bottom: 20px;
    ">
      Session Successfully Rescheduled!
    </div>
    
    <div style="
      font-size: 16px;
      line-height: 1.6;
      color: #555;
      margin-bottom: 30px;
    ">
      <p>Thank you! Your consultation session has been rescheduled.</p>
      <p>You will receive a confirmation email with all the details shortly.</p>
    </div>
    
    <div style="
      background: #e3f2fd;
      padding: 25px;
      border-radius: 12px;
      margin: 25px 0;
      border-left: 5px solid #2196f3;
    ">
      <h3 style="color: #1565c0; margin-bottom: 15px; font-size: 20px;">
        📅 Your New Session
      </h3>
      <div style="margin-bottom: 10px; font-size: 16px;">
        <strong>📅 Date:</strong> \${newDate}
      </div>
      <div style="margin-bottom: 10px; font-size: 16px;">
        <strong>🕒 Time:</strong> \${newTime}
      </div>
      <div style="font-size: 16px;">
        <strong>💼 Session Type:</strong> <?= sessionTypeDisplay ?>
      </div>
    </div>
    
    <div style="
      background: #f8f9fa;
      padding: 20px;
      border-radius: 12px;
      margin: 25px 0;
      text-align: left;
    ">
      <h4 style="color: #333; margin-bottom: 15px; text-align: center;">
        📋 What's Next?
      </h4>
      <ul style="color: #555; line-height: 1.6;">
        <li>Your appointment has been updated in our system</li>
        <li>You'll receive meeting details closer to the session date</li>
        <li>Please update your personal calendar</li>
        <li>Join the session 5-10 minutes early</li>
      </ul>
    </div>
    
    <div style="
      font-size: 14px;
      color: #666;
      border-top: 1px solid #eee;
      padding-top: 20px;
      margin-top: 30px;
    ">
      <p><strong>Anurag Sharma - Strategic Consultation Services</strong></p>
      <p>If you have any questions, please contact us at <strong>theanuragsharma.web@gmail.com</strong></p>
    </div>
  </div>
</div>
\`;
    }
  </script>
</body>
</html>`);
    
    // Set template variables with proper formatting
    htmlTemplate.appointmentId = appointmentId;
    htmlTemplate.scriptUrl = scriptUrl;
    
    // Format date and time properly
    const currentDate = appointment.selectedDate || appointment['Selected Date'] || appointment['selected-date'] || appointment.date;
    const currentTime = appointment.selectedTime || appointment['Selected Time'] || appointment['selected-time'] || appointment.time;
    
    // Get the RAW session type value for calendar logic (keep dashes, lowercase)
    let rawSessionType = appointment['session-type'] || appointment.sessionType || appointment['Session Type'] || appointment['Session-Type'] || appointment.category || '';
    // Normalize to lowercase with dashes for calendar logic
    rawSessionType = rawSessionType.toString().toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, '-');
    
    // Create display version for UI (formatted nicely)
    let sessionCategoryDisplay = rawSessionType;
    if (sessionCategoryDisplay) {
      sessionCategoryDisplay = sessionCategoryDisplay.replace(/-/g, ' ').replace(/\b\w/g, l => l.toUpperCase());
    } else {
      sessionCategoryDisplay = 'General Consultation';
    }
    
    htmlTemplate.currentDate = formatDateForDisplay(currentDate);
    htmlTemplate.currentTime = formatTimeForDisplay(currentTime);
    htmlTemplate.sessionType = rawSessionType;  // RAW value for JavaScript calendar logic
    htmlTemplate.sessionTypeDisplay = sessionCategoryDisplay;  // Formatted value for display
    htmlTemplate.clientLocation = appointment.location || appointment.Location || 'Online';
    
    // Load blocked and available dates data for calendar
    const blockedDatesData = getBlockedDatesFromSheet() || [];
    const availableDatesData = getAvailableDatesFromSheet() || [];
    
    // Pass dates data to the template (ensure they are always arrays)
    htmlTemplate.blockedDates = Array.isArray(blockedDatesData) ? blockedDatesData : [];
    htmlTemplate.availableDates = Array.isArray(availableDatesData) ? availableDatesData : [];
    
    return htmlTemplate.evaluate()
      .setTitle('Reschedule Your Session')
      .setXFrameOptionsMode(HtmlService.XFrameOptionsMode.ALLOWALL);
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error showing reschedule calendar:', error);
    return createRescheduleErrorResponse(error.toString());
  }
}

/**
 * Get blocked dates from BlockedDates sheet for reschedule calendar
 */
function getBlockedDatesFromSheet() {
  try {
    const blockedDatesSheet = getOrCreateSheet('BlockedDates');
    const data = blockedDatesSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const blockedDates = [];
    
    // Skip header row
    for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
      const row = data[i];
      if (row[0] || row[1]) { // If there's data in the first or second column
        const blockedDate = {
          date: row[0] ? convertToDateString(row[0]) : null,
          startDate: row[1] ? convertToDateString(row[1]) : null,
          endDate: row[2] ? convertToDateString(row[2]) : null,
          reason: row[3] ? row[3].toString() : ''
        };
        
        blockedDates.push(blockedDate);
      }
    }
    
    return blockedDates;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error getting blocked dates from sheet:', error);
    return [];
  }
}

/**
 * Get available dates from AvailableDates sheet for reschedule calendar
 */
function getAvailableDatesFromSheet() {
  try {
    const availableDatesSheet = getOrCreateSheet('AvailableDates');
    const data = availableDatesSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const availableDates = [];
    
    // Skip header row
    for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
      const row = data[i];
      if (row[0] || row[1]) { // If there's data in the first or second column
        const availableDate = {
          date: row[0] ? convertToDateString(row[0]) : null,
          startDate: row[1] ? convertToDateString(row[1]) : null,
          endDate: row[2] ? convertToDateString(row[2]) : null,
          reason: row[3] ? row[3].toString() : ''
        };
        
        availableDates.push(availableDate);
      }
    }
    
    return availableDates;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error getting available dates from sheet:', error);
    return [];
  }
}

/**
 * Helper function to convert date values to YYYY-MM-DD string format
 */
function convertToDateString(dateValue) {
  if (!dateValue) return null;
  
  // If it's already a string in correct format, return it
  if (typeof dateValue === 'string' && /^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/.test(dateValue)) {
    return dateValue;
  }
  
  // If it's a Date object, format it
  if (dateValue instanceof Date) {
    return Utilities.formatDate(dateValue, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  }
  
  // Try to parse as date
  try {
    const date = new Date(dateValue);
    if (!isNaN(date.getTime())) {
      return Utilities.formatDate(date, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    }
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('Error parsing date:', dateValue, e);
  }
  
  return dateValue.toString();
}

 * Handle reschedule submission from client (no-cors mode)
 */
/**
 * DEPRECATED: Reschedule submission handler

 * Kept for reference only - can be removed in future cleanup.

 * Keeping for reference but renamed to avoid conflict
 */

  try {
    console.log('handleRescheduleSubmission_OLD called with params:', params);

    const { appointmentId, selectedDate, selectedTime, additionalNotes } = params;

    if (!appointmentId || !selectedDate || !selectedTime) {
      console.error('Missing required info for reschedule:', { appointmentId, selectedDate, selectedTime });
      return HtmlService.createHtmlOutput('<html><body><h1>Error: Missing required information</h1></body></html>');
    }

    // Get current appointment data
    const appointment = getAppointmentData(appointmentId);
    if (!appointment) {

    const oldTime = appointment['Selected Time'] || appointment.selectedTime || 'Not specified';

    // Update spreadsheet

/**
 * Update appointment date/time for client reschedule
 */
function updateAppointmentDateTimeForReschedule(appointmentId, newDate, newTime, oldDate, oldTime, notes) {
  try {
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = spreadsheet.getActiveSheet();
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    
    if (data.length <= 1) {
      throw new Error('No appointment data found');
    }
    
    const headers = data[0];
    const rowIndex = findRowIndexBySessionId(appointmentId);
    
    if (rowIndex >= 2 && rowIndex <= data.length) {
      // Find column indices
      const selectedDateIndex = headers.indexOf('Selected Date');
      const selectedTimeIndex = headers.indexOf('Selected Time');
      const statusIndex = headers.indexOf('Status');
      const clientStatusIndex = headers.indexOf('Client Status');
      const lastUpdatedIndex = headers.indexOf('Last Updated');
      let rescheduleHistoryIndex = headers.indexOf('Reschedule History');
      
      // Add Reschedule History column if it doesn't exist
      if (rescheduleHistoryIndex === -1) {
        console.log('Reschedule History column not found, adding it...');
        headers.push('Reschedule History');
        rescheduleHistoryIndex = headers.length - 1;
        sheet.getRange(1, rescheduleHistoryIndex + 1).setValue('Reschedule History');
        console.log('Reschedule History column added at index:', rescheduleHistoryIndex);
      }
      
      // Create reschedule history entry first to get formatted dates
      const rescheduleTimestamp = new Date().toLocaleString('en-IN', { 
        timeZone: 'Asia/Kolkata',
        day: '2-digit',
        month: 'short', 
        year: 'numeric',
        hour: '2-digit',
        minute: '2-digit',
        hour12: true
      });
      
      // Format old and new times for history
      const formattedOldDate = formatDateForDisplay(oldDate);
      const formattedOldTime = formatTimeForDisplay(oldTime);
      const formattedNewDate = formatDateForDisplay(newDate);
      const formattedNewTime = formatTimeForDisplay(newTime);
      
      // Update Selected Date and Selected Time
      if (selectedDateIndex !== -1) {
        sheet.getRange(rowIndex, selectedDateIndex + 1).setValue(newDate);
      }
      
      // Update Selected Time column with just the new time (no reschedule history)
      if (selectedTimeIndex !== -1) {
        sheet.getRange(rowIndex, selectedTimeIndex + 1).setValue(newTime);
      }
      
      // Update status to "Session Rescheduled"
      if (statusIndex !== -1) {
        sheet.getRange(rowIndex, statusIndex + 1).setValue('Session Rescheduled');
      }
      
      // Get existing reschedule history
      const existingHistory = rescheduleHistoryIndex !== -1 ? 
        sheet.getRange(rowIndex, rescheduleHistoryIndex + 1).getValue() || '' : '';
      
      // Create new history entry
      const historyEntry = `${rescheduleTimestamp}: Client rescheduled from ${formattedOldDate} ${formattedOldTime} to ${formattedNewDate} ${formattedNewTime}`;
      
      // Append to existing history
      const updatedHistory = existingHistory ? 
        `${existingHistory}\n${historyEntry}` : historyEntry;
      
      // Save reschedule history
      if (rescheduleHistoryIndex !== -1) {
        sheet.getRange(rowIndex, rescheduleHistoryIndex + 1).setValue(updatedHistory);
      }
      
      // Update client status with old and new time information (properly formatted with <br> tags)
      if (clientStatusIndex !== -1) {
        const clientStatusText = `New Time Slot Chosen<br>Old: ${formattedOldDate} - ${formattedOldTime}<br>New: ${formattedNewDate} - ${formattedNewTime}`;
        sheet.getRange(rowIndex, clientStatusIndex + 1).setValue(clientStatusText);
      }
      
      // Update last modified timestamp
      if (lastUpdatedIndex !== -1) {
        sheet.getRange(rowIndex, lastUpdatedIndex + 1).setValue(new Date().toString());
      }
      
      console.log('Appointment updated successfully with new schedule');
    } else {
      throw new Error('Invalid appointment ID');
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error updating appointment for reschedule:', error);
    throw error;
  }
}

/**
 * Format date for display in client status
 */
function formatDateForDisplay(dateInput) {
  // IMPROVEMENT: Handle null or undefined input immediately
  if (!dateInput) {
    return 'Not specified';
  }
  
  try {
    // This will correctly handle both string dates ('2025-11-18') and Date objects
    const date = new Date(dateInput);
    
    if (isNaN(date.getTime())) {
      // If parsing fails, return the original input as-is
      return dateInput.toString();
    }
    
    return date.toLocaleDateString('en-US', {
      weekday: 'short',
      month: 'short',
      day: '2-digit',
      year: 'numeric'
    });
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error formatting date:', error, 'Input:', dateInput);
    return dateInput.toString(); // Fallback to the original string
  }
}

/**
 * Format time for display in client status
 */
function formatTimeForDisplay(timeInput) {
  // IMPROVEMENT: Handle null or undefined input immediately
  if (!timeInput) {
    return 'Not specified';
  }

  try {
    // Handle cases where the input is just a time string like "11:00"
    if (typeof timeInput === 'string' && /^\d{2}:\d{2}(:\d{2})?$/.test(timeInput)) {
      const [hours, minutes] = timeInput.split(':');
      const tempDate = new Date();
      tempDate.setHours(hours, minutes, 0, 0);
      return tempDate.toLocaleTimeString('en-US', {
        hour: '2-digit',
        minute: '2-digit',
        hour12: true
      });
    }

    // Handle full Date objects (which is what Google Sheets often provides for time)
    const date = new Date(timeInput);
    
    if (isNaN(date.getTime())) {
      return timeInput.toString(); // Fallback if parsing fails
    }

    return date.toLocaleTimeString('en-US', {
      hour: '2-digit',
      minute: '2-digit',
      hour12: true
    });

  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error formatting time:', error, 'Input:', timeInput);
    return timeInput.toString(); // Fallback to the original string
  }
}

/**
 * Sends a simple, plain-text email to the admin with error details.
 * This function is designed to be as simple as possible to ensure it never fails.
 */
function sendErrorNotificationToAdmin(error, functionName = 'Unknown Function') {
  try {
    const adminEmail = CONFIG.OWNER_EMAIL;
    const subject = `CRITICAL SCRIPT ERROR in ${functionName}`;
    const body = `A severe error occurred in the script. Please review the details below:\n\n` +
                 `Function: ${functionName}\n` +
                 `Timestamp: ${new Date().toISOString()}\n\n` +
                 `Error Message: ${error.message}\n\n` +
                 `Stack Trace:\n${error.stack}`;

    // Use the most basic email service to ensure delivery
    MailApp.sendEmail(adminEmail, subject, body);

  } catch (e) {
    // If even the error reporter fails, log it as a last resort.
    console.error('FATAL: Could not send error notification email.', e);
  }
}

/**
 * Send reschedule notification to admin (Definitive, Ultra-Robust Version)
 */
function sendRescheduleNotificationToAdmin(appointment, newDate, newTime, oldDate, oldTime, notes) {
  const FUNCTION_NAME = 'sendRescheduleNotificationToAdmin';
  try {
    // --- EXTREMELY DEFENSIVE DATA SANITIZATION ---
    // Use optional chaining (?.) and nullish coalescing (??) to safely access properties.
    const clientName = appointment?.name ?? appointment?.['Full Name *'] ?? 'Unknown Client';
    const clientEmail = appointment?.email ?? appointment?.['Email Address *'] ?? 'No email provided';
    const sessionType = appointment?.['session-type'] ?? appointment?.sessionType ?? 'Not specified';
    const adminEmail = CONFIG.OWNER_EMAIL;
    const dashboardLink = "http://theanuragsharma.com/admin-login.html";

    // Log the sanitized data we are about to use.
    console.log(`Preparing admin email with sanitized data: Name=${clientName}, Email=${clientEmail}, Session=${sessionType}`);

    // Safely format all date/time values.
    const formattedNewDate = formatDateForDisplay(newDate);
    const formattedNewTime = formatTimeForDisplay(newTime);
    const formattedOldDate = formatDateForDisplay(oldDate);
    const formattedOldTime = formatTimeForDisplay(oldTime);

    const subject = `Client Rescheduled Session: ${clientName}`;

    const htmlBody = `
      <div style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; color: #333;">
        <div style="background: #fff3cd; padding: 15px; border-left: 5px solid #ffc107; margin-bottom: 20px;">
          <h2 style="margin: 0; color: #856404;">Action Required: Client Rescheduled Session</h2>
        </div>
        <p>A client has self-rescheduled their appointment. Please review and update your calendar.</p>
        <h3>Client Details:</h3>
        <ul>
          <li><strong>Name:</strong> ${clientName}</li>
          <li><strong>Email:</strong> ${clientEmail}</li>
          <li><strong>Session Type:</strong> ${sessionType}</li>
        </ul>
        <h3>Schedule Changes:</h3>
        <p style="background: #f8d7da; padding: 10px; border-radius: 4px;"><strong>❌ Old Schedule:</strong> ${formattedOldDate} at ${formattedOldTime}</p>
        <p style="background: #d4edda; padding: 10px; border-radius: 4px;"><strong>✅ New Schedule:</strong> ${formattedNewDate} at ${formattedNewTime}</p>
        ${notes && notes.trim() ? `<h3>Client's Message:</h3><p style="background: #f0f0f0; padding: 10px; font-style: italic;">"${notes}"</p>` : ''}
        <p style="margin-top: 25px;"><a href="${dashboardLink}" style="background-color: #007bff; color: white; padding: 12px 20px; text-decoration: none; border-radius: 5px;">View in Dashboard</a></p>
      </div>
    `;

    // Use GmailApp for its reliability and sent-mail history.
    GmailApp.sendEmail(adminEmail, subject, "", {
      htmlBody: htmlBody,
      name: CONFIG.FROM_NAME
    });

    console.log('✅ Admin reschedule notification sent successfully via GmailApp.');

  } catch (error) {
    // --- THIS IS THE CRITICAL PART ---
    // If anything in the 'try' block fails, call the error reporter.
    console.error(`❌ CRITICAL FAILURE in ${FUNCTION_NAME}:`, error.toString());
    sendErrorNotificationToAdmin(error, FUNCTION_NAME);
  }
}

        <p><strong>Test Type:</strong> Manual Email Functionality Test</p>

        <p>If you receive this email, the basic email functionality is working and the issue with reschedule notifications may be elsewhere.</p>
      `
    });
    
    console.log('✅ Test email sent successfully');
    return { success: true, message: 'Test email sent successfully' };
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('❌ Test email failed:', error);
    return { success: false, error: error.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Get appointment data by ID
 */
function getAppointmentData(appointmentId) {
  try {
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = spreadsheet.getActiveSheet();
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    
    if (data.length <= 1) {
      return null;
    }
    
    const headers = data[0];
    const rowIndex = findRowIndexBySessionId(appointmentId);
    
    if (rowIndex >= 2 && rowIndex <= data.length) {
      const appointmentData = {};
      const rowData = data[rowIndex - 1]; // Convert to 0-based index
      
      headers.forEach((header, index) => {
        appointmentData[header] = rowData[index];
      });
      
      // Add some convenience properties
      appointmentData.selectedDate = appointmentData['Selected Date'];
      appointmentData.selectedTime = appointmentData['Selected Time'];
      appointmentData.sessionType = appointmentData['session-type'];
      
      // Debug logging to understand the data format
      console.log('getAppointmentData - Selected Date type:', typeof appointmentData['Selected Date']);
      console.log('getAppointmentData - Selected Date value:', appointmentData['Selected Date']);
      console.log('getAppointmentData - Selected Time type:', typeof appointmentData['Selected Time']);
      console.log('getAppointmentData - Selected Time value:', appointmentData['Selected Time']);
      
      return appointmentData;
    }
    
    return null;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error getting appointment data:', error);
    return null;
  }
}

// Helper functions for rescheduling
function formatTime(timeString) {
  if (!timeString || timeString === 'TBD') {
    return 'To be coordinated';
  }
  
  try {
    // Parse time string (HH:mm format)
    const [hours, minutes] = timeString.split(':').map(Number);
    const date = new Date();
    date.setHours(hours, minutes, 0, 0);
    
    return date.toLocaleTimeString('en-US', {
      hour: '2-digit',
      minute: '2-digit',
      hour12: true
    });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error formatting time:', error);
    return timeString;
  }
}

function createCalendarEvent(appointment) {
  try {
    const selectedDate = appointment.selectedDate || appointment['Selected Date'];
    const selectedTime = appointment.selectedTime || appointment['Selected Time'];
    
    if (!selectedDate || !selectedTime) {
      console.log('No date/time specified for calendar event');
      return;
    }
    
    if (selectedTime === 'TBD') {
      console.log('Time is TBD, skipping calendar event creation');
      return;
    }
    
    // Parse date and time
    const [hours, minutes] = selectedTime.split(':').map(Number);
    const startTime = new Date(selectedDate);
    startTime.setHours(hours, minutes, 0, 0);
    
    // Set end time (1 hour later)
    const endTime = new Date(startTime);
    endTime.setHours(startTime.getHours() + 1);
    
    // Create calendar event
    const calendar = CalendarApp.getDefaultCalendar();
    const event = calendar.createEvent(
      `Consultation Session - ${appointment.name}`,
      startTime,
      endTime,
      {
        description: `
Client: ${appointment.name}
Email: ${appointment.email}
Organization: ${appointment.organization || 'N/A'}
Session Type: ${appointment['session-type'] || appointment.sessionType || appointment['sessiontype'] || appointment['Type of Session *'] || 'Not specified'}
        `,
        guests: appointment.email,
        sendInvites: true
      }
    );
    
    console.log('Calendar event created:', event.getId());
    return event;
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error creating calendar event:', error);
    throw error;
  }
}

/**
 * Test function to verify date/time formatting
 */
function testDateTimeFormatting() {
  console.log('=== Testing Date/Time Formatting Functions ===');
  
  // Test various date formats
  const testDates = [
    '2025-10-21',
    'Tue Sep 09 2025 00:00:00 GMT+0530 (India Standard Time)',
    new Date('2025-09-09'),
    '09/09/2025',
    'Sep 9, 2025'
  ];
  
  const testTimes = [
    '11:30',
    '14:00',
    'Sat Dec 30 1899 11:00:00 GMT+0521 (India Standard Time)',
    new Date('2025-01-01T11:30:00'),
    '09:45'
  ];
  
  console.log('Date formatting tests:');
  testDates.forEach((date, index) => {
    const formatted = formatDateForDisplay(date);
    console.log(`Test ${index + 1}: "${date}" → "${formatted}"`);
  });
  
  console.log('\nTime formatting tests:');
  testTimes.forEach((time, index) => {
    const formatted = formatTimeForDisplay(time);
    console.log(`Test ${index + 1}: "${time}" → "${formatted}"`);
  });
  
  // Test the client status format with the exact problematic input
  const oldDate = 'Wed Oct 08 2025 00:00:00 GMT+0530 (India Standard Time)';
  const oldTime = 'Sat Dec 30 1899 11:00:00 GMT+0521 (India Standard Time)';
  const newDate = '2025-11-18';
  const newTime = '13:30';
  
  const formattedOldDate = formatDateForDisplay(oldDate);
  const formattedOldTime = formatTimeForDisplay(oldTime);
  const formattedNewDate = formatDateForDisplay(newDate);
  const formattedNewTime = formatTimeForDisplay(newTime);
  
  const clientStatusText = `New Time Slot Chosen\nOld: ${formattedOldDate} - ${formattedOldTime} (IST)\nNew: ${formattedNewDate} - ${formattedNewTime} (IST)`;
  
  console.log('\nClient Status Format Test:');
  console.log('Original problematic format:', `New Time Slot Chosen (Old: ${oldDate} ${oldTime} → New: ${newDate} ${newTime})`);
  console.log('NEW CORRECTED FORMAT:');
  console.log(clientStatusText);
  
  // Test with actual Date objects like from Google Sheets
  const dateObj = new Date('2025-10-08');
  const timeObj = new Date('1899-12-30T11:00:00'); // How Google Sheets stores time
  
  console.log('\nTesting with Date objects:');
  console.log('Date object:', dateObj, '→', formatDateForDisplay(dateObj));
  console.log('Time object:', timeObj, '→', formatTimeForDisplay(timeObj));
  
  return {
    success: true,
    clientStatusExample: clientStatusText
  };
}

// Helper functions for query management
/**
 * Get the count of queries from the appointment's query history
 * @param {Object} appointment - The appointment object
 * @returns {number} - Number of queries submitted
 */
function getQueryCountFromHistory(appointment) {
  const queryHistory = appointment.queryHistory || appointment['Query History'] || '';
  
  if (!queryHistory || queryHistory.trim() === '') {
    return 0;
  }
  
  // Count the number of query entries
  // Each query creates an entry like "timestamp: Client submitted query: ..."
  const queryEntries = queryHistory.split('\n').filter(entry => 
    entry.trim() !== '' && (entry.includes('submitted query') || entry.includes('Query:'))
  );
  
  return queryEntries.length;
}

/**
 * Add query resolution to the query history
 * @param {string} appointmentId - The appointment ID (row index)
 * @param {string} resolution - The resolution notes
 * @param {string} fileLink - Optional file link
 */
function addQueryResolutionToHistory(appointmentId, resolution, fileLink = '') {
  try {
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = spreadsheet.getActiveSheet();
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const headers = data[0];
    
    // Convert appointmentId to row index (appointmentId is the row number)
    const rowIndex = findRowIndexBySessionId(appointmentId);
    
    if (rowIndex < 2 || rowIndex > data.length) {
      throw new Error(`Invalid appointment row index: ${appointmentId}`);
    }
    
    const appointmentRowIndex = rowIndex - 1; // Convert to 0-based index for data array
    
    // Find Query History column
    const queryHistoryIndex = headers.indexOf('Query History');
    let currentQueryHistory = '';
    
    if (queryHistoryIndex !== -1) {
      currentQueryHistory = data[appointmentRowIndex][queryHistoryIndex] || '';
    }
    
    // Create resolution entry
    const timestamp = new Date().toLocaleString('en-US', { 
      timeZone: 'Asia/Kolkata',
      year: 'numeric',
      month: '2-digit', 
      day: '2-digit',
      hour: '2-digit',
      minute: '2-digit',
      second: '2-digit'
    });
    
    const resolutionEntry = `${timestamp}: Admin resolved query - ${resolution}`;
    
    // Append to existing history
    const updatedHistory = currentQueryHistory 
      ? currentQueryHistory + '\n' + resolutionEntry 
      : resolutionEntry;
    
    // Update the sheet (rowIndex is already 1-based)
    if (queryHistoryIndex !== -1) {
      sheet.getRange(rowIndex, queryHistoryIndex + 1).setValue(updatedHistory);
    } else {
      // If Query History column doesn't exist, add it
      const newColumnIndex = headers.length + 1;
      sheet.getRange(1, newColumnIndex).setValue('Query History');
      sheet.getRange(rowIndex, newColumnIndex).setValue(updatedHistory);
    }
    
    console.log('Query resolution added to history:', resolutionEntry);
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error adding query resolution to history:', error);
    throw error;
  }
}

/**
 * Add a client query to the query history
 * @param {string} appointmentId - The appointment ID (row index)
 * @param {string} query - The client's query text
 * @param {string} fileLink - Optional file link
 */
function addQueryToHistory(appointmentId, query, fileLink = '') {
  try {
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = spreadsheet.getActiveSheet();
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const headers = data[0];
    
    // Convert appointmentId to row index (appointmentId is the row number)
    const rowIndex = findRowIndexBySessionId(appointmentId);
    
    if (rowIndex < 2 || rowIndex > data.length) {
      throw new Error(`Invalid appointment row index: ${appointmentId}`);
    }
    
    const appointmentRowIndex = rowIndex - 1; // Convert to 0-based index for data array
    
    // Find Query History column
    const queryHistoryIndex = headers.indexOf('Query History');
    let currentQueryHistory = '';
    
    if (queryHistoryIndex !== -1) {
      currentQueryHistory = data[appointmentRowIndex][queryHistoryIndex] || '';
    }
    
    // Create query entry
    const timestamp = new Date().toLocaleString('en-US', { 
      timeZone: 'Asia/Kolkata',
      year: 'numeric',
      month: '2-digit', 
      day: '2-digit',
      hour: '2-digit',
      minute: '2-digit',
      second: '2-digit'
    });
    
    const queryEntry = fileLink 
      ? `${timestamp}: Client submitted query: ${query} [Document: ${fileLink}]`
      : `${timestamp}: Client submitted query: ${query}`;
    
    // Append to existing history
    const updatedHistory = currentQueryHistory 
      ? currentQueryHistory + '\n' + queryEntry 
      : queryEntry;
    
    // Update the sheet (rowIndex is already 1-based)
    if (queryHistoryIndex !== -1) {
      sheet.getRange(rowIndex, queryHistoryIndex + 1).setValue(updatedHistory);
    } else {
      // If Query History column doesn't exist, add it
      const newColumnIndex = headers.length + 1;
      sheet.getRange(1, newColumnIndex).setValue('Query History');
      sheet.getRange(rowIndex, newColumnIndex).setValue(updatedHistory);
    }
    
    console.log('Query added to history:', queryEntry);
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error adding query to history:', error);
    throw error;
  }
}

  console.log('=== Testing Reschedule Workflow Fixes ===');

    // Test 2: Client response status logic

      'New Time Slot Chosen\nOld: Tue, Oct 08, 2025 - 11:00:00 AM IST\nNew: Mon, Nov 18, 2025 - 01:30:00 PM IST',
      'Approved - Awaiting Response',
      'Proceed',
      'Query',
      'Feedback Pending'
    ];
    
    console.log('Testing response blocking logic:');
    testStatuses.forEach((status, index) => {
      const blockedStatuses = ['Proceed', 'Query'];
      const isBlocked = blockedStatuses.some(blockedStatus => 
        status && status.toString().includes(blockedStatus)
      );

    const oldTime = 'Sat Dec 30 1899 11:00:00 GMT+0521 (India Standard Time)';
    const newDate = '2025-11-18';
    const newTime = '13:30';
    
    const formattedOldDate = formatDateForDisplay(oldDate);
    const formattedOldTime = formatTimeForDisplay(oldTime);
    const formattedNewDate = formatDateForDisplay(newDate);
    const formattedNewTime = formatTimeForDisplay(newTime);

    console.log('Session time column format:', displayTime);

    console.log('Client status format:', clientStatusText);
    
    console.log('\n✅ All workflow fixes have been implemented!');
    console.log('\nFixed Issues:');
    console.log('1. ✅ Client status now updates properly after approval');
    console.log('2. ✅ Reschedule history now visible in session time column');
    console.log('3. ✅ "Response Already Recorded" error fixed - clients can respond after approval');
    
    return {
      success: true,
      message: 'All reschedule workflow fixes implemented successfully',
      fixes: [
        'handleApproveAction now updates client status after approval',
        'Session time column shows reschedule history',
        'getClientResponseStatus allows responses after approval',
        'Date/time formatting improved for better readability'
      ]
    };
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error in test function:', error);
    return {
      success: false,
      error: error.message
    };
  }
}

      console.log('✅ Calendar permission granted');

    }
    
    // 5. Script properties permissions
    console.log('\n⚙️ 5. Requesting Script Properties permissions...');
    try {
      PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty('test', 'authorized');
      PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().deleteProperty('test');
      console.log('✅ Script Properties permission granted');
    } catch (e) {
      console.log('❌ Script Properties permission needed:', e.message);
    }

      console.log('   Timezone:', userTimezone);

      console.log('❌ User Info permission needed:', e.message);

      success: false,
      message: error.toString(),
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    };
  }
}

/**
 * Handle refund initiation by admin
 */
function handleRefundInitiation(params) {
  try {
    console.log('handleRefundInitiation called with:', params);
    console.log('🔍 Detailed parameter analysis:', {
      appointmentId: params.appointmentId,
      refundNotes: params.refundNotes,
      hasRefundProofDocument: !!params.refundProofDocument,
      refundProofName: params.refundProofName,
      refundProofType: params.refundProofType,
      documentLength: params.refundProofDocument ? params.refundProofDocument.length : 0
    });
    
    const { appointmentId, refundNotes, refundProofDocument, refundProofName, refundProofType } = params;
    
    if (!appointmentId) {
      return createCORSResponse({
        status: 'error',
        message: 'Missing appointment ID'
      });
    }
    
    // Get appointment data
    const appointment = getAppointmentData(appointmentId);
    if (!appointment) {
      console.log('❌ Appointment not found for ID:', appointmentId);
      return createCORSResponse({
        status: 'error',
        message: 'Appointment not found'
      });
    }
    console.log('✅ Appointment found:', appointment.name);

    // Check if refund already initiated
    const currentStatus = appointment.status || appointment['Status'] || '';
    console.log('🔍 Current appointment status:', currentStatus);
    if (currentStatus.includes('Refund')) {
      console.log('❌ Refund already initiated. Current status:', currentStatus);
      return createCORSResponse({
        status: 'error',
        message: 'Refund has already been initiated for this appointment'
      });
    }
    console.log('✅ Refund not yet initiated, proceeding...');

    // Check refund cooldown to prevent spam
    console.log('🔍 Checking refund cooldown...');
    if (isRefundOnCooldown(appointment)) {
      console.log('❌ Refund is on cooldown');
      return createCORSResponse({
        status: 'error',
        message: `Please wait at least ${CONFIG.REFUND_COOLDOWN_MINUTES} minutes between refund actions.`
      });
    }
    console.log('✅ No cooldown restriction, proceeding...');    let refundProofLink = '';
    console.log('🔍 Initialized refundProofLink as empty string');

    // Upload refund proof if provided
    console.log('🔍 Checking if refund proof document is provided...');
    console.log('   - hasDocument:', !!refundProofDocument);
    console.log('   - hasName:', !!refundProofName);
    console.log('   - hasType:', !!refundProofType);
    
    if (refundProofDocument && refundProofName && refundProofType) {
      console.log('✅ All file data present, proceeding with upload...');
      try {
        console.log('Processing refund proof upload:', {
          fileName: refundProofName,
          fileType: refundProofType,
          fileSize: refundProofDocument ? refundProofDocument.length : 0,
          appointmentId: appointmentId
        });
        
        console.log('🔄 Step 1: Attempting base64 decode...');
        const decodedData = Utilities.base64Decode(refundProofDocument);
        console.log('✅ Base64 decode successful, decoded size:', decodedData.length);
        
        console.log('🔄 Step 2: Creating file blob...');
        const fileBlob = Utilities.newBlob(
          decodedData,
          refundProofType,
          refundProofName
        );
        
        console.log('✅ File blob created successfully:', {
          blobName: fileBlob.getName(),
          blobType: fileBlob.getContentType(),
          blobSize: fileBlob.getBytes().length
        });
        
        const clientName = appointment.name || appointment['Full Name *'] || 'UnknownClient';
        console.log('🔄 Step 3: Calling uploadRefundProof with client name:', clientName);
        
        const uploadedFile = uploadRefundProof(appointmentId, fileBlob, clientName);
        refundProofLink = uploadedFile.url;
        console.log('✅ Refund proof uploaded successfully:', {
          fileId: uploadedFile.id,
          fileName: uploadedFile.name,
          fileUrl: uploadedFile.url,
          fileSize: uploadedFile.size
        });
      } catch (fileError) {
        console.error('❌ ERROR in file upload process:', fileError);
        console.error('❌ Error name:', fileError.name);
        console.error('❌ Error message:', fileError.message);
        console.error('❌ Error stack:', fileError.stack);
        return createCORSResponse({
          status: 'error',
          message: 'Failed to upload refund proof: ' + fileError.toString()
        });
      }
    } else {
      console.log('ℹ️ No refund proof document provided. Checking what data we received:', {
        hasDocument: !!refundProofDocument,
        hasName: !!refundProofName,
        hasType: !!refundProofType,
        documentLength: refundProofDocument ? refundProofDocument.length : 0,
        fileName: refundProofName,
        fileType: refundProofType
      });
    }
    
    console.log('🔍 File upload section completed. refundProofLink:', refundProofLink);

    // Update appointment status and add refund information
    console.log('🔄 Step 4: Updating appointment status...');
    try {
      updateAppointmentForRefund(appointmentId, refundNotes || '', refundProofLink);
      console.log('✅ Appointment updated successfully');
    } catch (updateError) {
      console.error('❌ Error updating appointment:', updateError);
      // Continue anyway - don't fail the whole process
    }

    // Send refund notification email to client
    console.log('🔄 Step 5: Sending notification to client...');
    try {
      sendRefundNotificationToClient(appointmentId, refundNotes || '', refundProofLink);
      console.log('✅ Client notification sent');
    } catch (emailError) {
      console.error('❌ Error sending client notification:', emailError);
      // Continue anyway - don't fail the whole process
    }

    // Send confirmation email to admin
    console.log('🔄 Step 6: Sending confirmation to admin...');
    try {
      sendRefundInitiatedConfirmationToAdmin(appointmentId, refundNotes || '', refundProofLink);
      console.log('✅ Admin confirmation sent');
    } catch (adminEmailError) {
      console.error('❌ Error sending admin confirmation:', adminEmailError);
      // Continue anyway - don't fail the whole process
    }

    console.log('🎉 Creating success response...');
    const successResponse = createCORSResponse({
      status: 'success',
      message: 'Refund initiated successfully. Client has been notified.',
      refundProofLink: refundProofLink
    });
    console.log('✅ Success response created:', successResponse);
    
    return successResponse;  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error handling refund initiation:', error);
    return createCORSResponse({
      status: 'error',
      message: error.toString()
    });
  }
}

/**
 * Handle refund acknowledgment by client
 */
function handleRefundAcknowledgment(params) {
  try {
    console.log('handleRefundAcknowledgment called with:', params);
    
    const { appointmentId } = params;
    
    if (!appointmentId) {
      return { status: 'error', message: 'Missing appointment ID' };
    }
    
    // Get appointment data
    const appointment = getAppointmentData(appointmentId);
    if (!appointment) {
      return { status: 'error', message: 'Appointment not found' };
    }
    
    // Check if client has already acknowledged refund
    const currentClientStatus = appointment.clientStatus || appointment['Client Status'] || '';
    if (currentClientStatus === 'Refund Acknowledged') {
      return { status: 'error', message: 'Refund has already been acknowledged' };
    }
    
    // Check if refund was actually initiated
    const currentStatus = appointment.status || appointment['Status'] || '';
    if (!currentStatus.includes('Refund Initiated')) {
      return { status: 'error', message: 'No refund has been initiated for this appointment' };
    }
    
    // Update client status and main status
    updateClientStatus(appointmentId, 'Refund Acknowledged', null);
    updateMainAppointmentStatus(appointmentId, 'Refund Process Completed');
    
    // Add refund acknowledgment to history
    addRefundAcknowledgmentToHistory(appointmentId);
    
    // Send confirmation email to admin
    sendRefundAcknowledgedNotificationToAdmin(appointmentId);
    
    return { status: 'success', message: 'Refund acknowledgment recorded successfully' };
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error handling refund acknowledgment:', error);
    return { status: 'error', message: error.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Show refund acknowledgment form for client
 */
function showRefundAcknowledgmentForm(appointmentId) {
  try {
    // Check if client has already acknowledged refund
    const appointment = getAppointmentData(appointmentId);
    if (!appointment) {
      return createErrorPage('Appointment not found');
    }
    
    const currentClientStatus = appointment.clientStatus || appointment['Client Status'] || '';
    if (currentClientStatus === 'Refund Acknowledged') {
      return showRefundAlreadyAcknowledgedPage(appointmentId);
    }
    
    // Check if refund was initiated
    const currentStatus = appointment.status || appointment['Status'] || '';
    if (!currentStatus.includes('Refund Initiated')) {
      return createErrorPage('No refund has been initiated for this appointment');
    }
    
    const scriptUrl = getPublicWebAppUrl();
    
    const htmlTemplate = HtmlService.createTemplate(`

      e.preventDefault();
      
      const submitText = document.getElementById('submitText');
      const submitLoader = document.getElementById('submitLoader');
      
      // Disable button to prevent double submission
      submitBtn.disabled = true;
      submitText.style.display = 'none';
      submitLoader.style.display = 'inline-block';
      
      // Prepare parameters for google.script.run
      const params = {
        action: 'acknowledgeRefund',
        appointmentId: '<?= appointmentId ?>'
      };

      // Use google.script.run instead of fetch to avoid CORS issues
      google.script.run
        .withSuccessHandler(function(response) {
          if (response && response.status === 'success') {
            // Show success message by replacing the form
            document.getElementById('formContainer').innerHTML = \`
              <div style="text-align: center;">
                <div style="font-size: 48px; color: #28a745;">✅</div>
                <h2 style="color: #333;">Refund Acknowledged!</h2>
                <p style="font-size: 16px; color: #555;">Your refund receipt has been confirmed successfully. The admin has been notified.</p>

                </div>
              </div>
            \`;
          } else {
            // Show error message
            alert('Error: ' + (response ? response.message : 'Unknown error occurred'));
            resetSubmitButton();
          }
        })
        .withFailureHandler(function(error) {
          console.error('Submission Error:', error);
          alert('There was a technical error processing your acknowledgment. Please try again.');
          resetSubmitButton();
        })
        .handleRefundAcknowledgment(params);
    });

    function resetSubmitButton() {
      const submitText = document.getElementById('submitText');
      const submitLoader = document.getElementById('submitLoader');
      submitBtn.disabled = false;
      submitText.style.display = 'inline-block';
      submitLoader.style.display = 'none';
    }

</body>
</html>`);

    htmlTemplate.appointment = appointment;
    
    return htmlTemplate.evaluate()
      .setTitle('Acknowledge Refund Receipt')
      .setXFrameOptionsMode(HtmlService.XFrameOptionsMode.ALLOWALL);
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error showing refund acknowledgment form:', error);
    return createErrorPage(error.toString());
  }
}

/**
 * Upload refund proof to Google Drive
 */
function uploadRefundProof(appointmentId, fileBlob, clientName) {
  try {
    console.log('Uploading refund proof for appointment:', appointmentId);
    console.log('Original blob name:', fileBlob.getName());
    console.log('Blob size:', fileBlob.getBytes().length);
    
    // Create filename with appointment ID and client name
    const timestamp = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 19).replace(/:/g, '-');
    const originalName = fileBlob.getName() || 'refund_proof';
    const extension = originalName.split('.').pop() || 'pdf';
    const finalFileName = `REFUND_${appointmentId}_${clientName}_${timestamp}.${extension}`;
    
    // Create the final blob with the proper filename
    const finalBlob = Utilities.newBlob(
      fileBlob.getBytes(),
      fileBlob.getContentType(),
      finalFileName
    );
    
    console.log('Final blob name:', finalBlob.getName());
    
    // Get the folder
    const folder = DriveApp.getFolderById(CONFIG.REFUND_PROOF_FOLDER_ID);
    console.log('Folder accessed successfully:', CONFIG.REFUND_PROOF_FOLDER_ID);
    
    // Create file in Drive
    const file = folder.createFile(finalBlob);
    console.log('File created in Drive with ID:', file.getId());
    console.log('File name in Drive:', file.getName());
    
    // Set sharing to anyone with link can view
    try {
      file.setSharing(DriveApp.Access.ANYONE_WITH_LINK, DriveApp.Permission.VIEW);
      console.log('File sharing permissions set successfully');
    } catch (e) {
      console.log('Could not set sharing, file may inherit folder permissions:', e);
    }
    
    // Use the sharing URL format that works
    const fileUrl = `https://drive.google.com/file/d/${file.getId()}/view?usp=sharing`;
    
    console.log('✅ Refund proof uploaded successfully');
    console.log('   File Name:', finalFileName);
    console.log('   File ID:', file.getId());
    console.log('   File URL:', fileUrl);
    
    return {
      id: file.getId(),
      name: finalFileName,
      url: fileUrl,
      size: finalBlob.getBytes().length
    };
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('❌ Error uploading refund proof:', error);
    console.error('Error details:', error.message);
    console.error('Error stack:', error.stack);
    throw error;
  }
}

/**
 * Update appointment with refund information
 */
function updateAppointmentForRefund(appointmentId, refundNotes, refundProofLink) {
  try {
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = spreadsheet.getActiveSheet();
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const headers = data[0];
    
    const rowIndex = findRowIndexBySessionId(appointmentId);
    
    if (rowIndex >= 2 && rowIndex <= data.length) {
      // Update main status
      const statusColIndex = headers.indexOf('Status');
      if (statusColIndex !== -1) {
        sheet.getRange(rowIndex, statusColIndex + 1).setValue('Refund Initiated');
      }
      
      // Add/update refund notes column
      let refundNotesIndex = headers.indexOf('Refund Notes');
      if (refundNotesIndex === -1) {
        headers.push('Refund Notes');
        refundNotesIndex = headers.length - 1;
        sheet.getRange(1, refundNotesIndex + 1).setValue('Refund Notes');
      }
      sheet.getRange(rowIndex, refundNotesIndex + 1).setValue(refundNotes);
      
      // Add/update refund proof column
      if (refundProofLink) {
        let refundProofIndex = headers.indexOf('Refund Proof Link');
        if (refundProofIndex === -1) {
          headers.push('Refund Proof Link');
          refundProofIndex = headers.length - 1;
          sheet.getRange(1, refundProofIndex + 1).setValue('Refund Proof Link');
        }
        sheet.getRange(rowIndex, refundProofIndex + 1).setValue(refundProofLink);
      }
      
      // Add refund history
      addRefundToHistory(appointmentId, 'Refund initiated by admin', refundNotes, refundProofLink);
      
      console.log('Appointment updated with refund information');
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error updating appointment for refund:', error);
    throw error;
  }
}

/**
 * Add refund entry to history
 */
function addRefundToHistory(appointmentId, action, notes = '', proofLink = '') {
  try {
    const spreadsheet = getOrCreateSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = spreadsheet.getActiveSheet();
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const headers = data[0];
    
    const rowIndex = findRowIndexBySessionId(appointmentId);
    
    if (rowIndex >= 2 && rowIndex <= data.length) {
      let refundHistoryIndex = headers.indexOf('Refund History');
      
      if (refundHistoryIndex === -1) {
        headers.push('Refund History');
        refundHistoryIndex = headers.length - 1;
        sheet.getRange(1, refundHistoryIndex + 1).setValue('Refund History');
      }
      
      const timestamp = new Date().toLocaleString('en-US', { timeZone: 'Asia/Kolkata' });
      const existingHistory = sheet.getRange(rowIndex, refundHistoryIndex + 1).getValue() || '';
      
      let historyEntry = `${timestamp}: ${action}`;
      if (notes) historyEntry += ` - Notes: ${notes}`;
      if (proofLink) historyEntry += ` [Proof: ${proofLink}]`;
      
      const updatedHistory = existingHistory ? 
        `${existingHistory}\n${historyEntry}` : historyEntry;
      
      sheet.getRange(rowIndex, refundHistoryIndex + 1).setValue(updatedHistory);
      console.log('Refund history updated');
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error adding refund to history:', error);
    throw error;
  }
}

/**
 * Add refund acknowledgment to history
 */
function addRefundAcknowledgmentToHistory(appointmentId) {
  try {
    addRefundToHistory(appointmentId, 'Client acknowledged refund receipt');
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error adding refund acknowledgment to history:', error);
    throw error;
  }
}

/**
 * Check if refund is on cooldown
 */
function isRefundOnCooldown(appointment) {
  try {
    const refundHistory = appointment.refundHistory || appointment['Refund History'] || '';
    
    if (!refundHistory || refundHistory.trim() === '') {
      return false; // No previous refund actions
    }
    
    // Get the most recent refund action timestamp
    const refundEntries = refundHistory.split('\n').filter(entry => 
      entry.trim() !== ''
    );
    
    if (refundEntries.length === 0) {
      return false; // No refund actions found
    }
    
    // Parse the most recent refund timestamp
    const mostRecentEntry = refundEntries[refundEntries.length - 1];
    const timestampMatch = mostRecentEntry.match(/^([^:]+):/);
    
    if (!timestampMatch) {
      return false; // Could not parse timestamp
    }
    
    try {
      const lastRefundTime = new Date(timestampMatch[1]);
      const now = new Date();
      const minutesSinceLastRefund = (now - lastRefundTime) / (1000 * 60);
      
      console.log('Last refund action was', minutesSinceLastRefund, 'minutes ago');
      return minutesSinceLastRefund < CONFIG.REFUND_COOLDOWN_MINUTES;
    } catch (parseError) {
      console.log('Could not parse refund timestamp, allowing refund action');
      return false;
    }
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error checking refund cooldown:', error);
    return false; // Allow refund if we can't check
  }
}

        <li>Once received, click the acknowledgment button above</li>
        <li>We will update our records and consider the refund process complete</li>
      </ul>
    </div>
    
    <hr style="border: none; border-top: 1px solid #eee; margin: 30px 0;">

      <strong>theanuragsharma.web@gmail.com</strong>
    </p>
    
    <p style="text-align: center; color: #666; font-size: 12px; margin-top: 20px;">

    </p>

    MailApp.sendEmail({
      to: clientEmail,
