/**
 * Quick test function you can run to verify the new format
 */
function testRescheduleStatusFormat() {
  console.log('=== Testing Reschedule Status Format ===');
  
  // Simulate the exact scenario from your issue
  const oldDateFromSheets = new Date('Wed Oct 08 2025 00:00:00 GMT+0530 (India Standard Time)');
  const oldTimeFromSheets = new Date('Sat Dec 30 1899 11:00:00 GMT+0521 (India Standard Time)');
  const newDate = '2025-11-18';
  const newTime = '13:30';
  
  console.log('Input data:');
  console.log('Old Date (from sheets):', oldDateFromSheets);
  console.log('Old Time (from sheets):', oldTimeFromSheets);
  console.log('New Date:', newDate);
  console.log('New Time:', newTime);
  
  // Test formatting
  const formattedOldDate = formatDateForDisplay(oldDateFromSheets);
  const formattedOldTime = formatTimeForDisplay(oldTimeFromSheets);
  const formattedNewDate = formatDateForDisplay(newDate);
  const formattedNewTime = formatTimeForDisplay(newTime);
  
  const clientStatusText = `New Time Slot Chosen\nOld: ${formattedOldDate} - ${formattedOldTime} (IST)\nNew: ${formattedNewDate} - ${formattedNewTime} (IST)`;
  
  console.log('\nFormatted results:');
  console.log('Old Date formatted:', formattedOldDate);
  console.log('Old Time formatted:', formattedOldTime);
  console.log('New Date formatted:', formattedNewDate);
  console.log('New Time formatted:', formattedNewTime);
  
  console.log('\nFinal Client Status:');
  console.log(clientStatusText);
  
  return clientStatusText;
}

/**
 * Test function to upload a file to the Refund Documents folder and then delete it
 * This helps verify if the issue is with code or folder permissions
 */
function testRefundDocumentUploadAndDelete() {
  console.log('=== STARTING REFUND DOCUMENT UPLOAD TEST ===');
  
  try {
    // Step 1: Create a test PDF document
    console.log('Step 1: Creating test PDF document...');
    const testContent = 'This is a test refund document for testing upload functionality.\n' +
                       'Created at: ' + new Date().toISOString() + '\n' +
                       'Test ID: ' + Utilities.getUuid();
    
    const testBlob = Utilities.newBlob(testContent, 'application/pdf', 'test_refund_document.pdf');
    console.log('   ✅ Test PDF created');
    
    // Step 2: Test parameters
    const testAppointmentId = 'TEST_' + Date.now();
    const testClientName = 'Test Client Upload';
    
    console.log('Step 2: Test parameters:');
    console.log('   Appointment ID:', testAppointmentId);
    console.log('   Client Name:', testClientName);
    console.log('   File Name:', testBlob.getName());
    console.log('   File Type:', testBlob.getContentType());
    console.log('   File Size:', testBlob.getBytes().length, 'bytes');
    
    // Step 3: Upload the file
    console.log('Step 3: Calling uploadRefundProof function...');
    const uploadResult = uploadRefundProof(testAppointmentId, testBlob, testClientName);
    
    console.log('✅ Upload successful!');
    console.log('   File ID:', uploadResult.id);
    console.log('   File Name:', uploadResult.name);
    console.log('   File URL:', uploadResult.url);
    console.log('   File Size:', uploadResult.size, 'bytes');
    
    // Step 4: Verify the file exists in the folder
    console.log('\nStep 4: Verifying file exists in Drive...');
    const folder = DriveApp.getFolderById(CONFIG.REFUND_PROOF_FOLDER_ID);
    const files = folder.getFilesByName(uploadResult.name);
    
    if (files.hasNext()) {
      const verifyFile = files.next();
      console.log('   ✅ File verified in Drive');
      console.log('   Verified File ID:', verifyFile.getId());
      console.log('   Verified File Name:', verifyFile.getName());
      
      // Step 5: Delete the test file
      console.log('\nStep 5: Cleaning up test file...');
      try {
        DriveApp.getFileById(uploadResult.id).setTrashed(true);
        console.log('   ✅ Test file deleted successfully');
      } catch (deleteError) {
        console.error('   ❌ Error deleting test file:', deleteError);
      }
    } else {
      console.error('   ❌ File not found in Drive folder after upload!');
    }
    
    console.log('\n=== TEST COMPLETED SUCCESSFULLY ===');
    console.log('📌 The refund document upload functionality is working correctly!');
    console.log('📌 If refunds are not saving documents, the issue is likely in frontend data mapping.');
    
    return {
      status: 'success',
      message: 'Test completed successfully',
      uploadResult: uploadResult
    };
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('=== TEST FAILED ===');
    console.error('❌ Error during test:', error);
    console.error('Error details:', error.toString());
    
    return {
      status: 'error',
      message: 'Test failed: ' + error.toString(),
      error: error
    };
  }
}

/**
 * Test the exact data flow from admin dashboard to handleRefundInitiation
 */
function testRealRefundFlow() {
  console.log('=== TESTING REAL REFUND FLOW ===');
  
  try {
    // Simulate what the admin dashboard sends
    const formData = {
      action: 'initiateRefund',
      appointmentId: 'GIS-2025-001',
      appointment: JSON.stringify({
        sessionId: 'GIS-2025-001',
        name: 'Anurag Sharma - Dev',
        email: 'ANURAG@gmail.com'
      }),
      actionData: JSON.stringify({
        notes: 'Test notes from simulated frontend',
        refundProofDocument: 'JVBERi0xLjQKJfbk/N8KMSAwIG9iago8PAovVHlwZSAvQ2F0YWxvZwovUGFnZXMgMiAwIFIKPj4KZW5kb2JqCjIgMCBvYmoKPDwKL1R5cGUgL1BhZ2VzCi9LaWRzIFsgMyAwIFIgXQovQ291bnQgMQo+PgplbmRvYmoKMyAwIG9iago8PAovVHlwZSAvUGFnZQovUGFyZW50IDIgMCBSCi9NZWRpYUJveCBbIDAgMCA2MTIgNzkyIF0KPj4KZW5kb2JqCnhyZWYKMCA0CjAwMDAwMDAwMDAgNjU1MzUgZiAKMDAwMDAwMDAwOSAwMDAwMCBuIAowMDAwMDAwMDU4IDAwMDAwIG4gCjAwMDAwMDAxMTUgMDAwMDAgbiAKdHJhaWxlcgo8PAovU2l6ZSA0Ci9Sb290IDEgMCBSCj4+CnN0YXJ0eHJlZgoxODUKJSVFT0Y=',
        refundProofName: 'test_real_flow.pdf',
        refundProofType: 'application/pdf'
      })
    };
    
    console.log('📤 Simulated form data created');
    
    // Parse the data exactly like the backend does
    const action = formData.action;
    const appointmentId = formData.appointmentId;
    const actionData = JSON.parse(formData.actionData);
    
    console.log('📥 Parsed data:', {
      action: action,
      appointmentId: appointmentId,
      actionDataKeys: Object.keys(actionData),
      hasRefundProofDocument: 'refundProofDocument' in actionData,
      documentLength: actionData.refundProofDocument ? actionData.refundProofDocument.length : 0
    });
    
    // Call the exact function that gets called from doPost
    console.log('🔄 Calling handleRefundInitiation with parsed data...');
    const result = handleRefundInitiation({
      appointmentId: appointmentId,
      refundNotes: actionData.notes || '',
      refundProofDocument: actionData.refundProofDocument,
      refundProofName: actionData.refundProofName,
      refundProofType: actionData.refundProofType
    });
    
    console.log('📋 Result:', result);
    
    if (result && result.getContent) {
      // It's an HTML response, parse it
      const content = result.getContent();
      console.log('📄 Response content (first 500 chars):', content.substring(0, 500));
      
      // Try to parse as JSON
      try {
        const jsonResult = JSON.parse(content);
        console.log('📊 Parsed JSON result:', jsonResult);
        console.log('🔗 Refund proof link:', jsonResult.refundProofLink || 'EMPTY');
      } catch (parseError) {
        console.log('❌ Could not parse response as JSON');
      }
    }
    
    return result;
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('❌ Test failed:', error);
    return { status: 'error', message: error.toString() };
  }
}

/**
 * Test the complete refund initiation process with actual handleRefundInitiation function
 * This version bypasses the "already initiated" check to test the file upload
 */
function testHandleRefundInitiationBypassCheck() {
  console.log('=== TESTING HANDLEREFUNDINITIATION WITH BYPASS ===');
  
  try {
    // Step 1: Create test data
    console.log('Step 1: Creating test refund initiation data...');
    
    const testAppointmentId = 'GIS-2025-004'; // Use existing appointment ID
    const testRefundNotes = 'Test refund notes for debugging - BYPASS TEST';
    
    // Create test PDF content in base64
    const testPdfContent = 'JVBERi0xLjQKJfbk/N8KMSAwIG9iago8PAovVHlwZSAvQ2F0YWxvZwovUGFnZXMgMiAwIFIKPj4KZW5kb2JqCjIgMCBvYmoKPDwKL1R5cGUgL1BhZ2VzCi9LaWRzIFsgMyAwIFIgXQovQ291bnQgMQo+PgplbmRvYmoKMyAwIG9iago8PAovVHlwZSAvUGFnZQovUGFyZW50IDIgMCBSCi9NZWRpYUJveCBbIDAgMCA2MTIgNzkyIF0KPj4KZW5kb2JqCnhyZWYKMCA0CjAwMDAwMDAwMDAgNjU1MzUgZiAKMDAwMDAwMDAwOSAwMDAwMCBuIAowMDAwMDAwMDU4IDAwMDAwIG4gCjAwMDAwMDAxMTUgMDAwMDAgbiAKdHJhaWxlcgo8PAovU2l6ZSA0Ci9Sb290IDEgMCBSCj4+CnN0YXJ0eHJlZgoxODUKJSVFT0Y=';
    
    console.log('✅ Test data created');
    
    // Step 2: Test the file upload part directly
    console.log('Step 2: Testing file upload directly...');
    
    const appointment = getAppointmentData(testAppointmentId);
    console.log('✅ Got appointment:', appointment.name);
    
    // Test base64 decoding
    console.log('🔄 Testing base64 decode...');
    const decodedData = Utilities.base64Decode(testPdfContent);
    console.log('✅ Base64 decode successful, decoded size:', decodedData.length);
    
    // Test blob creation
    console.log('🔄 Testing blob creation...');
    const fileBlob = Utilities.newBlob(
      decodedData,
      'application/pdf',
      'test_bypass_handleRefundInitiation.pdf'
    );
    console.log('✅ File blob created:', {
      name: fileBlob.getName(),
      type: fileBlob.getContentType(),
      size: fileBlob.getBytes().length
    });
    
    // Test uploadRefundProof function
    console.log('🔄 Testing uploadRefundProof function...');
    const clientName = appointment.name || 'TestClient';
    const uploadedFile = uploadRefundProof(testAppointmentId, fileBlob, clientName);
    
    console.log('✅ File upload test successful:', {
      fileId: uploadedFile.id,
      fileName: uploadedFile.name,
      fileUrl: uploadedFile.url,
      fileSize: uploadedFile.size
    });
    
    console.log('🎉 === FILE UPLOAD TEST SUCCESSFUL ===');
    console.log('📌 The uploadRefundProof function works correctly in handleRefundInitiation context!');
    
    return {
      status: 'success',
      message: 'File upload test completed successfully',
      uploadResult: uploadedFile
    };
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('❌ === FILE UPLOAD TEST FAILED ===');
    console.error('Error details:', error);
    console.error('Error message:', error.toString());
    console.error('Error stack:', error.stack);
    
    return {
      status: 'error',
      message: 'File upload test failed: ' + error.toString(),
      error: error
    };
  }
}

function testCurrentAppointmentStatuses() {
  console.log("=== CHECKING APPOINTMENT STATUSES ===");
  
  const testAppointments = ['GIS-2025-001', 'GIS-2025-003', 'GIS-2025-004', 'GIS-2025-005'];
  
  testAppointments.forEach(appointmentId => {
    console.log(`\n📋 Checking appointment: ${appointmentId}`);
    try {
      const appointmentData = getAppointmentData(appointmentId);
      if (appointmentData) {
        console.log(`   Status: ${appointmentData.appointmentStatus || 'No status'}`);
        console.log(`   Client: ${appointmentData.clientName || 'No name'}`);
        console.log(`   Email: ${appointmentData.clientEmail || 'No email'}`);
        console.log(`   Date: ${appointmentData.selectedDate || 'No date'}`);
        console.log(`   ✅ Available for refund testing: ${appointmentData.appointmentStatus !== 'Refund Initiated'}`);
      } else {
        console.log(`   ❌ Appointment not found`);
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.log(`   ❌ Error: ${error.message}`);
    }
  });
  
  console.log("\n=== SUMMARY ===");
  console.log("To test refund functionality:");
  console.log("1. Use an appointment with status 'Pending' or 'Confirmed'");
  console.log("2. Make sure you're checking the correct Google Drive folder: 1Yn-tCdNzqDfVh-sK2oq2EJafHKoRcgpM");
  console.log("3. Files are named: REFUND_{appointmentId}_{clientName}_{timestamp}.pdf");
  
  return "Status check complete";
}
